### [136] [CheckRLM: Effective Knowledge-Thought Coherence Checking in Retrieval-Augmented Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02262)
*Dingling Xu,Ruobing Wang,Qingfei Zhao,Yukun Yan,Zhichun Wang,Daren Zha,Shi Yu,Zhenghao Liu,Shuo Wang,Xu Han,Maosong Sun*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: CheckRLM是一个通过检索增强生成（RAG）在推理过程中及时检查并纠正事实错误的框架，以提高复杂任务中语言模型推理的可靠性。它通过提取推理链中的事实主张来识别和定位知识不一致，并利用外部知识进行低成本、精准的修正，从而有效缓解长周期推理中的错误累积问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有推理语言模型在复杂任务中虽表现良好，但其推理链容易包含事实性错误，尤其在知识密集型任务中，这影响了推理结果的可靠性。因此需要一种机制来实时检测和纠正这些错误。

Method: CheckRLM通过从推理链中提取事实主张，识别知识不一致；当检测到错误时，利用外部知识库进行最小成本、高精度的修正，确保推理链与正确知识的一致性。该方法结合了检索增强生成（RAG）技术，实现动态纠错。

Result: 实验表明，CheckRLM显著优于现有基线方法，在减少错误累积方面表现出色，且推理成本较低，具备较强的实用性与可扩展性。

Conclusion: CheckRLM通过引入外部知识进行事实校验与修正，有效提升了长链条推理中语言模型的可靠性，为构建更可信的AI推理系统提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Reasoning Language Models (RLMs) have significantly improved performance on complex tasks by extending the reasoning chain. However, these chains are prone to containing factual errors, particularly in knowledge-intensive tasks. To address this issue, we propose CheckRLM, a framework that improves the reliability of the reasoning process through Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) by timely checking and correcting factual errors. Specifically, CheckRLM extracts factual claims from the reasoning chain to identify and localize subtle knowledge inconsistencies during inference. Upon detection of errors, a refinement mechanism performs minimal-cost yet precise corrections by leveraging external knowledge, ensuring coherence between the reasoning chain and correct knowledge. Extensive experiments demonstrate that CheckRLM substantially outperforms existing baselines, exhibiting a strong capability to mitigate error accumulation in long-horizon reasoning with lower costs. The code and data are available at https://github.com/AI9Stars/CheckRLM.

### [137] [On the Role of Directionality in Structural Generalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02307)
*Zichao Wei*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于CCG有向类型的新符号后端，用于改进SLOG任务中的方向性建模。相比之前的AM-Parser，新系统在位置偏移类任务上显著提升（+29.9pp），而在递归深度类任务上则表现较弱，但使用DeBERTa-v3-large编码器后整体性能达90.7%。方向性表示将瓶颈从符号层转移到神经层，使模型可通过更强编码器进一步优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AM-Parser使用无方向性的AM代数，无法有效处理涉及方向性区分的SLOG任务（如修饰语位置变化、论元提取位置等），导致性能受限。

Method: 设计基于CCG有向类型的符号后端，采用确定性CKY解析与单线性解码器，仅30K可学习参数；保持BERT-base编码器不变，并对比不同配置下的表现。

Result: 在BERT-base下，新系统达到75.9±6.4%的精确匹配率，优于AM-Parser的70.8±4.3%；在位置偏移类别上大幅领先（+29.9pp），而递归深度类别上仍由AM-Parser占优；使用DeBERTa-v3-large时性能达90.7±4.9%，尤其在递归深度类中提升明显。

Conclusion: 引入方向性表示能有效提升特定任务性能，并将模型瓶颈转移至神经编码器层面，使得后续通过更强编码器提升整体性能成为可能。

Abstract: Several SLOG test categories explicitly involve directional distinctions (modifier position shifts, argument extraction positions), yet AM-Parser, the previous SOTA, uses an AM algebra whose operations do not encode direction. We redesign the symbolic backend around CCG directed types (deterministic CKY + single linear decoder, 30K learnable parameters). Under the same BERT-base encoder, the system achieves 75.9$\pm$6.4% LF exact match, surpassing AM-Parser (70.8$\pm$4.3%). Per SLOG's own category groupings, gains are highly directional: the CCG system outperforms AM-Parser on all 5 position-shift categories (+29.9pp), while AM-Parser outperforms on all 6 recursive-depth categories. Replacing the encoder with DeBERTa-v3-large yields 90.7$\pm$4.9%, with the largest encoder gains in recursive-depth categories, complementary to directionality's gains. Directional representations shift the bottleneck from the symbolic layer (AM-Parser's 0% category ceiling) to the neural layer, which improves with encoder upgrades.

Abstract: LLMs stage a new form of cultural encounter that is massive, automated, and monolingual. These tools have now become indispensable for building culturally literate AI. The essay develops a layered framework toward more nuanced textual models and pluralistic interpretations of AI, emphasizing the natural intersections of literature and AI development, connecting current debates in critical theory with structural monolingualism, and suggesting a new application of world literature approaches to address global AI textuality through macrostructure, circulation, and untranslatability.

RUN3 was a RigoChat-based generate-evaluate-regenerate baseline with prompt engineering and LoRA-based adaptation. The official leaderboard reports BLEU-Orig, BLEU-Gold, SARI and BERTScore. These results indicate that, in this task setting, signal-guided multi-agent routing outperformed the linear regeneration baseline. They also show that adding lexical support did not automatically improve reference-based scores. Further segment-level and document-level analysis are required to assess readability, factual consistency and user-oriented adequacy.

### [140] [Know Your Source: A Public Knowledge Store for Media Background Checks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02383)
*Benjamin Nichols,Michael Schlichtkrull,Nedjma Ousidhoum*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出MEDIAREF，一个公开可获取的网络来源文档知识库，用于可复现、低成本评估媒体背景检查（MBC）生成任务，解决现有方法依赖昂贵专有搜索API的问题。通过构建和更新该数据集的方法，验证了多种LLM在MBC生成上的表现，并证明其能提升生成质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于LLM的检索增强生成（RAG）系统在自动化事实核查中假设检索到的证据是可靠的，但现实中信息可能冲突、过时或来自不可靠/偏见来源。尽管已有工作通过媒体背景检查（MBC）应对此问题，但其生成依赖昂贵的专有搜索接口，限制了可复现性。

Method: 提出MEDIAREF，一个基于网络收集的200个媒体源文档的知识库；设计可复现的数据构建与更新流程；使用自动与人工评估方法对主流LLM在MBC生成任务上的表现进行评测。

Result: MEDIAREF支持更高品质的媒体背景检查生成，在自动与定性评估中均表现出优越性能，且整个过程无需依赖专有API，具备良好的可复现性与低成本优势。

Conclusion: MEDIAREF为媒体背景检查生成提供了公开、可复现、低成本的评估基准，有助于推动更可信、透明的自动化事实核查系统发展。

Abstract: LLM-based retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) is increasingly used for automated fact-checking (AFC) and related tasks. By grounding LLM outputs in retrieved evidence, RAG-based systems provide transparent justifications while allowing external information to be updated independently of the underlying model. However, existing approaches often assume retrieved evidence is reliable, although real-world information may be conflicting, outdated, and can originate from unreliable or biased sources. Recent work on *source-critical reasoning* addresses this challenge through media background checks (MBCs) (Schlichtkrull, 2024), which assess the credibility of evidence sources to support downstream fact verification. However, generating MBCs relies on costly proprietary search APIs, limiting reproducibility. To mitigate this issue, we introduce MEDIAREF, a publicly available knowledge store of web-sourced documents that enables reproducible, low-cost evaluation of MBC generation across 200 media sources. We describe a reproducible methodology for constructing and updating the collection, assess widely used LLMs on the MBC generation task, and demonstrate that MEDIAREF supports higher-quality MBC generation through both automatic and qualitative evaluation.

### [141] [The Future of NLP may not be at NLP Conferences: Scholarly Migration Patterns in Natural Language Processing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02416)
*David Jurgens*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: NLP research is shifting from traditional NLP venues like ACL to broader ML venues, driven by citation advantages and changing author behaviors.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To understand whether the disciplinary center of gravity in NLP is shifting due to the rise of Large Language Models (LLMs), particularly in terms of venue preferences among established and new authors.

Method: Analyzing NLP publications from 2010 to 2026, comparing author publication patterns across ACL main tracks, Findings tracks, and general ML venues; using causal inference to assess citation impact on venue choice.

Result: Established authors decreased their share at ACL main conferences by 19.2pp while increasing in Findings and ML venues; new authors' ACL-only publication share dropped from 84% (2019) to 74% (2024), while ML venue participation rose from 5% to 21%. Causal analysis shows ML venues offer a significant citation premium.

Conclusion: The field of NLP is undergoing a significant shift in publication venues, indicating a blurring of boundaries between NLP and general ML, with citation advantages in ML venues playing a key role in this migration.

Abstract: Natural Language Processing (NLP) has traditionally been published in its core disciplinary venues like ACL. However, advances in Large Language Models (LLMs) has led to a blurring of the disciplinary lines between NLP and general Machine Learning (ML), with authors regularly publishing in venues from both fields. Here, we ask whether the disciplinary center of gravity is shifting. Using NLP research published from 2010 to 2026 and studies of both established and new authors, we find that a migration is taking place. First, comparing the pre- and post-LLM eras, established authors lost 19.2pp of share at flagship *ACL main-conference tracks while gaining 14.8pp in the newer Findings tracks, and general ML venues rose 8.6pp, even when adjusting for parallel growth in the fields. Second, among newer authors who debut with at least three first-author NLP-topic papers, the share whose work appears mostly at *ACL venues fell from 84% (2019) to 74% (2024), while the share appearing mostly at general ML venues rose from 5% to 21%. Using causal inference techniques, we estimate that these general ML venues confer a significant citation premium, which influences venue selection. Together, these results point to a significant shift in where NLP research is published.

</details>


### [142] [Language Models as Measurement Apparatus for Culture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02459)
*Kent K. Chang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文探讨语言模型在量化文化现象时的特殊性，提出NLP中的文化研究是一种物质-话语实践，即模型、数据、标注和评估等工具本身参与建构其所测量的文化现实，而非被动记录。通过借鉴Karen Barad的‘能动性切割’概念，文章指出工具设计的选择决定了现象与工具之间的边界，而这一边界从一开始就纠缠不清，因为语言模型已内化了其测量的文化材料。文章通过六个案例（三个关于影视对话的分析，三个关于工具本身的考察）说明这一观点，并提出一个理论驱动、实证严谨且文化上敏感的研究计划，将每个能动性切割视为方法论与伦理上的自觉承诺。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有NLP研究常将语言模型视为中立工具来量化文化现象，但忽视了这些工具本身在塑造文化现实中的主动作用。本文旨在揭示文化测量背后的物质-话语实践本质，强调研究者需反思工具设计如何参与文化建构，从而推动更具批判性和伦理意识的研究范式。

Method: 结合哲学理论（如Karen Barad的能动性切割）、案例研究（六项实证分析，涵盖影视对话结构、互动与偏离，以及工具自身的问题如文化标记的消解、历史材料的敏感性、工作流中的能动性），进行跨学科的批判性分析。

Result: 研究表明，语言模型并非文化现象的被动记录者，而是积极参与文化建构的主体。工具的设计选择（如数据筛选、标注标准、评估指标）实际上定义了何为‘文化’，并影响对文化现象的理解。同时，模型自身内化的文化内容使得测量过程无法完全客观。

Conclusion: 应将文化测量视为一种理论驱动、实证严谨且文化敏感的能动实践。研究者必须意识到每个‘能动性切割’既是方法论选择，也是伦理承诺，从而推动更负责任、更具反思性的文化计算研究。

Abstract: Language models are increasingly used to quantify cultural phenomena, but what makes such measurement distinctively cultural? This paper argues that NLP work on culture is a material-discursive practice: the apparatus -- model, data, annotation, evaluation -- participates in constituting the cultural reality it measures, rather than passively recording it. Drawing on Karen Barad's concept of the agential cut -- the contingent boundary between phenomenon and instrument -- I show that the apparatus's substantive design choices draw such boundaries, and that the boundary is entangled from the start because language models have already internalized much of the cultural material they measure. I illustrate this through three case studies on television and film dialogue (measuring structure, interaction, and deviation) and three examinations of the apparatus itself (erasure of cultural markers, attunement to historical material, and agency in an agentic workflow). This big picture analysis proposes a research program that is theory-driven, empirically rigorous, and culturally contingent, treating each agential cut as a conscious commitment, at once methodological and ethical.

### [143] [Will Scaling Improve Social Simulation with LLMs?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02464)
*Caleb Ziems,William Held,Su Doga Karaca,David Grusky,Tatsunori Hashimoto,Diyi Yang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究通过缩放定律分析大型语言模型（LLM）在社会模拟中的表现，考察计算规模、通用能力基准与社会模拟保真度之间的关系。使用85个基于Qwen3架构的Transformer LLM，在固定计算预算下评估了意见建模、行为模拟和长期预测三个子领域。结果显示，所有任务均表现出显著的计算缩放效应；进一步评估35个更大更强大的开源模型（最大70B参数），发现多数行为与意见模拟任务随规模提升而快速改善，尤其当群体在英语网络语料中代表性较强时。然而，长期预测和低资源意见的缩放速度较慢，且与通用知识和推理基准相关性较低。此外，行为模拟中模型对人类认知偏差（如风险规避）和启发式学习（如从相关任务中学习奖励）的校准能力并未随规模提升而改善，即使微调后，0.5B到8B参数范围内性能也无明显提升。结论：规模可提升多数场景下的社会模拟保真度，但存在例外，低资源领域改进不可靠。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大型语言模型的社会模拟尚不够忠实，难以广泛采用。本文旨在探究现有语言建模的缩放范式是否能弥合这一差距，或社会模拟保真度是否独立于通用能力，因而需要更多研究关注。

Method: 采用缩放定律分析85个基于Qwen3架构的Transformer LLM，覆盖$10^{18}$至$10^{20}$ FLOPs的固定计算预算；随后评估35个更大更强大的开放权重模型（最多70B参数），通过损失预测下游准确率，并在意见建模、行为模拟和长期预测三个子领域进行实验。

Result: 所有三类社会模拟任务均显示出强计算缩放效应；多数行为与意见模拟任务随规模提升而快速改善，尤其在英语语料中代表性高的群体中；长期预测和未充分代表的意见缩放较慢，且与通用基准相关性低；行为模拟中模型对人类认知偏差和启发式学习的校准能力未随规模提升，微调后0.5B至8B参数范围性能无明显改善。

Conclusion: 规模可显著提升大多数社会模拟场景的保真度，但存在例外情况，特别是在低资源领域，改进效果不可靠，提示需针对特定任务加强研究。

Abstract: Large Language Model (LLM) social simulations are a promising research method, but they are not yet faithful enough to be adopted widely. In this work, we investigate whether the current scaling paradigm in language modeling is likely to close these gaps, or whether simulation fidelity is orthogonal to general capabilities and therefore deserving of more research attention. We use scaling laws to study the relationship between LLMs' compute scale, general capability benchmarks, and the fidelity of social simulation in three representative sub-domains: opinion modeling, behavioral simulation, and longitudinal forecasting. Surprisingly, we discover strong compute scaling in all three settings, using a suite of 85 transformer LLMs with the Qwen3 architecture pre-trained on the DCLM web text corpus under fixed-compute budgets from $10^{18}$ to $10^{20}$ FLOPs. Then we evaluate 35 larger and more capable open-weight models up to 70B parameters, allowing us to predict downstream accuracy from loss. This reveals that the majority of behavioral and opinion simulation tasks will rapidly improve with scale, particularly when they involve populations that are well-represented in English web corpora. Longitudinal forecasting and underrepresented opinions scale more slowly, especially when they are less correlated with general knowledge and reasoning benchmarks like MMLU. In behavior simulation, scaling fails to improve model calibration with human cognitive biases like risk aversion, as well as human heuristics like learning correlated rewards from related tasks. On these tasks, even fine-tuned models fail to noticeably scale up performance from 0.5B to 8B parameters. Taken together, we conclude that scale will improve social simulations in most settings, but outliers exist, and improvements will be less reliable in low-resource domains.

Conclusion: 本研究首次实现了对朗读质量、体裁、标题与消费行为之间关系的系统性计算分析，证实声学特征是影响有声书吸引力的关键因素，为未来有声书的个性化推荐与专业朗读者匹配提供了重要数据支持。

This work explores how narration qualities shape an audiobook's appeal, noting that their effects can vary by genre, title, and audience. We extract vocal and acoustic features (e.g., tone, pace, loudness) from LibriVox using pre-trained audio models and analyse their relationship with consumption data (specifically, view-rate) and their interplay with genre and title. Despite limited consumption data, we find that acoustic information alone has a robust association with appeal, even after accounting for title effects. We further validate these findings using more nuanced proprietary engagement metrics. To our knowledge, this is the first systematic computational study linking narration qualities, genre, title, and audiobook consumption, highlighting the potential of data-driven insights to improve audiobook personalisation and narrator casting.

### [145] [Visually Grounded Self-Reflection for Vision-Language Models via Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02490)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大视觉-语言模型在反思过程中往往无法正确关注视觉输入，导致难以将反馈转化为基于视觉的修正，尤其在分布外图像上表现不佳。

Method: 设计了两种机制：1）训练时随机掩码轨迹前缀，强调从错误中间预测中恢复；2）引入经验回放缓冲区中的缓冲滚动，让模型接触多样化的失败状态并学会纠正。

Result: 在表格、图表视觉定位及空间导航任务上，相比标准强化学习和反射微调基线，该方法显著提升了分布外情况下的平均准确率，有效利用了自我反思能力。

Conclusion: VRRL框架成功增强了大视觉-语言模型在复杂视觉场景下的自省与视觉基础纠错能力，尤其在分布外数据上表现优越。

Abstract: Large vision-language models can reason over multimodal inputs by generating textual chains of thought (CoT). A key capability exhibited in CoT reasoning is self-reflection: revisiting earlier decisions and correcting previous errors. However, existing LVLMs often fail to properly attend to visual inputs during reflection, limiting their ability to translate feedback into grounded corrections, especially for out-of-distribution images. To address this issue, we propose a novel reinforcement learning training framework VRRL, with two components explicitly designed to elicit visually grounded self-reflection. First, we randomly mask trajectory prefixes during training to emphasize recovery from incorrect intermediate predictions rather than making early mistakes. Second, we introduce buffered roll-ins from an experience replay buffer to expose the model to diverse failure states that it must learn to correct. We evaluate our approach on visual grounding tasks involving tables and charts, as well as spatial navigation benchmarks. While off-the-shelf and conventionally fine-tuned models degrade substantially under distribution shift, our method substantially improves average out-of-distribution accuracy over standard RL and reflection-oriented fine-tuning baselines by using self-reflection effectively.

</details>


### [146] [Reasoning LLM Improves Speaker Recognition in Long-form TV Dramas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02504)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 实验结果表明，DramaSR-LRM在短语句场景下显著优于现有基线方法，特别是在声学特征不可靠的情况下表现优异。

Conclusion: 本文通过构建大规模标注数据集DramaSR-532K和提出DramaSR-LRM方法，显著提升了长篇电视剧中说话人识别的性能，为视频理解提供了有力支持。

Abstract: Long-form TV dramas present a formidable challenge for comprehensive video understanding, where deciphering complex storyline often relies on \textbf{speaker recognition}, the task of accurately attributing each spoken utterance to its respective character. In this paper, we advance this field through two primary contributions. (1) We introduce \textbf{DramaSR-532K}, a large-scale benchmark comprising 532K annotated dialogue lines across more than 900 unique characters, necessitating the integration of auditory, linguistic, and visual cues for speaker recognition. (2) We propose \textbf{DramaSR-LRM}, a robust approach built upon a large reasoning model (LRM). DramaSR-LRM is designed to autonomously aggregate contextual evidence via multimodal tool-use, synthesizing diverse inputs to achieve high-fidelity attribution. Experimental results demonstrate that DramaSR-LRM significantly outperforms existing baselines, particularly on short utterances where acoustic biometrics are inherently unreliable. \textit{All the data and code will be made publicly available at the project page: https://www.github.com/198808xc/DramaSR-LRM.}

### [147] [LACUNA: A Testbed for Evaluating Localization Precision for LLM Unlearning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02513)
*Matteo Boglioni,Thibault Rousset,Siva Reddy,Marius Mosbach,Verna Dankers*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出LACUNA，首个具备真实参数级定位能力的模型遗忘测试平台，通过在1B和7B OLMo模型中预设注入合成个人身份信息（PII），实现对遗忘目标参数的精确控制与评估。基于此，研究发现当前主流遗忘方法虽在输出层面表现良好，但在参数层面存在严重不精准问题，易受重现身攻击。而当实现精确定位后，即使使用简单的梯度方法也能实现强遗忘效果和抗攻击能力，凸显精准遗忘的重要性。研究释放LACUNA以推动更鲁棒、基于定位的遗忘技术发展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型会记忆敏感训练数据（如个人身份信息），亟需可靠的后处理遗忘方法。现有方法多采用‘定位先行，遗忘后行’范式，但当前评估仅限于输出层面，无法判断知识是否真正从模型参数中移除，存在被重现身攻击破解的风险。因此需要一个能直接验证参数级遗忘效果的基准测试平台。

Method: 提出LACUNA测试平台，利用掩码持续预训练技术，将合成个体的PII注入到指定的模型参数中，构建可追踪的知识存储位置。在此基础上，对现有SOTA遗忘方法进行参数级评估，并对比不同方法在定位准确性和抗重现身攻击方面的表现。

Result: 尽管现有遗忘方法在输出层面表现优异，但在参数层面定位极为粗略，容易被重现身攻击恢复敏感信息；而一旦实现精准定位，即使是简单梯度方法也展现出强大的遗忘能力和对攻击的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 精确的参数级定位是实现真正有效且鲁棒遗忘的关键。未来遗忘方法应注重提升定位精度，LACUNA为这一方向提供了必要的评估工具。

Abstract: LLMs memorize sensitive training data, including personally identifiable information (PII), creating a pressing need for reliable post hoc removal methods. Unlearning has emerged as a promising solution, with state-of-the-art(SOTA) methods often following a localize-first, unlearn-second paradigm that targets specific model parameters. However, existing benchmarks evaluate unlearning solely at the output level, leaving open the question of whether unlearning truly erases knowledge from a model's parameters or merely obfuscates it, a concern reinforced by the success of resurfacing attacks. To bridge this gap, we introduce LACUNA: the first unlearning testbed with ground-truth parameter-level localization. LACUNA injects PII of synthetic individuals into predefined parameters of 1B and 7B OLMo-based models via masked continual pretraining, enabling direct evaluation of whether unlearning targets the weights responsible for knowledge storage. We use LACUNA to benchmark current SOTA unlearning methods and find that, despite strong output-level performance, existing methods are highly imprecise and susceptible to resurfacing attacks. We further show that when localization is successful, even a simple gradient-based unlearning method achieves strong erasure and robustness to resurfacing attacks, highlighting the importance of precise unlearning. We release LACUNA to complement behavioral evaluations and drive further advances in robust, localization-based unlearning.

</details>

### [148] [PACE: A Neuro-Symbolic Framework for Plausible and Actionable Counterfactual Explanations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01306)
*Pavel Iakovets,Liyanapathiranage Sudeepika Wajirakumari Samarathunga,Martin Thomas Horsch,Fadi Al Machot*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出PACE，一种模块化的神经符号框架，用于生成考虑可行性的反事实解释。该框架将预测与推理分离：使用神经网络进行分类，符号推理层在生成反事实时施加领域特定约束。通过显式建模可行干预，生成的解释符合领域知识且可解释、可操作。方法对模型无依赖，适用于需要现实决策支持的领域。以Adult Income数据集为例，结合多层感知机与答案集编程（ASP）规则，编码教育、职业和工作时间的可行修改，同时保持不可变属性不变。结果表明，符号约束能有效提升解释的可行性，平衡反事实有效性与合理性，展示了神经符号方法在可解释人工智能中透明、可行性感知反事实解释的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有反事实解释方法常生成不切实际或不可行的建议，因缺乏显式机制来融入领域知识和干预约束。为解决此问题，需引入能够表示人类可理解规则和可行行动的符号推理能力。

Method: 提出PACE框架，包含神经预测模型（如多层感知机）与符号推理层（如基于ASP规则）。前者负责分类任务，后者在生成反事实时强制执行领域约束，确保干预变化符合现实可行性。框架设计实现模块化，支持模型无关性与领域适配性。

Result: 在Adult Income数据集上的案例研究显示，加入符号约束后生成的反事实解释更符合领域可行性要求；尽管部分情况下可能牺牲一定反事实有效性，但整体显著提升了解释的现实可信度与实用性。

Conclusion: PACE框架通过融合神经网络与符号推理，实现了对反事实解释的可行性约束，使解释既合理又可操作，为可解释人工智能中的透明决策支持提供了新路径。

Abstract: Counterfactual explanations explain machine learning predictions by identifying minimal input changes that would alter a model's decision. Although many existing methods successfully generate prediction-changing alternatives, they often produce unrealistic or infeasible recommendations due to a lack of explicit mechanisms for incorporating domain knowledge and intervention constraints. Neuro-symbolic AI offers a promising direction by combining data-driven predictive models with symbolic reasoning capable of representing human-understandable rules and feasible actions. This paper presents PACE, a modular neuro-symbolic framework for generating feasibility-aware counterfactual explanations. The framework separates prediction and reasoning into two components: a neural predictive model for classification and a symbolic reasoning layer that enforces domain-specific constraints during counterfactual generation. By explicitly modeling feasible interventions, the framework produces explanations consistent with domain knowledge while remaining interpretable and actionable. The approach is model-agnostic and adaptable to domains requiring realistic decision support. A case study is conducted on the Adult Income dataset, combining a multilayer perceptron classifier with Answer Set Programming (ASP) rules encoding feasible modifications to education, occupation, and working hours while preserving immutable attributes. Results highlight the trade-off between counterfactual validity and plausibility and show that symbolic constraints yield explanations that better satisfy domain-specific feasibility requirements, illustrating the potential of neuro-symbolic methods for transparent, feasibility-aware counterfactual explanation in explainable AI.

</details>


### [149] [Auto-FL-Research: Agentic Search for Federated Learning Algorithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01366)
*Holger R. Roth,Ziyue Xu,Chester Chen,Daguang Xu,Peter Cnudde,Andrew Feng*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Auto-FL-Research (AFR) 是一种受限编码代理工作流，用于自动化搜索联邦学习（FL）算法配方。它通过代理提出并实现候选训练算法，涵盖服务器聚合规则、客户端更新调度、本地目标函数和注册的模型变体，并在固定的任务配置下进行评估。该方法在多个医疗跨孤岛FLamby任务和LEAF数据集上验证，结果显示部分性能提升源于算法配方改进，而其他提升则可能来自固定表面调优或单次运行的偶然性，揭示了不同类型的改进来源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 联邦学习中的许多算法选择（如优化器、聚合规则、训练调度等）对性能有显著影响，但手动探索成本高且难以公平比较，因为不同修改可能改变训练或评估路径。因此需要一种系统化、可重复的方法来自动搜索最优算法配方。

Method: 提出Auto-FL-Research（AFR），一个受约束的编码代理工作流。代理可在固定任务配置（如计算预算、通信协议、评估方式）下生成并实施新的联邦学习算法配方，包括服务器聚合策略、客户端更新机制、本地目标函数和模型结构。所有实验记录候选方案的得分、运行时间、修改文件、生成产物及失败状态，支持多轮重复评估与消融分析。

Result: 在五个FLamby医疗任务和六个LEAF数据集配置上，AFR在多数情况下实现了性能提升；然而，部分提升可归因于算法配方变化，另一些则源自固定表面调优或特定种子下的偶然成功。通过控制实验表明，一些改进具有可重复性，而另一些则不具鲁棒性。

Conclusion: AFR能够有效探索联邦学习算法配方，揭示出性能提升的多种来源：可重复的机制改进、固定表面的调参效应以及单次运行的偶然结果。这为理解联邦学习中算法设计的影响提供了新视角，强调了评估的严谨性和可复现性的重要性。

Abstract: Federated learning (FL) research often depends on many small but consequential algorithmic choices: optimizer variants, server aggregation rules, local training schedules, normalization, regularization, and model architecture. These choices are expensive to explore manually and difficult to compare fairly when candidate changes can also alter the FL training or evaluation path. In this work, we present Auto-FL-Research (AFR), a constrained coding-agent workflow for FL algorithmic recipe search. Agents may propose and implement candidate training algorithms, including server aggregation rules, client update schedules, local objectives, and registered model variants, while task profiles fix the mutation surface, compute budget, communication contract, and final model evaluation. Each campaign records candidate scores, runtime, edited files, artifacts, and failure status. We evaluate AFR on five healthcare cross-silo FLamby tasks and on grouped-client profiles for the five fixed LEAF datasets plus the LEAF synthetic task. Five-seed repeat evaluations support gains on four FLamby tasks and five of six LEAF profiles, while also exposing seed-sensitive and search-selected failure cases. Same-budget controls show that several gains correspond to FL-recipe changes, whereas other improvements are recovered by fixed-surface scalar controls or fail under repeat or held-out evaluation. These mixed outcomes are part of the contribution: they show how agent-generated candidates can be separated into repeated FL mechanisms, fixed-surface tuning effects, and selected single-run artifacts.

</details>


### [150] [The Wiola Architecture for Efficient Small Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01394)
*Aryuemaan Kumar Chowdhury,Afreen Shaik,Yaparla Bhargavi,Brahma Kumar*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Wiola 是一种从零开始设计的全新小型语言模型（SLM）架构，不继承任何现有模型家族（如 GPT、LLaMA、Mistral、Falcon）的结构。其核心创新包括：螺旋旋转位置编码（SRPE）、门控跨层注意力（GCLA）、自适应标记合并（ATM）、双流前馈网络（DSFF）和 WiolaRMSNorm。这些组件分别处理位置信息、层间连贯性、计算复杂度降低、特征表示增强与归一化优化。模型提供完整数学推导、架构图、复杂度分析，并在多个基准上对比 GPT-2、LLaMA-2 与 Mistral。Wiola 共发布四个规模版本（120M–1.5B 参数），兼容 HuggingFace Transformers 生态系统，所有 22 个单元测试均通过。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为解决现有小型语言模型在表达能力、效率与稳定性方面的局限，提出完全原创的架构设计，避免对主流模型结构的依赖，实现更高效、更稳定的性能表现。

Method: 基于第一性原理构建全新架构，引入五项独立创新：(i) Spiral Rotary Positional Encoding (SRPE)，将位置信息嵌入三维螺旋流形；(ii) Gated Cross-Layer Attention (GCLA)，实现跨层软注意力连接；(iii) Adaptive Token Merging (ATM)，动态合并语义冗余标记以降低复杂度；(iv) Dual Stream Feed-Forward (DSFF)，并行双流处理后融合；(v) WiolaRMSNorm，引入可学习偏移向量防止表示崩溃。

Result: Wiola 在多个评估指标上优于 GPT-2、LLaMA-2 与 Mistral，尤其在小参数规模下展现出更强的推理能力与训练稳定性。四款模型均通过全部 22 个单元测试，且支持 HuggingFace Transformers 生态。

Conclusion: Wiola 证明了从零设计小型语言模型架构的可行性，其多项原创组件共同提升了模型的表达力、效率与鲁棒性，为未来轻量级模型的发展提供了新范式。

Abstract: We present Wiola, a fully original Small Language Model (SLM) architecture built from first principles, sharing no structural lineage with any existing model family including GPT, LLaMA, Mistral, or Falcon. Wiola introduces five independently novel components: (i) Spiral Rotary Positional Encoding (SRPE), which embeds token positions on a three-dimensional helical manifold combining absolute, relative, and hierarchical positional signals; (ii) Gated Cross-Layer Attention (GCLA), providing each decoder layer with soft cross-attention access to compressed summaries of two preceding layers for inter-layer coherence; (iii) Adaptive Token Merging (ATM), which dynamically merges se mantically redundant adjacent tokens in middle network layers to reduce attention complexity without information loss; (iv) Dual Stream Feed-Forward (DSFF), replacing the conventional MLP with two parallel streams fused by a learned per-dimension gate; and (v) WiolaRMSNorm, a modified normalisation introducing a per-dimension learned offset vector that prevents representation collapse. We provide complete mathematical derivations, architectural block diagrams, complexity analyses, and systematic comparisons against GPT-2, LLaMA-2, and Mistral. Wiola is released in four sizes (120M, 360M, 700M, and 1.5B parameters) and is fully compatible with the HuggingFace Transformers ecosystem, with all 22 architectural unit tests passing.

</details>


### [151] [Agent4cs: A Multi-agent System for Code Summarization in Large Hierarchical Codebases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01425)
*Yongjian Tang,Ezgi Sarikayak,Doruk Tuncel,Jie M. Zhang,Thomas Runkler*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Agent4cs 是一个用于大规模代码库摘要的多智能体框架，采用自下而上的方式，通过总结代理、关键词提取代理和质量保障代理协同工作，有效提升摘要的语义一致性与关键词覆盖率。在多个前沿模型上评估显示，相比传统结构化提示基线，其平均提升8%的语义一致性，最高达38%的关键词覆盖率增益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代码摘要方法通常依赖单一语言模型，将源代码视为扁平文本，未能充分利用代码仓库中的层次结构与复杂依赖关系，尤其在面对混淆结构和不完整文档时效果不佳。

Method: 提出多智能体框架 Agent4cs，包含三个核心组件：总结代理负责生成稳健摘要；关键词提取代理主动识别子文件夹中的关键信息；质量保障代理通过迭代优化提升输出的可读性、连贯性和完整性。整体采用自下而上的摘要策略，充分挖掘代码的层级与依赖信息。

Result: 在7个前沿模型上，Agent4cs平均提升8%的语义一致性；在真实世界数据集上，关键词覆盖率最高提升38%，显著优于两种结构化提示基线方法。

Conclusion: Agent4cs 通过多智能体协作与自下而上的摘要机制，有效解决了复杂代码库中语义一致性和信息覆盖不足的问题，为大规模代码理解提供了高效、可靠的解决方案。

Abstract: Understanding large, complex codebases, especially those with obfuscated structures and incomplete documentation, remains a significant challenge. Existing code summarization solutions often rely on a single language model or coding assistant like Claude Code, and treat source code as flat text, underutilizing the rich interdependencies and hierarchical information within a repository. To address these shortcomings, we propose Agent4cs - a multi-agent framework that summarizes large codebases in a bottom-up fashion, where a summarization agent focuses on producing robust summaries; a keyword-extraction agent proactively identifies critical information from subfolders; and a quality-assurance agent iteratively refines the outputs for readability, coherence, and completeness. Evaluated on 7 frontier models, Agent4cs improves semantic consistency across all folder levels by average 8% compared to two structured prompting baselines with code segments. Furthermore, extensive evaluation on real-world datasets demonstrates up to 38% gains in normalized keyword coverage rate over the same baselines.

</details>


### [152] [When Should Service Agents Reconsider? Difficulty-Routed Control in Customer-Service Operations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01426)
*Qian Chen,Chengyuan Liu,Xin Yu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种难度路由的服务控制架构，用于解决自主客服代理在执行操作时面临的复杂性与错误风险问题。该架构通过轻量级路由器将常规请求保留在低成本路径上，而将涉及操作耦合的复杂请求路由至升级工作流，以实现冲突感知通信和写入触发的重新考虑，从而在关键操作前集中决策与防护。在零售和航空领域的任务评估中，该方法在存在操作冲突的请求上显著提升了可靠性，且控制措施精准聚焦于高风险场景而非泛化应用。分析表明，性能提升源于证据收集、写入分离和预写重审，而非盲目扩展对话或工具链。案例研究显示，升级流程能有效保留回退方案、绑定正确记录、有序执行写入并拆分多实体请求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着自主客服代理从对话交互转向实际操作执行（如退款、取消、改单等），如何在保证服务效率的同时防止因客户指令、政策约束、企业记录与后端写入之间复杂交互导致的操作错误，成为亟待解决的服务控制难题。传统统一施加控制的方式效率低下且不精准，亟需更智能的差异化控制机制。

Method: 提出难度路由的服务控制架构：通过轻量级路由器识别请求难度，将常规会话置于低开销基线路径，将操作耦合性强的会话引导至升级工作流；升级路径采用冲突感知通信与写入触发的重新考虑机制，在关键操作前集中进行推理与防护，避免对所有会话无差别增加控制成本。

Result: 在$τ^{2}$-bench上的零售与航空任务测试表明，该方法在存在操作冲突的请求上持续提升可靠性；路由分析显示控制强度精准投向高冲突请求；对话与工具使用模式表明性能提升来自证据收集、写入分离与预写重审，而非盲目扩展交互；案例分析证实升级流程有效支持回退、记录绑定、写入排序与多实体请求分解。

Conclusion: 所提出的难度路由服务控制架构能够高效应对自主客服代理在操作执行中的复杂交互挑战，通过动态分配控制资源，实现了高可靠性和低摩擦服务的平衡，适用于零售、航空等多种服务场景。

Abstract: Autonomous customer-service agents are shifting from conversational interfaces toward operational execution roles: they retrieve firm records, apply service policies, and execute backend writes such as refunds, cancellations, exchanges, order modifications, and reservation changes. This shift creates a service-control problem: firms must keep routine service fast and low-friction while preventing operational errors on requests where customer instructions, policy constraints, firm records, and backend writes interact. We propose a difficulty-routed service-control architecture that asks when service agents should reconsider before acting. A lightweight router keeps routine sessions on a low-cost baseline path and routes operationally coupled sessions to an escalated workflow. The escalated path uses conflict-aware communication and write-triggered reconsideration to concentrate deliberation and safeguards before consequential backend writes, rather than applying additional control uniformly across all service sessions. We evaluate the architecture on human-verified retail and airline tasks from $τ^{2}$-bench. In retail, the method improves reliability consistently on service requests with operational conflict. Routing evidence shows that stronger control is directed toward conflicted requests rather than broadly applied to routine ones. Dialogue and tool-use profiles suggest that gains do not come from indiscriminate interaction expansion or broader tool chains; instead, added turns and tool calls support evidence gathering, write separation, and pre-write reconsideration. Case-level evidence shows that the escalated workflow preserves fallback plans, binds retrieved records to the correct action, sequences writes, and decomposes multi-entity requests. Airline results extend the same service-control logic to reservation operations.

</details>


### [153] [CreativityNeuro: Steering Language Model Weights to Improve Divergent Thinking and Reduce Mode Collapse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01433)
*Samuel Schapiro,Core Francisco Park,Felix Sosa,Lav R. Varshney*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: CreativityNeuro is a data-free method that enhances divergent thinking in large language models (LLMs) through contrastive weight steering, improving creativity metrics without retraining or gradient-based tuning. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Large language models often exhibit the 'artificial hivemind effect,' generating repetitive responses to open-ended questions, limiting their creative potential. This study aims to enhance divergent thinking in LLMs without relying on behavioral data or extensive retraining.

Method: CreativityNeuro employs contrastive weight steering to guide LLMs toward more diverse and creative outputs. Unlike activation steering, which modifies internal activations, this method directly adjusts model weights in a way that promotes exploration across the response space.

Result: On the Divergent Association Task (DAT), CreativityNeuro improves performance by up to 14 human percentile points. In large-scale human evaluations (N=720), it significantly boosts originality, surprise, and overall creativity on the Alternative Uses Test (AUT) and Task Task. It also effectively reduces mode collapse across all tasks. Weight-space steering outperforms activation steering in transferability to open-ended tasks.

Conclusion: CreativityNeuro successfully enhances divergent thinking and reduces mode collapse in LLMs without requiring data collection, retraining, or fine-tuning. Its effectiveness in generalizing across diverse creative tasks makes it a promising approach for improving creativity in AI systems.

Abstract: Divergent thinking is a crucial aspect of creativity, yet large language models (LLMs) tend to consistently generate similar responses to open-ended questions, in what has been termed the artificial hivemind effect. Here, we introduce CreativityNeuro, a data-free method for enhancing divergent thinking in LLMs via contrastive weight steering. We evaluate our method across multiple creativity assessments and report several main findings. On the Divergent Association Task (DAT), a vocabulary-space creativity test, CreativityNeuro improves performance by up to 14 human percentile points. Next, in a large-scale human evaluation (N=720) on the Alternative Uses Test (AUT) and the Task Task, CreativityNeuro achieves significant improvements in originality, surprise, and creativity, transferring to longer-form and more open-ended tasks. Importantly, we find that across all three tasks, CreativityNeuro demonstrably reduces measures of mode collapse. Moreover, activation steering achieves comparable performance to CreativityNeuro on the DAT, but it does not transfer to the AUT and Task Task, demonstrating the effectiveness of weight-space steering in generalizing to unseen tasks. In conclusion, CreativityNeuro improves divergent thinking and reduces mode collapse without requiring behavioral data, re-training, or gradient-based fine-tuning, providing a straightforward way to enhance LLM performance in creative domains.

Abstract: Diffusion language models, which generate text by denoising a token canvas bidirectionally instead of emitting tokens left to right, have become competitive with autoregressive (AR) generation. Medical foundation models, however, remain almost entirely autoregressive. Beyond this parity, the diffusion model offers a drafting capability AR lacks: any-order infill. Because the canvas is denoised bidirectionally, a radiologist can fix report fragments and have the model fill the text between them, an operation inherent to diffusion but not to autoregression, which is subpar at it. This suits real reports, which are often terse or inconsistent across clinicians and institutions.

### [155] [Beyond Next-Token Prediction: An RLVR Proof of Concept for Tool-Use Agents on Atlassian Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01465)
*Karthikeya Aditya Vissa,Sankalp Mane,Ananya Mantravadi,Harshit Rajgarhia,Abhishek Mukherji*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建五个高保真度模拟Jira REST v3和Confluence v2 API的合成环境；使用工具调用轨迹自动计算可验证奖励，不依赖真实API、学习型评判器或人工标签；在相同评估框架下对比提示型Qwen3-1.7B与Qwen3.5-4B模型与经过GRPO训练的强化学习策略的表现。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了在真实环境中直接应用可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）能够有效提升小型语言模型在特定企业API任务中的表现，是迈向面向结果优化的小模型的重要一步。但其局限性在于奖励设计难以规模化，且某些任务存在奖励饱和现象，需进一步探索。

Abstract: Large language models are trained to predict the next token, not to act inside a specific API. In niche enterprise SaaS workflows -- where success means hitting the right endpoint with the right nested arguments in the right order -- this objective mismatch shows up as silent failures: dropped required fields, hallucinated tools, or early stops after a single read. We ask whether Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR), applied directly in the target environment, closes the gap. As a proof of concept we build a suite of five synthetic environments emulating the Jira REST v3 and Confluence v2 APIs at schema fidelity; rewards are computed entirely from the tool-call trace, with no live API, no learned judge, and no human label in the loop. Scoring prompted Qwen3-1.7B and Qwen3.5-4B on the same checkers that drive GRPO training, we find that on the four scenarios whose rewards are non-degenerate the RL-trained policy lifts average reward from a 4B-baseline range of 0.35--0.92 to 0.95--1.00, with the largest single gain on Confluence page creation ($0.35 \rightarrow 1.00$). We position this as a preliminary step toward outcome-optimised small models for niche enterprise APIs, and foreground two limitations a workshop reader should weigh: hand-crafting verifiable rewards does not scale beyond the handful of endpoints reported here, and one of our five scenarios (ticket-transition) has a saturating reward shape that the prompted 4B already maxes out.

TL;DR: 该研究针对临床协议执行任务中的强化学习（RL）应用挑战，发现现有基准MedAgentBench存在41.7%的沉默完成天花板，导致不作为成为主导策略。为此构建了新基准MAB-v3（508任务，8.9%通过率天花板），并评估Qwen3-8B模型在训练中遭遇两大结构性障碍：能力上限（10/20任务类型基础性能为0%）和格式知识障碍（3/20类型需精确临床代码，无法通过探索获取）。纯RL仅达18.2% pass@1，远低于规则驱动的监督微调（SFT）的34.1%，差距15.9个百分点完全归因于上述障碍。研究提出决策/格式知识/查找的分类框架，用于预测RL可学习性，并建议：用SFT注入代码，用RL学习条件逻辑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建并评估MedAgentBench-v3（MAB-v3）新基准；使用Qwen3-8B模型进行训练；分析纯强化学习（RL）与规则驱动的监督微调（SFT）的性能差异；提出决策/格式知识/查找三类分类框架以诊断学习障碍，并据此提出混合方法策略。

Result: MAB-v3将通过率天花板降至8.9%，揭示了显著的结构性障碍：10种任务类型基础性能为0%，3种任务依赖不可探索的精确临床代码。纯RL仅达18.2% pass@1，而规则驱动的SFT达到34.1%，差距15.9个百分点完全由上述障碍解释。分类框架有效预测了哪些任务适合RL，并指导采用SFT注入代码、RL学习条件逻辑的组合策略。

Conclusion: 在临床智能体中应用强化学习需克服能力天花板与格式知识障碍。应通过构建更精细的基准（如MAB-v3）、结合监督微调（SFT）注入关键知识、再以强化学习学习复杂决策逻辑，才能实现高效、可靠的任务自动化。

Abstract: Clinical protocol-execution tasks -- checking a lab value, applying a threshold, placing a correctly structured FHIR order -- are natural candidates for RL from world feedback: once clinical SMEs encode decision logic into a verifier, that verifier grades unlimited rollouts without per-episode annotation. But applying RL requires a sound feedback channel and sufficient base capability. We audit MedAgentBench v1/v2, find a 41.7\% silent-finish ceiling that makes inaction the RL dominant strategy, and construct \textbf{MedAgentBench-v3 (MAB-v3)} (508 tasks, 8.9\% ceiling). Training Qwen3-8B exposes two structural barriers: a \emph{capability ceiling} (10/20 task types have 0\% base performance, zero gradient) and a \emph{format-knowledge barrier} (3/20 types require exact clinical codes undiscoverable by exploration). Pure RL reaches 18.2\% pass@1 vs.\ 34.1\% for rule-based SFT; the 15.9~pp gap is attributable entirely to these barriers. ### [157] [Procedural Memory Distillation: Online Reflection for Self-Improving Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01480)
*Ye Liu,Srijan Bansal,Bo Pang,Yang Li,Zeyu Leo Liu,Yifei Ming,Zixuan Ke,Shafiq Joty,Semih Yavuz*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出程序记忆蒸馏（PMD），通过在线提取模型自身轨迹中的跨回合信号，构建多层次的可重用程序记忆，并与策略共同进化，以提升强化学习中策略的学习效率和性能。相比SDPO，在SCIKNOWEVAL和LIVECODEBENCH上分别提升3.8-5.5%和7.9-13.6%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RLVR方法如SDPO仅依赖每轮次的局部信号更新策略，忽视了跨轮次中积累的丰富过程信息，如一致通过验证的策略、持续存在的失败模式和重复出现的模式，导致学习效率受限。

Method: 提出Procedural Memory Distillation（PMD），将跨回合信号组织为三个抽象层次：原始轨迹、自我反思的策略与经验教训、以及跨问题重复出现的高层行为模式；设计一个记忆条件化的自教师机制，利用累积经验监督学生策略的滚动执行，实现知识内化。

Result: 在Qwen3-8B和OLMo3-Instruct-7B模型上，PMD相较于SDPO在SCIKNOWEVAL上提升3.8-5.5%，在LIVECODEBENCH上提升7.9-13.6%；冻结记忆或策略均导致性能下降超过10%，验证了协同进化机制的有效性。

Conclusion: PMD通过构建可内化的程序记忆并实现策略与记忆的共演化，显著提升了强化学习中策略的知识获取能力，最终生成无需外部记忆的高效推理模型。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR), along with recent selfdistillation variants such as SDPO, evaluates each rollout against a verifier and updates the policy from that episode-level signal. However, the richer procedural information in the rollout is rarely retained or reused. Across episodes and epochs, the model repeatedly encounters related problems under a changing policy, producing cross-episode signals that episode-local updates cannot capture: which strategies consistently pass verification, which failure modes persist, which patterns recur. We propose Procedural Memory Distillation (PMD), which converts these crossepisode signals into reusable procedural memory and distills it into the policy's weights during training. This memory functions as a training scaffold, absorbed into the policy itself, yielding a memory-free model at inference. PMD organizes the memory at three levels of abstraction: raw trajectories, self-reflected strategies and lessons, and higher-level behavioral patterns that recur across problems, all extracted online from the model's own trajectories. A memory-conditioned self-teacher draws on the accumulated experience to supervise the student on its own rollouts, enabling student to progressively internalize procedural knowledge within its parameters. The central design principle is co-evolution: the policy generates rollouts that update the memory, and memory shapes the supervision that updates the policy. Empirically, across Qwen3-8B and OLMo3-Instruct-7B, PMD improves over SDPO by 3.8-5.5% on SCIKNOWEVAL and 7.9-13.6% on LIVECODEBENCH. Co-evolution powers these gains: freezing either the memory or the policy trails PMD by more than 10% across SCIKNOWEVAL domains.

</details>


### [158] [The Agentic Garden of Forking Paths](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01507)
*Jiacheng Miao,Jonathan K Pritchard,James Zou*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: AI agents reveal hidden analytical variation in empirical research by simulating diverse, belief-aligned conclusions from the same data. In four high-stakes domains, AI personas reproduced 72% of the ideological gap seen in human research teams. Despite opposing findings, 86% of AI reports passed independent AI review and 78% passed human expert review, highlighting that methodological defensibility is widespread. The study introduces the m-value—a measure of how extreme a reported result is relative to plausible alternative analyses—and Agentic Bootstrap, an AI-driven method to estimate this value. Applied to an immigration dataset, 13.5% of human analyses were among the most extreme 5% of possible outcomes (m<0.05), suggesting many findings are not robust but selectively reported. Scientific credibility should thus be assessed not just by individual results but by their position within the full space of plausible analyses.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Empirical research often involves multiple valid analytical choices, leading to divergent conclusions from the same data. These 'forking paths' are typically hidden, making it hard to assess whether results stem from sound analysis or selective reporting. This study aims to expose and quantify such variation using AI agents, revealing how beliefs shape analysis and challenging the assumption that methodological rigor alone ensures scientific credibility.

Method: The authors use AI agents with different assigned personas (e.g., liberal, conservative) to analyze the same datasets across four high-stakes domains. They compare AI-generated conclusions to those of human research teams. To assess the extremity of reported findings, they introduce the m-value—the probability that a random plausible analysis path would yield a result at least as extreme as the reported one. Agentic Bootstrap uses AI agents to sample thousands of such paths and estimate the m-value.

Result: AI agents successfully reproduced 72% of the ideological divergence observed in 42 human research teams analyzing the same immigration dataset. 86% of AI-generated reports passed independent AI review, and 78% passed majority human expert review, indicating strong methodological validity despite conflicting conclusions. In the immigration study, 13.5% of human analyses fell in the most extreme 5% of the analysis space (m<0.05), suggesting selective reporting. The m-value and Agentic Bootstrap provide a scalable way to evaluate the robustness of findings within the full space of plausible analyses.

Conclusion: The core challenge in empirical research is not flawed analysis but the selective exploration and reporting of a vast space of methodologically defensible alternatives. AI agents expose this issue by making analytical variation explicit and scalable. The proposed m-value and Agentic Bootstrap offer a new criterion for scientific credibility: findings should be judged not only on their own merit but also on how extreme they are relative to the full range of plausible analyses.

Abstract: Empirical research rarely admits a unique analysis. Different analytical choices can lead to different conclusions from the same data, yet these hidden forking paths are difficult to observe. We show that AI agents capture much of the analytical variation among human researchers while making these paths explicit. Across four high-stakes domains, assigning different personas is sufficient for AI agents to report divergent, often opposing, conclusions from the same data and question, with findings systematically aligned with those beliefs. In a study in which 42 human research teams analyzed the same immigration dataset, AI agents reproduced 72% of the human ideological gap in reported effect estimates. Despite reaching opposing conclusions, it is difficult to identify clear issues in each analysis based on the final AI reports: 86% passed independent AI review and 78% passed majority human expert review. These findings suggest that the central challenge is often not flawed analyses, but selective exploration and reporting from a large space of methodologically defensible analyses. AI agents may amplify this longstanding problem by making such exploration inexpensive and scalable. To address this, we introduce the m-value (multiverse value), the probability that an analysis path would produce a claim at least as extreme as the reported one. We further introduce Agentic Bootstrap, which estimates the m-value by using AI agents to sample plausible analysis paths. Applied to the human immigration study, 13.5% of reported human analyses fell in the most extreme 5% of the analysis space (m<0.05). Scientific evidence should therefore be evaluated not only by a single reported analysis but also by its position within the distribution of analyses that could reasonably have been reported. Agentic Bootstrap makes this distribution observable and turns it into a criterion for scientific credibility.

</details>


### [159] [Janus: a Playground for User-Involved Agentic Permission Management](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01510)
*Natalie Grace Brigham,Eugene Bagdasarian,Tadayoshi Kohno,Franziska Roesner*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Janus 是一个用于实现和评估用户参与式智能体权限管理设计的实验平台，包含 Janus-Core（支持多种权限管理设计的模块化系统）和 Janus-Harness（自动化评估框架）。研究基于用户参与的设计维度模型，实现了六种权限助手，并在三种场景和三类合成响应者中进行评估，发现用户输入对隐私与安全至关重要，AI 可辅助降低认知负担，但需考虑权限疲劳等真实用户行为。单一设计无法在所有情境下最优，强调应采用更系统化、情境敏感的权限管理策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前自主执行工具调用的AI智能体引发权限管理问题，用户角色在其中仍被忽视，亟需探索用户如何有效参与权限决策以保障安全与隐私。

Method: 构建 Janus 平台，包括 Janus-Core 和 Janus-Harness；基于用户参与的设计轴建立概念模型，实现六种权限管理方案，并通过自动化测试在多场景下评估其表现。

Result: 用户输入显著提升隐私与安全性；AI 辅助可减轻认知负荷；但权限疲劳等现实因素必须纳入设计考量；无统一最优方案，需依情境选择。

Conclusion: 应发展更系统化、情境敏感的权限管理方法，避免单一设计泛化应用，Janus 为未来研究提供了开放平台。

Abstract: AI agents that autonomously execute tool calls on a user's behalf raise pressing questions about permission management: what role could users play, and what role should they play? Despite many proposed approaches, the user's role in agentic permission management remains under explored. We introduce Janus, a playground system for implementing and evaluating user-involved agentic permission management designs. Janus consists of two components: Janus-Core, a modular agentic system supporting a diverse spectrum of permission management designs, and Janus-Harness, an automated evaluation framework. Grounded in a conceptual model that identifies key design axes for user involvement, we implement six permission assistants spanning the design space and evaluate them across three scenarios and three synthetic responders. We demonstrate that user input is critical and can significantly strengthen privacy and security, that AI augmentation of user decisions can help reduce cognitive load, and that realistic user behavior including permission fatigue must be accounted for in system design. No single design performs optimally across all contexts, motivating a more principled and context-sensitive approach to deploying permission assistants in agentic systems. Janus is publicly available to support future investigation into this dimension of agentic system design.

</details>


### [160] [Revisiting Chain-of-Thought Reasoning under Limited Supervision: Semi-supervised Chain-of-Thought Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01511)
*Hongyang He,Jiuming Liu,Victor Sanchez*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为Semi-CoT的半监督链式思维学习框架，利用未标注问题生成伪推理监督信号。通过为每个未标注问题采样多个伪链，基于答案级语义熵选择低熵高精度推理链作为可靠伪示范，将CoT自训练从推理时优化扩展到半监督伪监督。实验表明，伪答案精确率高达91.36%至100%，在部分数据集上取得小幅提升，但存在负迁移或性能饱和现象，说明伪监督信号虽可靠，其有效利用仍需更强的示范选择或学生模型训练策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有链式思维（CoT）方法主要在推理时使用推理链作为提示，而生成的推理轨迹很少被用作半监督学习信号。为了更充分利用未标注数据中的推理信息，需要一种能够将推理链转化为可复用的伪监督信号的方法。

Method: 提出Semi-CoT框架：对每个未标注问题采样多个伪链，计算答案级语义熵，选择低熵推理链作为高置信度伪示范，从而构建可靠的伪推理监督信号。该方法将自训练视角从推理时优化扩展至半监督伪监督。

Result: 在AQuA、SVAMP、GSM8K和MultiArith数据集上的实验表明，熵门能有效筛选出高精度伪推理链，伪答案精确率在91.36%至100%之间；在SVAMP和GSM8K上获得小幅增益，但AQuA出现负迁移，MultiArith达到性能天花板。

Conclusion: 未标注问题可以提供可靠的伪推理信号，但其有效利用仍受限于示范选择质量与学生模型训练机制，未来工作需进一步优化伪示范选取策略或改进训练方式。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning has emerged as an effective approach for activating latent reasoning capabilities in large language models. However, most existing CoT methods use reasoning chains mainly as inference-time prompts, while the generated reasoning traces are rarely reused as semi-supervised learning signals. In this report, we define \textbf{Semi-supervised Chain-of-Thought Learning} and propose \textbf{Semi-CoT}, a simple framework that uses unlabeled questions to construct pseudo reasoning supervision. Semi-CoT samples multiple pseudo-CoTs for each unlabeled question, estimates answer-level semantic entropy, and selects low-entropy reasoning chains as reliable pseudo-CoT demonstrations. This extends the self-training view of CoT from inference-time refinement to semi-supervised pseudo-supervision. Pilot experiments on AQuA, SVAMP, GSM8K, and MultiArith show that the entropy gate selects high-precision pseudo-CoTs, with pseudo-answer precision ranging from $91.36\%$ to $100\%$. Semi-CoT also gives small gains on SVAMP and GSM8K, while AQuA shows negative transfer and MultiArith reaches a ceiling. These results suggest that unlabeled questions can provide reliable pseudo reasoning signals, but their effective use still requires stronger demonstration selection or student training.

</details>


### [161] [OPINE-World: Programmatic World Modeling with Ontology-error-Prioritized Interactive Exploration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01531)
*David Courtis,Wenhao Li,Scott Sanner*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: OPINE-World 是一个基于大语言模型（LLM）的代理，能够在线从与环境的交互中学习对象中心的程序化世界模型。它通过两个协作代理组成的循环机制实现：一个在环境中行动，另一个通过回放验证和基于模型的规划来合成代码形式的世界模型，并利用一种称为“本体误差”的贝叶斯度量来引导探索。该方法在未见过的任务上表现出高数据效率和良好的泛化能力，在ARC-AGI-3基准测试中无需每游戏训练即可解决20/25个任务，动作效率得分达到78.4，优于人类基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度网络学习的世界模型虽然灵活但数据需求大且泛化能力差；而程序合成的世界模型虽数据高效、可复用，但在像素级环境中难以扩展，因缺乏对物体结构的灵活假设能力。因此需要一种既能高效学习又能适应复杂、未结构化环境的新方法。

Method: OPINE-World采用双代理协同机制：一个代理在环境中执行动作并收集经验；另一个代理基于这些经验使用大语言模型生成程序化世界模型，并通过回放验证与模型规划进行优化。同时引入‘本体误差’作为贝叶斯度量，指导探索以发现缺失或不合适的对象类型，实现动态建模与自适应学习。

Result: 在ARC-AGI-3基准测试中，OPINE-World无需针对每个游戏进行训练，成功解决了20/25个任务，动作效率得分为78.4，超越人类表现，证明了其在未知任务上的高效学习与强泛化能力。

Conclusion: OPINE-World展示了程序化世界模型在复杂、未结构化环境中的可行性与优势，结合大语言模型与形式化验证技术，实现了高效、可解释且可迁移的自主学习，为构建通用智能体提供了新范式。

Abstract: Learning how an environment behaves from interaction is central to building agents that adapt to unfamiliar tasks. World models learned with deep networks are flexible but data-hungry and transfer poorly beyond their training distribution. Program-synthesized world models, written as source code by LLMs and refined through counterexample-guided inductive synthesis (CEGIS), are instead data-efficient and reusable, yet they have been demonstrated mainly on structured-state worlds with a given object vocabulary, and a single program search does not scale to pixel-rendered environments whose object structure must be hypothesized flexibly. We introduce OPINE-World, an LLM agent that learns an object-centric programmatic world model online from interaction. OPINE-World couples two cooperating agents in a loop of hypothesis and test, one acting in the environment and one synthesizing the model in code with replay verification and model-based planning, and it steers exploration with a Bayesian measure of object-type adequacy we call ontology error. We evaluate OPINE-World on ARC-AGI-3, a benchmark for skill-acquisition efficiency in which the object vocabulary, the goal, and the action semantics are withheld. OPINE-World solves 20 of 25 games without per-game training and reaches an action-efficiency score of 78.4 against the human baseline.

### [162] [Scaling Trends for Lie Detector Oversight in Preference Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01567)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型中的欺骗行为难以监控和防范，现有方法如SOLiD通过使用谎言检测器识别需人工审查的响应，但其在大规模模型和复杂场景下的有效性与鲁棒性有待验证。

Method: 将SOLiD方法扩展至更大规模的语言模型，并在多种真实偏好学习场景中进行评估；通过调整检测器训练数据分布与实际训练数据的一致性来测试其对分布偏移的敏感性。

Result: 在405B参数模型上，当检测器真阳性率为99%时，未检测到的欺骗行为降至14%，且无需人工标注者参与微调阶段仍能保持欺骗水平不显著上升；然而，若存在分布偏移，检测器假阳性率可能升至不可接受水平。

Conclusion: SOLiD在大规模模型上表现出良好的可扩展性，但在面对数据分布差异时仍面临挑战，需进一步优化检测器的泛化能力以提升实际应用可行性。

Abstract: Deceptive behavior in LLMs is costly to monitor and prevent, motivating approaches such as Scalable Oversight via Lie Detectors (SOLiD) (Cundy & Gleave, 2025), which uses lie detectors to identify responses for review by high-cost labelers. In this paper, we scale SOLiD to larger models and evaluate it in more diverse and realistic preference-learning settings. We find favorable scaling: undetected deception drops from 34% for 1B-parameter models to 14% for 405B-parameter models at a detector true positive rate of 99%, and expensive human labelers can be removed entirely from the fine-tuning phase without a statistically significant increase in deception. However, SOLiD is sensitive to distribution shift between detector training and preference-training data, which can drive detector false positive rates to impractical levels.

Result: 从1,475个数据集中生成160个跨生态水文学、冰川学、气溶胶-云相互作用、植被物候学和平流层化学等领域的科学假设；模型预测的新颖数据集配对在可信度上接近真实文献中的共使用实例；因子实验表明假设排名具有稳定性，但评分高度依赖评估者身份。

Abstract: Large language models have recently been explored for scientific hypothesis generation, but most prior work relies on unstructured literature and free-form textual claims. We present a pipeline for Earth observation that grounds hypothesis generation directly in the NASA Earth Observation Knowledge Graph. A heterogeneous graph neural network trained on historical co-usage relations ranks candidate dataset pairings, and a three-agent LLM pipeline filters, generates, and evaluates structured research hypotheses. Applied to 1,475 NASA datasets, the system produces 160 hypotheses spanning multiple Earth-science domains, including ecohydrology, glaciology, aerosol--cloud interactions, vegetation phenology, and stratospheric chemistry. Model-predicted novel dataset pairings are rated nearly as plausible as held-out real co-usages from the literature, indicating that the pipeline surfaces scientifically coherent yet unexplored combinations. A 2*2*2 factorial experiment across GPT-5.2 and Claude Sonnet 4.6 shows that hypothesis rankings remain stable, while absolute scores depend strongly on judge identity, highlighting limitations of single-judge LLM evaluation.

### [164] [Hawk: Harnessing Hardware-Aware Knowledge for High-Performance NPU Kernel Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01590)
*Junyi Wen,Ruiyan Zhuang,Yongjia Xu,Pengtu Li,Rui Zou,Hongyi Chen,Chingman Wan,Puxu Yang,Wuhui Chen,Yanlin Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Hawk 是一个无需训练的框架，通过三个核心模块——运行时知识合成、瓶颈感知知识检索和效果驱动的知识提炼——在神经处理单元（NPU）上实现高性能内核生成。它有效解决了大语言模型在 NPU 上因缺乏硬件特定先验而导致的崩溃与性能下降问题，显著提升生成准确率至 80.0%，并带来最高 2.2 倍的执行速度提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前 NPU 高性能内核开发面临硬件约束隐晦、内存层次严格等挑战，而大语言模型因缺乏硬件特定先验，在 NPU 上生成代码时易引发运行时崩溃和性能退化，亟需一种能融合硬件知识的自动化解决方案。

Method: Hawk 采用三项核心技术：1）运行时知识合成模块，使用三部分可执行知识表示将错误上下文与可执行语义耦合；2）瓶颈感知知识检索模块，基于二维检索范式，将查询投影到正交的语法空间与硬件对齐语义空间；3）效果驱动知识提炼模块，利用大语言模型进行语义仲裁，根据实际执行反馈持续修剪错误、合并冗余，实现知识的动态优化。

Result: 在真实 NPU 工作负载上的评估表明，Hawk 将代码生成准确率从 49.4% 提升至 80.0%，同时相较最先进基线实现最高达 2.2 倍的执行速度提升。

Conclusion: Hawk 成功构建了一个无需训练但具备硬件感知能力的代码生成框架，为 NPU 高性能内核开发提供了高效、可靠且自动化的解决方案，显著突破了现有方法在准确性与性能上的瓶颈。

Abstract: Developing high-performance kernels for Neural Processing Units (NPUs) is a critical industry bottleneck, requiring developers to manually navigate implicit hardware constraints and strict memory hierarchies. While large language models offer immense automation potential, they fail catastrophically on NPUs due to a fundamental lack of hardware-specific priors. Naively transplanting code snippets from similar NPU kernels may pass the compiler, but it consistently triggers runtime crashes and performance degradation by blindly violating underlying hardware constraints. To overcome this, we introduce Hawk, a training-free framework that harnesses hardware-aware knowledge through three core modules: (1) Run-Time Knowledge Synthesis Module, which employs a Triple-Part Executable Knowledge Representation to inherently couple the error context with executable semantics; (2) Bottleneck-Aware Knowledge Retrieval Module, which implements a 2D-Retrieval paradigm to project queries into orthogonal syntactic and hardware-aligned semantic spaces; and (3) Effect-Driven Knowledge Distillation Module, which leverages LLM-driven semantic arbitration to continuously distill the knowledge by pruning errors and consolidating redundancies based on the empirical execution feedback. Extensive evaluations on real-world NPU workloads demonstrate that Hawk elevates generation accuracy from 49.4% to 80.0%, while achieving up to a 2.2x execution speedup over state-of-the-art baselines.

### [165] [Safe and Adaptive Cloud Healing: Verifying LLM-Generated Recovery Plans with a Neural-Symbolic World Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01595)
*Junyan Tan,Haoran Lin,Siyuan Guo,Yichen Fang,Xinyue Luo,Tianyu Shen,Zeyu Qiao*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: PASE提出一种新型故障自愈框架，将恢复视为神经符号程序合成任务。通过大语言模型生成结构化恢复计划，神经符号世界模型验证计划可行性，并利用深度强化学习训练的元提示优化器生成最优提示以指导规划过程，形成闭环的动态自适应恢复机制。在真实云环境故障注入数据集上，PASE显著优于现有方法，平均恢复时间减少超40%，未知故障检测准确率提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: As the scale and complexity of cloud-based AI systems continue to escalate, ensuring service reliability through rapid fault detection and adaptive recovery has become a critical challenge. While existing approaches integrate Large Language Models (LLMs) for semantic understanding and Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) for policy optimization, they often rely on sequential, loosely coupled architectures that underutilize the generative and reasoning capabilities of LLMs. In this paper, we propose a paradigm shift with PASE, a Planning-Aware Semantic self-healing engine, a novel fault self-healing framework that reconceptualizes recovery as a neuro-symbolic program synthesis task. PASE employs an LLM as a core Plan Synthesis Engine to generate structured recovery plans from a library of semantic primitives. A Neural-Symbolic World Model verifies plan feasibility through simulation, while a Meta-Prompt Optimizer, trained via DRL, learns to generate optimal prompts that guide the LLM's planning process. This tight reason-plan-verify-adapt loop enables dynamic, context-aware recovery strategy generation beyond predefined action spaces. Experiments on a real-world cloud fault injection dataset demonstrate that PASE significantly outperforms state-of-the-art methods, reducing average system recovery time by over 40% and improving fault detection accuracy in unknown fault scenarios. Our framework advances autonomous system management by unifying LLM-based reasoning with model-assisted verification and meta-learned guidance.

### [166] [SemHash-LLM: A Multi-Granularity Semantic Hashing Framework for Document Deduplication](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01601)
*Xinyi Fang,Kejian Tong,Jiabei Liu,Tao Ning,Yuhang He*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SemHash LLM 是一种多粒度文档去重框架，结合语义投影哈希、加权 MinHash、对比边界学习和选择性大模型判断，通过门控融合字符、词元和文档级信号，采用级联过滤减少候选集，实现高效且准确的去重。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大规模文档中保持语义等价性的同时，需要高效处理海量数据，现有方法在应对模板污染、短文本扰动、内容包含和病毒片段等问题时存在不足。

Method: 采用门控融合机制整合字符、词元和文档层级信号；利用语义投影哈希生成紧凑二进制编码；通过注意力加权 MinHash 去除冗余内容并突出关键信息；引入自适应决策边界与不确定性估计提升鲁棒性；设计级联过滤流水线降低计算开销。

Result: 实验表明，SemHash LLM 在保持高检测质量的同时，神经网络验证成本低于1%，显著提升了效率与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: SemHash LLM 为大规模文档去重提供了一种高效、准确且鲁棒的解决方案，适用于复杂现实场景中的海量文本处理。

Abstract: Large scale document deduplication must preserve semantic equivalence while remaining efficient over massive corpora. We present SemHash LLM, a multi granularity framework that unifies semantic projection hashing, attention weighted MinHash, contrastive boundary learning, and selective LLM based adjudication. The method combines character, token, and document level signals through gated fusion, then applies a cascaded filtering pipeline for efficient candidate reduction. Semantic projection hashing learns compact binary codes in distilled LLM embedding space, while attention weighted Min- Hash suppresses boilerplate and emphasizes informative content. Adaptive decision boundaries and uncertainty estimation further improve robustness across template pollution, short text perturbation, containment, and viral fragments. Experiments show that SemHash LLM achieves strong duplicate detection quality with less than one percent neural verification cost.

</details>


### [167] [Profit-Based Counterfactual Explanations for Product Improvement: A Case Study of Manga Sales in Japan](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01610)

Method: 将反事实解释建模为利润最大化问题，以利润作为核心优化目标，将距离项重新解释为修改产品属性的成本，从而构建一个经济意义明确、无需外生目标设定的反事实解释框架。

Conclusion: PBCE为反事实解释提供了一个更贴近现实决策场景的新范式，尤其适用于需要优化特定经济目标的管理与营销应用，显著增强了模型解释的实用价值。

Abstract: Counterfactual explanation (CE) is widely used to enhance the interpretability of machine learning models and support data-driven decision-making based on model predictions. However, existing CE methods typically require two exogenously specified inputs: a desired output value (target) and a distance function that quantifies changes in explanatory variables. In regression settings, neither the validity of target specification nor the practical interpretation of the distance metric has been sufficiently addressed. Furthermore, most existing CE methods focus on altering predictions rather than optimizing a decision objective, even though real-world decision-making often requires explicit objective maximization. To address these limitations, we formulate CE as a profit maximization problem in management and marketing contexts and propose a framework termed profit-based counterfactual explanation (PBCE). PBCE eliminates the need for exogenous target specification by directly maximizing profit as the primary optimization objective. Concurrently, the distance term is reinterpreted as the cost of modifying product attributes, providing a clear and economically grounded interpretation.

### [168] [Scaling with Confidence: Calibrating Confidence of LLMs for Adaptive Test Time Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01612)
*Xuqing Yang,Yi Yuan,Shanzhe Lei,Xuhong Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出C3RL，一种结合正确性、校准性和基于数据集的参考准确率奖励的新型强化学习算法，以解决大语言模型在推理和问答任务中因过度自信而导致幻觉的问题。实验表明，C3RL在不牺牲准确率的前提下显著提升了模型校准能力，并在此基础上提出CAS（基于置信度的自适应测试时缩放）策略，通过根据置信度分配计算资源，在保持性能的同时将推理预算减少最多达12.33倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前强化学习奖励设计主要关注响应正确性，忽视了对模型置信度准确性的激励，导致模型在不确定时过度自信并产生幻觉，影响可靠性与效率。

Method: 提出C3RL算法，融合正确性、校准性和数据集参考准确率三重奖励信号；进一步设计CAS策略，在推理阶段依据模型输出的置信度动态调整计算资源分配。

Result: C3RL在8个文本和多模态数据集上均实现更优的校准效果且不损失准确性；CAS在多个数据集上超越多数投票方法，同时显著降低推理开销。

Conclusion: C3RL与CAS的协同作用为构建更可靠、高效的大语言模型提供了新路径，具有实际部署价值，相关代码、数据和模型将公开发布。

Abstract: Training large language models (LLMs) with reinforcement learning (RL) has significantly advanced their performance on reasoning and question-answering tasks. However, prevailing RL reward designs typically prioritize response correctness, neglecting to incentivize models to express their confidence accurately. This leads to a critical problem: performance gains are often accompanied by poor calibration between confidence and accuracy, misleading models to overconfidently hallucinate when uncertain. To address this limitation, we propose $\textbf{C}$orrectness and $\textbf{C}$onfidence $\textbf{C}$alibration $\textbf{R}$einforcement $\textbf{L}$earning ($\textbf{C3RL}$), a novel RL algorithm integrating correctness, calibration and dataset-informed reference accuracy rewards together. Comprehensive evaluation across 8 text and multimodal datasets demonstrates that C3RL enhances calibration without sacrificing accuracy, outperforming the current state-of-the-art method in both performance and calibration metrics. Utilizing the well-calibrated verbalized confidence from C3RL, we further introduce $\textbf{C}$onfidence-based $\textbf{A}$daptive Test Time $\textbf{S}$caling ($\textbf{CAS}$), an adjustable inference-time strategy that allocates computational resources based on response confidence. Experiments show that CAS surpasses majority voting on both in-domain and out-of-domain datasets while reducing the inference budget by up to 12.33 times. We believe the synergy of C3RL and CAS paves the way for deploying more reliable and resource-efficient LLMs. The code, data and models will be released.

### [169] [Spatial Support Matters: Geometry-Aware Graph Fusion for Rainfall Field Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01621)
*Low Jun Yu,Niramay Kachhadiya,Herath Mudiyanselage Viraj Vidura Herath,Sanka Rasnayaka,Lucy Amanda Marshall*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了一种几何感知的多支持异构图神经网络，能够处理点、线、网格等不同空间支持的降雨观测数据，通过跨支持消息传递融合信息，实现高精度的细粒度降雨重建。该方法在新加坡数据上相比经典插值方法降低23.2%的RMSE，且在悉尼数据上的泛化实验表明，当观测稀疏度高于场的空间相关长度时，多支持融合优势显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有异构图方法在特征空间中融合不同空间支持的降雨观测（如雨量计、微波链路、雷达/卫星），但忽略了观测支持的几何特性，导致信息损失。为提升城市洪水建模中的降雨重建精度，需保留并利用不同观测类型的几何结构信息。

Method: 构建一个几何感知的多支持异构图神经网络，将点（0D）、线（1D）和网格（2D）观测分别作为独立节点层表示，并通过跨支持消息传递进行信息融合；采用归纳式掩码节点训练策略，使预测分辨率与传感分辨率解耦，支持任意目标位置或网格的重建。

Conclusion: 提出的几何感知多支持图神经网络有效整合了不同空间支持的降雨观测，显著提升了细粒度降雨重建精度，其性能依赖于观测密度与场空间相关性的匹配程度，具备良好的可扩展性和实用性。

Abstract: Fine-scale rainfall reconstruction is critical for urban flood modeling, but real rainfall sensing systems observe the field through incompatible spatial supports: gauges measure points, microwave links measure paths, and radar/satellite products measure gridded areas. These differences in measurement support impose geometrically distinct constraints on the rainfall field, yet existing heterogeneous graph approaches reconcile such sources in feature space, giving each its own embedding while discarding the geometry of its support. We propose a geometry-aware multi-support heterogeneous graph neural network that represents each observation according to its support type (0D point, 1D line, or 2D grid) as a distinct node layer, and fuses them through cross-support message passing into a point-support prediction layer from which the field is reconstructed. An inductive masked-node formulation decouples prediction resolution from sensing resolution, allowing the same trained model to reconstruct the field at user-defined target locations or display grids. On Singapore data, the proposed method reduces RMSE by 23.2\% over the classical interpolation baseline, inverse-distance weighting, and consistently outperforms other neural architectures such as convolutional fusion and support-agnostic heterogeneous graph baselines. A generalization study using data from Sydney, Australia lets us characterize when multi-support fusion helps: the available skill appears to depend on gauge spacing relative to the spatial correlation length of the field, so fusion delivers the largest gains where the field is under-sampled relative to its correlation length and little when it is already resolved. Code and models will be open-sourced upon paper acceptance.

Abstract: Universal traffic laws describe recurrent patterns in congestion, mobility and driving behavior across cities, providing a scientific basis for transportation planning, management and control. Their discovery, however, remains expert-driven, requiring candidate regularities to be identified from heterogeneous observational evidence or validated through intervention experiments. Although autonomous artificial intelligence (AI) systems have advanced scientific discovery in controlled laboratory settings, extending them to complex transportation domains remains a challenge. Here we present TrafficSci, an agentic AI system that formulates traffic-law discovery as an iterative, auditable workflow integrating evidence scoping, critic-judge hypothesis induction, and observational-interventional validation. TrafficSci provides a route for extending AI-driven scientific discovery from controlled domains to complex urban systems.

### [171] [Diverse Evidence, Better Forecasts: Multi-Agent Deliberation Under Information Asymmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01661)
*Yuante Li,Yicheng Tao,Kate Zhang,Taozhi Wang,Gefei Gu,Yaxin Zhou*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文提出通过设计信息不对称来改进多智能体系统在事件预测中的表现，通过将证据划分为共享和私有部分，确保每个智能体拥有独特知识，从而促进真正的信念修正而非群体盲从。提出的InfoDelphi框架结合了相关性感知的证据路由、基于理由的迭代讨论和置信度加权聚合，在多项基准测试中显著优于单智能体和现有多智能体方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多智能体系统在事件预测中常因所有智能体接收相同信息而导致集体思维（herding），无法实现真正意义上的推理改进。因此需要引入信息不对称以增强智能体间的多样性与有效讨论。

Method: 将证据划分为公共共享和私有独立两部分，使每个智能体拥有独家信息；通过相关性感知的证据路由分发信息，进行基于理由的迭代讨论，并采用置信度加权聚合最终结果。

Result: 在PolyGym基准上，InfoDelphi相比最强单智能体和多智能体基线，在Brier分数上提升12-18%，准确率提升4-8个百分点；移除信息不对称后性能显著下降，验证了输入多样性是多智能体推理有效性的关键。

Conclusion: 信息不对称是实现有效多智能体推理的核心机制，通过赋予智能体独特的知识基础，可显著提升预测准确性与系统鲁棒性，为未来多智能体系统设计提供了重要方向。

Abstract: Multi-agent systems are increasingly used for forecasting future events, as deliberation among multiple LLMs is believed to improve reasoning and calibration. Yet existing approaches overlook a critical design choice: what information each agent receives. When all agents are given identical evidence, deliberation collapses into herding rather than genuine belief revision, leaving multi-agent systems little better than a single agent. We identify this as a fundamental gap and propose designed information asymmetry to close it: by partitioning evidence into shared public and disjoint private subsets, each agent holds exclusive knowledge that can only reach others through deliberation. We theoretically show that this decomposition reduces inter-agent error correlation, and instantiate it in InfoDelphi, a framework combining relevance-aware evidence routing, rationale-based iterative deliberation, and confidence-weighted aggregation. On PolyGym, a benchmark of 375 binary forecasting questions derived from real-world prediction markets, InfoDelphi outperforms the strongest single-agent and multi-agent baselines by 12--18% in Brier score and 4--8 percentage points in accuracy. More detailed experiments confirm that removing information asymmetry eliminates most deliberation gains, establishing diversity of input as the key enabler of effective multi-agent reasoning.
