### [172] [Separating Expert Retention from Autonomous Source Inference in Raw-ECG-Replay-Free Continual ECG Deployment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01674)
*Yufan Lu,Xinhui Liu,Chenyang Xu,Yuxi Zhou,Hao Wang,Shenda Hong*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为\ours{}的增量专家库方法，用于多源心电图（ECG）部署中在无法保留原始数据时的模型更新。该方法基于冻结的1024维ECGFounder特征，为每个新来源添加一个平衡Softmax线性专家，并仅在保留的训练特征和源标签上拟合轻量级路由器。通过验证校准的边际规则融合两个最可能的专家，避免单一路由决策。实验表明，在无源标识情况下，使用top-2边际融合可达到0.7782的宏F1，优于MLP路由器的0.7756，但提升有限，且与最优情况差距稳定在0.0111–0.0133之间，表明自主源推断仍是主要瓶颈。尽管不重放原始ECG，但需保留冻结的训练特征以更新路由器，因此非内存自由。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多源心电图部署中，当早期原始心电图数据无法保留或重放时，如何有效整合新数据源并保持模型性能成为关键挑战。传统方法虽可通过冻结主干网络并为各源分配独立分类器防止参数干扰，但在缺乏源元数据的情况下仍难以选择合适的专家，导致性能下降。因此需要一种无需重放原始数据、能自动识别源并高效融合专家预测的方法。

Method: \ours{}方法基于冻结的1024维ECGFounder特征，构建一个增量专家银行。每新增一个数据源即添加一个平衡Softmax线性专家；同时，仅利用已观察到的源的训练特征和标签训练一个轻量级路由器。采用验证校准的边际规则对两个最可能的专家进行融合，而非强制选择单一专家，从而提升鲁棒性和泛化能力。

Result: 在CPSC、PTB-XL、Georgia和Chapman-Shaoxing数据集上，有源信息时的专家选择达到0.7915±0.0036的宏F1，接近离线独立头参考结果0.7885±0.0009，证明了强源感知专家保留能力。在无源ID条件下，MLP路由器得分为0.7756±0.0027，而top-2边际融合提升至0.7782±0.0022，增幅仅为+0.0026，其95%置信区间包含零，表明改进不显著。三种不同源顺序下，top-2与最优之间的差距维持在0.0111–0.0133，说明自主源推断仍是主要瓶颈。

Conclusion: 所提出的\ours{}方法在无需重放原始心电图的前提下，实现了对多源数据的有效增量学习，具备良好的源感知能力。然而，当前性能受限于自主源推断能力，未来需进一步优化路由器在无源标签下的泛化能力。此外，由于需保留冻结的训练特征，系统并非完全内存自由，存在一定的存储开销。

Abstract: In multi-source ECG deployment, models may need to incorporate new data sources when earlier raw ECGs cannot be retained or replayed. Freezing a pretrained backbone and assigning each source an isolated classifier prevents parameter interference, but deployment still requires selecting an expert when source metadata are unavailable. We study this distinction through \ours{}, an incremental expert bank built on frozen 1024-dimensional ECGFounder features. Each arriving domain adds a balanced-softmax linear expert, while a lightweight router is fitted only on retained training features and domain labels from sources observed so far. A validation-calibrated margin rule fuses the two most likely experts instead of committing to a single routed expert.
  On CPSC, PTB-XL, Georgia, and Chapman-Shaoxing, source-aware expert selection reaches $0.7915\pm0.0036$ Macro-F1 and a matched offline independent-head reference reaches $0.7885\pm0.0009$, supporting strong source-aware expert retention. Without source IDs, an MLP router reaches $0.7756\pm0.0027$ and top-2 margin fusion reaches $0.7782\pm0.0022$. The top-2 gain over hard MLP routing is small ($+0.0026$), with a 95\% confidence interval from paired bootstrap that includes zero. Across three domain orders, the top-2-to-oracle gap remains $0.0111$--$0.0133$, identifying autonomous source inference as the main remaining bottleneck. No raw ECGs are replayed, but frozen training features are retained for router updates; the method is therefore not memory-free.

</details>


### [173] [Epistemic Goggles: A Pretrained Module that Induces an Epistemic Frame via Gradient Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01690)
*Joshua Penman*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究提出Goggles，一种通过干预微调梯度而非数据来改变语言模型对文本认知立场的模块。在训练中，Goggles修改LLM LoRA接收的梯度，赋予其特定的元认知框架（如‘此内容为虚构’），从而在不依赖虚构标注的情况下，使模型能正确识别虚构内容约91%的时间。该方法保留了模型能力（在GPQA和TruthfulQA上表现与基线相当或更优），且可迁移至不同框架（如‘属于红木研究的安全评估’）。即使后续微调试图恢复原信念，Goggles仍能维持所施加的框架，有效缓解‘否定忽视’问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有微调方法在处理明确标注为虚构的文档时，模型仍会错误相信其核心主张，即存在‘否定忽视’现象。传统方法依赖于数据层面的标注，但无法从根本上解决模型内化虚假信念的问题。因此需要一种能够持续影响模型认知立场的机制，尤其是在使用已知不一致或误导性数据进行训练时。

Method: 提出Goggles模块，通过在监督微调过程中动态修改模型梯度，向模型注入预设的元认知框架（如‘此内容为虚构’）。该模块以冻结状态应用于未见过的数据，无需重新训练。其核心是学习如何在梯度层面施加影响，使模型在理解文本时保持指定的认知立场。

Result: 使用Goggles训练后的模型在无虚构标注的文档中，能将内容识别为虚构的比例达到约91%，显著优于仅9%的基线表现。同时，模型在标准评测任务（GPQA、TruthfulQA）上的性能保持甚至超越基线，证明其能力未被损害。此外，该框架可灵活适配多种认知设定，并在持续微调中保持稳定性。

Conclusion: Goggles提供了一种有效的方法，在不改变数据的前提下，通过梯度干预实现对语言模型认知立场的控制。它解决了使用误导性或不一致数据训练时模型吸收错误信念的问题，为安全、可控地利用大规模非对齐数据提供了新路径。

Abstract: Finetuning a language model on documents that are explicitly annotated as fictional results in a model that still actually believes the documents' core claims, an effect known as Negation Neglect. In our evaluations, models trained on documents prefixed and suffixed with such annotations correctly identify the relevant claims as fictional only about 9% of the time. To address this, we introduce Goggles, a learned module that intervenes on the finetuning gradient rather than the data. During supervised finetuning, a Goggles module edits the gradients an LLM LoRA receives, imparting a chosen epistemic frame (the stance the model takes toward the nature of what it reads) to whatever the documents teach. A Goggles instance is trained once for a given base model, frame, and LoRA configuration, then applied frozen to documents it was never trained on. Trained through Goggles on those same documents, now carrying no fictional annotation, the model flags the content as fictional roughly 91% of the time, while preserving capability (GPQA and TruthfulQA match or exceed baseline). The same architecture supports other frames: a Goggles instance can be trained to treat documents as "part of an AI safety evaluation by Redwood Research" rather than simply as fiction. The imparted frame persists under continued finetuning that pushes back toward the claim, where prior interventions revert. Goggles suggests a path toward training language models on known-misaligned data without absorbing the behaviors that data demonstrates.

</details>


### [174] [COMFYCLAW: Self-Evolving Skill Harnesses for Image Generation Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01709)
*Zongxia Li,Dawei Liu,Fuxiao Liu,Yuhang Zhou,Xiyang Wu,Jingxi Chen,Jing Xie,Xiaomin Wu,Lichao Sun*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: COMFYCLAW 是一个用于控制 ComfyUI 工作流的代理技能演化框架，通过类型化图编辑、工具分阶段暴露、自动回滚无效编辑以及基于区域级视觉语言模型的验证器，实现高效的工作流构建。该框架通过提炼历史轨迹、执行错误和验证反馈，逐步构建可复用的代理技能库，在多个基准测试中显著优于基线方法，并获得人类评估者的偏好认可，证明了技能演化在提升代理可靠性与性能方面的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着代理在重复性、领域特定任务中的广泛应用，记忆和可复用技能对提高工作流构建效率至关重要。现有方法缺乏对历史经验的有效利用，难以应对视觉工作流中的复杂错误和约束，因此亟需一种能够持续学习并优化工作流构建能力的机制。

Method: COMFYCLAW 将工作流构建建模为类型化图编辑，按构建阶段组织工具，支持自动回滚无效操作；引入区域级视觉语言模型（VLM）作为验证器，将视觉失败转化为可操作的修复建议；通过整合历史运行数据（轨迹、错误、反馈），逐步演化出一个渐进披露的技能库，实现技能的积累与复用。

Result: 在四个基准划分、三种代理模型和两种图像骨干网络下，COMFYCLAW 在所有六种配置中均取得最佳平均图像生成评估分数，显著优于仅使用验证器但无技能演化的基线。人类评估也表明，用户更偏好 COMFYCLAW 而非无技能演化的变体。

Conclusion: 技能演化是提升代理在重复性视觉工作流构建中可靠性与性能的有效机制，有助于实现更智能、自适应的自动化流程。

Abstract: Agents are increasingly used to construct workflows and assist humans in completing recurring tasks more efficiently. As these workflows become repeated and domain-specific, agent memory and reusable skills become increasingly important: agents should be able to recall workflow patterns, execution constraints, and user preferences from previous runs. We study this problem in workflow-based image generation and introduce COMFYCLAW, an agentic skill evolution harness for controlling ComfyUI workflows. COMFYCLAW formulates workflow construction as typed graph editing, exposes tools organized by construction stage, automatically reverts invalid edits, and uses a region-level vision-language model (VLM) verifier to translate visual failures into actionable repair suggestions. The framework further evolves a progressively disclosed skill library, where trajectories, execution errors, and verifier feedback from previous runs are distilled into reusable Agent Skills. Across four benchmark splits, three agent models, and two image backbones, COMFYCLAW achieves the best average image-generation evaluation score across all six agent configurations, outperforming a verifier-only baseline without skill evolution. Human annotations further show that annotators prefer COMFYCLAW over variants without skill evolution. Our results suggest that skill evolution is an effective mechanism for improving agent reliability and performance in recurring visual workflow construction.

### [175] [Generic Expert Coverage for Pruning SparseMixture-of-Experts Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01710)
*Yongqin Zeng,Sicheng Pan,Jiale Wang,Hai-tao Zheng,Hong-Gee Kim,Chunxia Ma,XiuTeng Zhou*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出一种名为Generic TB-Coverage的覆盖感知专家剪枝方法，利用通用文本语料（WikiText2和C4）进行校准，通过分别评估每个专家在不同语料上的效用并遵循固定预算覆盖规则来保留高价值专家，从而在无需下游校准数据的情况下提升稀疏激活MoE模型的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有专家剪枝方法依赖单一聚合重要性评分，易受主导校准模式影响，导致保留的专家偏向特定模式；而稀疏激活的MoE语言模型中存在大量结构化冗余，需更鲁棒的剪枝策略以保持跨语料覆盖。

Method: 提出Generic TB-Coverage方法：对每个专家在WikiText2和C4两个通用语料上分别计算其效用，采用固定预算覆盖规则优先保留各语料中的高实用性专家，再构建最终剪枝掩码，避免单一评分偏差。

Result: 在Qwen1.5-MoE-A2.7B和DeepSeek-MoE-16B-Base模型上，于25%、50%、75%保留率下，相比随机剪枝、REAP和ExpertSparsity，在六个零样本基准测试中平均准确率均有提升，且在WikiText2和C4上的困惑度下降更少；尤其在激进剪枝（25%与50%保留）时增益显著，表明跨语料覆盖是有效的通用先验信息。

Conclusion: Generic TB-Coverage通过覆盖感知机制有效缓解了传统剪枝方法的偏差问题，在无下游校准数据条件下实现更优性能，证明了使用通用语料作为校准数据的可行性与有效性。

Abstract: Sparsely activated Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) language models contain substantial structured redundancy among routed experts, but pruning them without downstream calibration data remains challenging. Existing expert-pruning methods typically rely on a single aggregated importance score, which can bias the retained set toward experts favored by dominant calibration patterns. We propose \textbf{Generic TB-Coverage}, a coverage-aware expert pruning method that uses only generic text corpora (WikiText2 and C4) for calibration. Instead of collapsing expert utility into one score, our method profiles per-expert utility separately on each corpus and enforces a fixed-budget coverage rule that preserves high-utility experts from each corpus before constructing the final pruning mask. Across Qwen1.5-MoE-A2.7B and DeepSeek-MoE-16B-Base at 25\%, 50\%, and 75\% retention budgets, our method improves average accuracy on six common zero-shot benchmarks over random pruning, REAP, and ExpertSparsity, while also reducing perplexity degradation on WikiText2 and C4. The gains are largest under aggressive pruning (25\% and 50\% retain), suggesting that preserving cross-corpus expert coverage is an effective generic-data prior for MoE pruning. Our improvements hold with fixed pruning budgets and no downstream calibration data.

### [176] [Distributionally Robust Listwise Preference Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01715)
*Xudong Wu,Jian Qian,Pangpang Liu,Vaneet Aggarwal,Jiayu Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究在排名标签不确定下的列表型偏好优化，提出一种点对点的总变差鲁棒Plackett-Luce目标函数，通过将排名标签的不确定性直接建模，实现对候选列表的鲁棒性优化。该方法可精确分解为名义PL损失与最坏情况修正项，并通过升序排序隐式得分简化计算复杂度至O(K log K)，具有良好的离线与在线优化保证。实验表明，在离线和在线场景下，该方法在干净标签下保持性能，在噪声环境下显著提升鲁棒性，并改善奖励模型与GPT-4评价指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有鲁棒偏好优化主要关注成对监督及数据集、提示或偏好对层面的鲁棒性，但未充分考虑在候选列表上由于标注者不一致、近似平局、损失的排名反馈或奖励模型噪声导致的排名标签不确定性问题。因此，亟需一种能直接处理列表级排名不确定性的鲁棒优化方法。

Method: 提出点对点总变差鲁棒Plackett-Luce目标函数，通过在给定候选列表条件下对排名标签进行鲁棒建模。该损失函数可分解为名义PL损失与最坏情况修正项；最坏情况排名可通过将当前隐式得分按升序排序获得，从而将原本需$K!$枚举的内层最大化问题降至$O(K\log K)$复杂度。

Result: 在离线固定列表设置中，该鲁棒目标函数为凸函数，投影随机次梯度算法可在$O(ε^{-2})$样本复杂度内达到全局$ε$-次优解；在在线策略诱导设置中，证明了弱凸性，并实现了$\widetilde O(ε^{-2})$的Moreau包络驻点收敛。实验显示，该方法在离线对齐中保持良好性能并增强抗噪能力，在在线对齐中提升了基于奖励模型的候选扩展可靠性，并改善了奖励模型与外部GPT-4评判指标。

Conclusion: 本文提出的鲁棒列表偏好优化方法有效应对了排名标签不确定性问题，兼具理论保障与实际性能优势，为大语言模型对齐提供了更稳健的优化框架。

Abstract: Existing robust preference optimization for language-model alignment mainly studies pairwise supervision and places robustness at the dataset, prompt, or preference-pair level. We instead study listwise preference optimization under ranking-label uncertainty: given a prompt and a candidate list, the observed ranking over that list may be ambiguous due to annotator inconsistency, near-ties, lossy rankwise feedback, or reward-model noise. We propose a pointwise total-variation robust Plackett--Luce objective that directly robustifies the ranking label conditional on the candidate list. The robust loss admits an exact decomposition into the nominal PL loss plus a worst-case PL correction, and the worst-case ranking is obtained by sorting current implicit scores in ascending order, reducing the inner maximization from $K!$ enumeration to $O(K\log K)$. This tractable structure yields strong offline and online optimization guarantees. In the offline fixed-list setting, the robust objective is convex and projected stochastic subgradient reaches global $ε$-suboptimality with $O(ε^{-2})$ sample complexity. In the online policy-induced setting, where candidate lists are generated by the current policy, we establish weak convexity and $\widetilde O(ε^{-2})$ Moreau-envelope stationarity. Experiments in offline LLM alignment show that the proposed robust correction largely preserves performance under clean labels and improves robustness under noise. In online alignment, it makes reward-model-ranked candidate expansion more reliable and improves both reward-model and external GPT-4 judge metrics.

</details>


### [177] [DRL-CLBA: A Clean Label Backdoor Attack for Speech Classification via DDPG Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01729)
*Yueming Huang,Wenhan Yao,Fen Xiao,Xiarun Chen,Weiping Wen*

Main category: cs.AI

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有语音分类深度学习模型易受后门攻击，尤其样本特定攻击虽能规避多数防御，但依赖污染标签，易被人工数据检测发现。因此亟需一种不依赖污染标签、更隐蔽且高效的后门攻击方法以评估系统安全性。

Method: 提出基于DDPG强化学习框架的DRL-CLBA攻击方法，结合深度音频隐写技术将样本特定触发器嵌入音频，在模型深层特征空间中构建特征锚点，通过强化学习优化目标样本向锚点靠近，实现无标签迁移的后门污染。

Result: 在三个数据集和四种不同深度神经网络上的实验显示，DRL-CLBA攻击成功率达高，能有效绕过微调、剪枝及频谱签名等防御手段，展现出对语音控制系统的严重威胁。

Conclusion: DRL-CLBA是一种高效且隐蔽的清洁标签后门攻击方法，其在特征空间中构建锚点并利用强化学习优化样本，显著提升了攻击成功率与抗防御能力，暴露出当前语音分类系统在安全防护方面的重大缺陷。

Abstract: Deep learning models for speech classification are vulnerable to backdoor attacks, where malicious triggers cause misclassification at inference time. While sample-specific attacks can bypass many defenses, they often rely on poisoned label attack, making them detectable via manual data defense. In this paper, we propose DRL-CLBA, a novel clean label backdoor attack for speech classification that leverages Deep Deterministic Policy Gradient (DDPG) reinforcement learning. We also utilize deep audio steganography to embed sample-specific triggers into source audio, creating feature-space anchors. The proposed reinforcement learning framework effectively optimizes target samples toward trigger-bearing anchor points in the model's deep latent space, enabling label-migration-free poisoning of target samples. Experimental results across three datasets and four different DNNs demonstrate that DRL-CLBA achieves a high attack success rate, effectively bypassing some backdoor defenses. The attack demonstrates strong resistance against fine-tuning, pruning, and spectral signature defenses, exposing critical vulnerabilities in speech-controlled systems.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: reformalization 是一项具有潜力但挑战显著的任务。成功实施依赖于精心设计的转换管道，包括对目标系统语义的深入理解、有效的映射策略以及适度的人工介入。未来工作应聚焦于构建通用中间表示和可复用的转换模块。

Abstract: We present a case study in reformalization, a variant of autoformalization in which the input proof is not natural language but a formal development in a different proof assistant. Concretely, we report three reformalizations of the Jordan Curve Theorem: from Mizar to Lean, from HOL Light to Lean, and from HOL Light to Agda. We analyse the results and identify pipeline design choices that matter for practical reformalization tasks.

*Blair Hudson*

Main category: cs.AI

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 框架成功在2026年6月的快照中对288个模型进行了评估，实现了跨基准的可比性评分，有效捕捉了模型在不同金融业务场景中的真实能力差异，且具备良好的可复现性与治理支持能力。

Abstract: Public LLM leaderboards optimise for global average performance and do not capture the specific cognitive demands of financial-services work: a model that leads on MMLU-Pro may underperform on document-grounded compliance reasoning, and a coding leader may handle multi-turn customer interactions poorly. We present a meta-benchmarking framework that organises 452 publicly reported benchmarks into 41 O*NET Generalized Work Activities and aggregates those into 38 BIAN banking business domains spanning sales, operations, risk, and support work. A multiplicative weighting scheme (discrimination x coverage x recency), computed over a rolling model window, rewards benchmarks that still separate the best models, are widely reported, and remain in active use, suppressing saturated legacy tests automatically. These weights scale the K-factor in a pairwise Elo tournament, producing cross-benchmark-comparable work-activity scores without raw score normalisation; business-domain scores are weighted averages of the constituent work-activity Elos. We demonstrate the framework on a point-in-time public snapshot covering 288 models across 25 organisations as of June 2026, and describe the methodology, full taxonomy, design decisions, and limitations with the aim of making the approach reproducible for institutions facing similar selection and governance challenges.

### [180] [Path-level Hindsight Instructions for Semantic Exploration in Vision-Language Navigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01754)
*Sung June Kim,Sangpil Kim,Honglak Lee*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Phi-Nav is a unified on-policy framework for Vision-Language Navigation that uses hindsight reasoning to align language instructions with actual agent exploration. It operates in a three-stage cycle: oracle-guided exploration, hindsight instruction synthesis from visual observations, and imitation learning using the synthesized trajectory-instruction pairs. This approach closes the semantic supervision gap in on-policy methods, enabling effective training with fewer expert demonstrations.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: On-policy exploration in Vision-Language Navigation introduces semantic mismatches between executed actions and original language instructions, limiting the effectiveness of policy training. Existing methods struggle to provide meaningful supervision during exploration.

Method: Phi-Nav employs a three-stage dual-supervision cycle: (1) oracle-guided on-policy exploration with expert feedback, (2) a hindsight speaker generates path-level instructions based on collected visual data, and (3) a second imitation pass treats the synthesized trajectory-instruction pair as an expert demonstration.

Result: Phi-Nav achieves competitive performance on R2R-CE and RxR-CE benchmarks while requiring significantly fewer expert demonstrations than current baselines, demonstrating its efficiency and effectiveness in low-data settings.

Conclusion: Semantic exploration is essential for robust VLN agents. Phi-Nav effectively addresses the semantic mismatch problem in on-policy training by leveraging hindsight reasoning, making it a promising solution for training embodied agents with limited expert data.

Abstract: On-policy exploration is a crucial component for training robust Vision-Language Navigation agents, as it exposes the policy to a broader state distribution. However, such exploration inevitably leads to trajectories that deviate from expert demonstrations, resulting in a semantic mismatch between the executed visual stream and the original language instruction. In this work, we address this challenge by introducing Phi-Nav, a unified on-policy framework that leverages hindsight reasoning to align instructions with the agent's actual exploratory journey. Specifically, Phi-Nav operates through a three-stage dual-supervision cycle: 1) the agent performs oracle-guided on-policy exploration, sampling a trajectory while learning from expert action feedback, 2) a hindsight speaker synthesizes a path-level hindsight instruction grounded in the collected visual observations, and 3) the agent conducts a second imitation pass, treating the synthesized trajectory-instruction pair as an additional expert demonstration. Through this process, Phi-Nav bridges the critical semantic supervision gap inherent in on-policy methods, transforming semantically unlabeled movement into dense training signals. Evaluations on the R2R-CE and RxR-CE benchmarks show that Phi-Nav yields competitive performance while requiring only a fraction of the expert demonstrations used by current baselines. These results underscore the necessity of semantic exploration in VLN, positioning Phi-Nav as an effective solution for training embodied agents with limited data.

</details>


### [181] [Mastermind: Strategy-grounded Learning for Repository-Scale Vulnerability Reproduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01764)
*Mingzhe Du,Luu Anh Tuan,Tianyi Wu,Renyang Liu,Zhijiang Guo,Dong Huang,See-Kiong Ng*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文提出Mastermind框架，通过分离可迁移的策略学习与任务特定经验，提升代码库级漏洞复现的效率。其核心思想是将策略而非完整执行轨迹作为学习单元，利用训练好的规划器通过SFT和基于里程碑的GRPO优化策略，同时经验循环记录本地策略以指导后续尝试。该方法在CyberGym上验证，使用GPT-5.5作为固定执行器时，通过率高达84.5%，显著优于现有方法。相同规划器还能提升其他模型表现，证明高阶策略学习具有高效性和可迁移性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM代理在漏洞复现任务中常因选择错误策略而失败，尽管能正确执行步骤。现有方法难以有效学习和复用高层策略，导致性能受限。因此需要一种更高效、可迁移的策略学习机制。

Method: 提出Mastermind双层框架：上层为可训练的规划器，通过监督微调（SFT）和基于里程碑的GRPO学习通用漏洞复现策略；下层为经验循环，保存任务特定的策略记录以指导后续尝试。规划器独立于执行器训练，支持对多个固定执行器进行策略增强而不修改其行为。

Result: 在CyberGym上，使用GPT-5.5作为冻结执行器时，Mastermind达到84.5%的通过率，优于开书PoC上下文（60.0%）、Best-of-8采样（63.0%）和迭代改进（77.0%）。相同规划器使GPT-5.4 mini和GLM~5.1的通过率分别从45.0%和58.5%提升至60.0%和71.0%。

Conclusion: 学习高层策略是一种有效且可迁移的方法，能够显著提升代码库级软件工程代理的性能，尤其适用于复杂、多变的漏洞复现任务。

Abstract: Repository-level vulnerability reproduction is a demanding software engineering (SE) task: an agent must inspect a codebase, infer the input grammar that reaches a vulnerable path, construct a proof-of-conceptv(PoC), and verify that the crash disappears on the patched build. Recent LLM agents can often execute these steps when the approach is correct, yet they still fail by choosing the wrong strategy. This paper argues that strategy, rather than the full action trajectory, is the right learning unit for such SE agents: it is compact enough to optimize, concrete enough to guide execution, and stable enough to store and reuse across attempts. We present Mastermind, a dual-loop framework that separates transferable strategy learning from task-specific experience. A trainable planner learns reusable vulnerability-reproduction strategies through SFT and milestone-based GRPO, while an experience loop maintains task-local strategy records that guide subsequent attempts. The planner is trained independently of the executor, allowing strategy learning to improve multiple frozen executors without modifying their action-generation capability. We evaluate Mastermind on CyberGym using 260 training tasks and 200 held-out evaluation tasks. With GPT-5.5 as the frozen executor, Mastermind achieves an 84.5% pass rate, outperforming open-book PoC context (60.0%), Best-of-8 sampling (63.0%), and iterative improvement (77.0%). The same planner also improves GPT-5.4 mini and GLM~5.1 from 45.0% and 58.5% to 60.0% and 71.0%. These results demonstrate that learning high-level strategies is an effective and transferable mechanism for improving repository-scale SE agents.

</details>


### [182] [SimWorlds: A Multi-Agent System for Dynamic 3D Scene Creation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01766)
*Chunjiang Liu,Xiaoyuan Wang,Haoyu Chen,Yizhou Zhao,Ming-Hsuan Yang,László A. Jeni*

TL;DR: SimWorlds 是一个用于从文本生成动态可编辑 4D 场景的多智能体框架，结合了 Blender 的程序化知识、规划-编码-审查工作流、分层场景协议和运行时状态检查工具，以解决动态场景生成中的空间布局、物理模拟、时间序列和视觉一致性等挑战。研究还提出了 4DBuildBench 基准测试，用于评估生成场景的视觉保真度与物理一致性。实验表明，该方法在动态场景生成方面优于现有基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文本到 3D 场景生成系统主要关注静态输出，而动态 4D 场景（如液体流动、粒子发射、刚体下落、关节机构运动）具有重要应用价值，但面临联合协调多个物理引擎、时间序列、相机与光照等复杂挑战，且难以通过渲染视频验证运动正确性。因此需要一种能生成可编辑、物理一致的动态 4D 场景的新方法。

Result: SimWorlds 在生成动态 4D 场景方面显著优于现有基线方法，在视觉保真度和物理一致性上均表现更优，验证了其在复杂动态场景生成任务中的有效性。

Conclusion: SimWorlds 成功实现了从文本到可编辑、物理一致的动态 4D 场景的生成，为视频生成和具身 AI 提供了高质量的训练数据，并推动了动态文本到 3D 场景生成领域的发展。

Abstract: LLM agents are increasingly used to translate natural language into 3D scenes in a procedural way, but existing systems focus on static output. Dynamic 4D scenes from text alone, in which liquids flow, particles emit, rigid bodies cascade, and articulated mechanisms move, remain largely unexplored despite their value as editable content and as physics-grounded training data for video generation and embodied AI. Two challenges set the dynamic case apart from static text-to-scene work: an agent must jointly coordinate spatial layout, multiple physics solvers, temporal sequencing, camera, and lighting in a single coherent scene, and verifying motion correctness from rendered video is fundamentally harder than judging a single image. We present SimWorlds: a multi-agent framework that produces dynamic, editable 4D scenes from text, with Blender-specific procedural knowledge, a planner-coder-reviewer workflow driving a fixed ordered sequence of construction stages, a layered scene protocol enforced by a deterministic verifier, and a runtime-state inspection tool suite that catches mechanism failures the rendered image cannot reveal. We also introduce 4DBuildBench, a benchmark for assessing both visual fidelity and physical consistency of the procedural dynamic 3D scenes generated from text prompts. Experiments show that SimWorlds outperforms prior dynamic Blender generation baselines.

### [183] [Repair the Amplifier, Not the Symptom: Stable World-Model Correction for Agent Rollouts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01767)
*Xinyuan Song,Zekun Cai*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文针对长流程规划中因错误积累导致大规模规划图失败的问题，提出一种名为WM-SAR（世界模型子图放大修复）的新型纠错机制。与传统工程方法需扫描整个图并修复可疑局部区域不同，WM-SAR通过反向追踪误差放大路径，精准定位持续传播错误的关键节点与边，并仅将这些因果子图提交给LLM进行修复。实验表明，在有限上下文预算下，WM-SAR显著优于传统方法，能以更小的修复区域实现接近全图稳定，且提供更清晰、聚焦的修复目标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在长期、复杂的代理规划任务中，错误会出现在大规模规划图内部而非孤立预测中，而重新规划整个图既不高效也不可行。因此需要一种能够在不重载全局信息的前提下，精准识别并修复错误根源的机制。

Method: 提出WM-SAR方法：基于子图放大原理，反向追踪导致错误不断放大的节点与边，识别出因果性错误传播路径，并仅将该子图发送给LLM进行修复。

Result: 在多种图模拟和LLM修复实验中，WM-SAR在有限上下文预算下表现远超传统工程型正确器，能够用极小的修复区域实现近似全图稳定，且显著提升修复效率与质量。

Conclusion: WM-SAR是一种高效、精准的规划图纠错框架，解决了大规模持久工作流中错误修复的瓶颈问题，为构建鲁棒、可扩展的自主代理系统提供了关键技术支持。

Abstract: As agent planning moves from short tool chains toward persistent workflows with thousands or tens of thousands of steps, failures will occur inside large planning graphs rather than in isolated predictions. Replanning the entire graph after every mistake is neither computationally realistic nor desirable: full-graph replay consumes large context budgets, exposes the LLM to many irrelevant symptoms, and can degrade long-context retrieval. This paper studies the missing component in such systems: a world-model corrector that repairs the failed planning graph in place. We compare two families of correctors. The first is the common engineering approach: scan nodes and edges, choose a suspicious local region, and ask an LLM to repair it. We implement strong engineering LLM correctors and find that they can help, especially when given very large contexts. The second family is our approach, WM-SAR (World-Model Subgraph Amplification Repair): instead of scanning for visible symptoms, it works backward from subgraph amplification, identifies the nodes and edges that keep re-amplifying error, and sends only that causal subgraph to the LLM. Across graph simulations and LLM repair experiments, WM-SAR substantially outperforms engineering correctors under realistic token budgets, achieves near-whole-graph stabilization with a compact region, and gives the LLM a cleaner repair target.

</details>


### [184] [Verifiable Knowledge Expansion through Retrieval-Grounded Formal Concept Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01773)
*Yujin Yang,Heejung Lee*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于检索增强的小型语言模型（SLM）框架，结合形式概念分析（FCA）作为符号验证循环，用于知识扩展。该框架从种子属性出发，利用FCA生成隐含关系，并通过检索增强的SLM oracle验证每个隐含关系或返回反例。该方法支持实例判断、一致性检查和属性建议，使被接受的隐含关系、反例、矛盾和修正均具有可解释性。在罕见共济失调数据集上，10个种子属性的实验获得0.29-0.52的关系F1和0.22-0.30的闭包隐含关系F1；更大的种子集通常提升隐含关系的F1值。较低的隐含关系得分反映对推导关系的严格评估，一个遗漏或多余关系会影响多个隐含判断。消融实验表明，在固定对象-属性设置下进行实例判断可提升闭包隐含关系得分，但即使在候选对象和属性固定的情况下，正向实例对的识别仍具挑战性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有语言模型虽能从文本中提出本体结构，但其输出可能存在不支持或不一致的问题。因此需要一种机制来验证和修正这些结构，确保知识的准确性和一致性。

Method: 提出一种检索增强的SLM框架，结合形式概念分析（FCA）作为符号验证循环。从种子属性开始，利用FCA生成隐含关系，再由检索增强的SLM oracle进行验证或提供反例，支持实例判断、一致性检查与属性建议，实现可解释的知识扩展过程。

Result: 在罕见共济失调数据集上，10个种子属性的实验得到关系F1为0.29–0.52，闭包隐含关系F1为0.22–0.30；更大的种子集提升了评估的隐含关系数量并常改善其性能。消融实验显示，固定对象-属性设置下的实例判断有助于提升闭包隐含关系得分，但正向实例对识别依然困难。

Conclusion: 该框架有效结合了符号推理与语言模型的生成能力，通过可解释的验证机制提升了本体构建的可靠性。尽管存在识别正向实例对的挑战，整体方法在复杂领域知识扩展中展现出潜力。

Abstract: Ontology construction requires deciding which objects, attributes, and structural relations should be accepted as valid knowledge. Language models can propose such structures from text, but their outputs can still be unsupported or inconsistent. This paper proposes a retrieval-augmented small language model (SLM) framework that uses formal concept analysis (FCA) as a symbolic verification loop for knowledge expansion. Starting from seed attributes, FCA proposes implications over a growing formal context. A retrieval-grounded SLM oracle then validates each implication or returns a counterexample. The oracle also supports incidence judgments, consistency checks, and attribute proposals, making accepted implications, counterexamples, contradictions, and corrections inspectable. In a rare ataxia setting constructed from Orphadata resources, retrieval-grounded 10-seed runs obtain relation F1 of 0.29-0.52 and closure-based implication F1 of 0.22-0.30. Larger seed sets increase the number of evaluated implications and often improve implication F1. The lower implication scores reflect a stricter evaluation of derived implications, where one missed or extra relation can affect several implication judgments. Ablations show that incidence judgments in a fixed object-attribute setting can improve closure-based implication scores. However, identifying positive object-attribute pairs remains difficult even when the candidate objects and attributes are fixed.

Abstract: Diffusion Language Models (DLMs) have recently emerged as a promising alternative to autoregressive models. Unlike standard diffusion-based approaches, DLMs are not explicitly conditioned on a timestep, raising a natural question: do these models internally represent denoising progress, and how is such information used downstream? In this work, we show that DLMs do in fact encode a latent representation related to the diffusion timestep within their residual streams. We find that this signal can be reliably extracted using probes across layers, indicating that denoising progress is decodable from internal activations. We further demonstrate that steering the model along a low-dimensional subspace associated with the inferred timestep allows us to systematically modulate its notion of denoising progress, leading to predictable changes in model confidence and entropy. Finally, we analyse the geometry of the identified representation, showing that it exhibits structured and interpretable properties in activation space, and shedding light on how such a signal is processed by these models.

### [186] [Safety Testing LLM Agents at Scale: From Risk Discovery to Evidence-Grounded Verification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01793)
*Yunhao Feng,Ruixiao Lin,Ming Wen,Qinqin He,Yanming Guo,Yifan Ding,Yutao Wu,Jialuo Chen,Yunhao Chen,Xiaohu Du,Jianan Ma,Zixing Chen,Zhuoer Xu,Xingjun Ma,Xinhao Deng*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Vera 是一个端到端的自动化安全测试框架，针对不断演化的 LLM 代理系统中的非确定性安全风险，采用三阶段自强化流水线：文献驱动的风险探索、基于分类体系的组合生成安全案例、以及基于运行时观察的自适应执行与证据验证。该框架在四个生产级代理框架中揭示了高达 93.9% 的攻击成功率，释放了包含 1600 个可执行安全案例的 Vera-Bench，证明模块化可执行测试基础设施对大规模、持续演化代理系统的安全评估至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出三阶段自强化测试流程：(1) 文献驱动探索构建安全风险、攻击方法与工具环境的分类体系；(2) 多维组合生成包含具体目标、初始状态和可验证断言的可执行安全案例；(3) 在隔离沙箱中通过控制代理引导多轮交互，并基于环境状态和工具调用证据进行结果验证，而非依赖模型自我报告。

Result: 在 OpenClaw、Hermes、Codex、Claude Code 四个主流代理框架上测试，平均攻击成功率达 93.9%，暴露出显著的安全缺陷；发布 Vera-Bench，包含 1600 个可执行案例，覆盖 124 类风险和三种执行环境。

Conclusion: 模块化、可执行的安全测试基础设施是实现对快速演进的智能体系统进行严格、可持续安全评估的关键，有助于提升大规模代理系统的安全性与可信度。

Abstract: LLM agents increasingly perform autonomous actions through external tools, leading to complex and evolving safety risks. However, existing safety testing targets expert-designed safety violations, and the corresponding outcomes are evaluated by hard-coded rules, making them costly to extend as agents evolve. To this end, we present Vera, an end-to-end automated safety testing framework that instantiates software engineering testing principles for non-deterministic agents through a three-stage, self-reinforcing pipeline. First, a literature-driven exploration continuously discovers and structures emerging risks into taxonomies of safety risks, attack methods, and tool execution environments. Second, combinatorial composition across taxonomy dimensions produces executable safety cases, each specifying a concrete safety goal, a programmatically constructed initial state, and a deterministic verification predicate grounded in observable artifacts. Third, adaptive execution runs heterogeneous agents in isolated sandboxes where a control agent steers multi-turn interaction based on runtime observations, while evidence-grounded verifiers judge outcomes from environment state and tool-call evidence rather than model self-report. We evaluate Vera on four production agent frameworks (OpenClaw, Hermes, Codex, Claude Code), revealing substantial safety weaknesses, with average attack success rates reaching 93.9\% under multi-channel attacks; we also release Vera-Bench, comprising 1600 executable safety cases spanning 124 risk categories across three execution settings. These results indicate that modular, executable testing infrastructure is essential for rigorous and maintainable safety evaluation of rapidly evolving agentic systems at scale. The code is publicly available at https://github.com/Yunhao-Feng/Vera.

Method: 提出三阶段架构：1）使用训练免费的记忆-SAM模块实现精准舌体分割；2）利用微调的Qwen3-VL模型生成结构化舌诊结论；3）通过Qwen3-RAG模块结合外部证据生成临床决策支持。同时构建MedTCM多模态数据集并开发专用评估指标TDEU。

Result: MMIR-TCM在多个评估维度上均显著优于当前主流模型（如GPT-4o、Gemini 2.5 Flash），尤其在诊断准确性和临床实用性方面表现突出，验证了其在真实医疗场景中的潜力。

Conclusion: MMIR-TCM成功实现了对中医舌诊过程的智能化模拟，克服了现有技术在语义理解与数据规模方面的瓶颈，为多模态人工智能在中医临床中的深度应用提供了新范式。

Abstract: Traditional Chinese Medicine (TCM) diagnosis, particularly through tongue inspection, faces persistent challenges in subjectivity and reproducibility. The application of multimodal artificial intelligence to TCM clinical tasks, such as syndrome differentiation and prescription generation, is significantly hampered by the semantic gap between visual tongue features and textual reasoning, as well as the lack of large-scale, standardized datasets. To address these challenges, we introduce MMIR-TCM, a novel framework that emulates the diagnostic process of TCM experts by integrating multimodal large language model(MLLM) with memory-augmented segmentation and retrieval-augmented generation (RAG). Employing a three-stage architecture, MMIR-TCM integrates a training-free Memory-SAM module for robust tongue extraction, a fine-tuned Qwen3-VL model for structured tongue diagnosis generation, and a Qwen3-based RAG component for evidence-grounded clinical decision support generation. The framework was developed and validated using MedTCM, a new large-scale multimodal dataset that we introduce specifically for advanced TCM research. To properly evaluate our framework's clinical accuracy, which existing metrics fail to capture, we also developed TDEU, a domain-specific evaluation metric incorporating semantic understanding and diagnostic importance. Our comprehensive experiments demonstrate that MMIR-TCM significantly outperforms leading models, including GPT-4o and Gemini 2.5 Flash.

</details>

*Alex Brooker,Tim Hughes*

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly proposed for aviation business operations, from documentation and training generation to customer facing assistants. General purpose benchmarks do not measure whether a model reasons safely and correctly about aviation specific operational knowledge, and the high stakes, regulated nature of the domain makes that gap consequential. We present Pre-Flight, an open source benchmark of 300 multiple choice questions drawn from international standards and airport ground operations material, covering international airport ground operations, ICAO and US FAA regulations, aviation general knowledge and complex operational scenarios. Questions were authored and reviewed by practitioners with experience in air traffic management, ground operations and commercial flying. We evaluate a range of contemporary commercial and open weight models using the Inspect evaluation framework, scoring by accuracy under a standard multiple choice protocol, and we maintain the leaderboard on a rolling basis as new models are released. Against an informal expert reference of around 95%, obtained from a low sample quiz of aviation professionals at a conference, even the strongest model evaluated (released in 2026) reaches 82.7%, having improved only gradually from roughly 75% in early 2025. A substantial and persistent gap below expert level reliability therefore remains. We release the dataset, the evaluation harness and the results, and the benchmark is available within the community evaluations package distributed with inspect_evals. We study fault trees from the perspective of Halpern & Pearl's theory of actual causality. This allows us to use fault trees to answer the question "why has it gone wrong?", which is fundamental to failure diagnostics. We give a complete classification of each of the different notions of actual causality in terms of the fault tree's graph structure and logical structure, and show how minimal cut sets give rise to actual causes.

### [190] [CLAP: Closed-Loop Training, Evaluation, and Release Control for Domain Agent Post-training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01846)
*Fangfei Li,Chenyang Zhao,Long Wang,Feng Tian,Zhiyue Zheng,Lv Guo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: CLAP提出一种闭环方法，将业务数据转化为结构化样本与风险诊断记录，通过数据验证、归一化、奖励/KL诊断、离线门控和应用链回放，评估适配器是否适合目标应用链。在五个制造场景批次中，QLoRA风格的LoRA-SFT带来小幅提升，但仅3个批次改善，部分出现退化，GRPO暴露高KL风险；应用链回放表明RAG对事实提取至关重要，优化后的适配器虽提升质量但增加延迟。结果支持通过集成的数据-训练-评估-发布循环管理领域代理后训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 领域代理面临业务数据噪声、训练后收益不确定、离线与应用不匹配及适配器发布风险等问题，传统方法依赖训练完成或单一离线评分，难以有效评估适配器适用性。

Method: CLAP采用闭环框架，整合数据验证、目标/证据归一化、奖励与KL诊断、离线门控机制以及应用链回放，动态判断适配器是否适合目标应用链。

Result: 在五个制造场景批次中，QLoRA-style LoRA-SFT带来平均得分提升0.0098、通过率提升0.0240、证据准确率提升0.0280，幻觉和错误事实减少；但仅3个批次改善，部分退化，GRPO显示高KL风险；应用链回放证实RAG对事实提取必要性，优化适配器提升质量但增加延迟。

Conclusion: 应通过集成的数据-训练-评估-发布闭环来管理领域代理的后训练过程，而非依赖训练完成或单一离线指标。

Abstract: Domain agents often face noisy business data, uncertain post-training gains, offline/application mismatch, and adapter-release risk. This paper presents CLAP (Closed-Loop Agent Post-training), a closed-loop method that converts business data into structured SFT samples, decision-preference samples, holdout sets, risk diagnostics, and release-gate records. CLAP combines data validation, target/evidence normalization, reward/KL diagnosis, offline gates, and application-chain replay to decide whether an adapter is suitable for the target application chain. On five anonymized manufacturing-scenario batches, QLoRA-style LoRA-SFT yields modest average gains: overall score increases by 0.0098, pass rate by 0.0240, and evidence accuracy by 0.0280, while hallucination and wrong facts decrease. Application-chain replay further shows that RAG is necessary for factual extraction; under the same 3B backbone and 100 replay cases, an application-RAG-oriented LoRA-SFT adapter improves value, core fields, and answer-evidence doc/page matching over base+RAG, but increases latency. These results support managing domain-agent post-training through an integrated data-training-evaluation-release loop rather than relying on training completion or a single offline score.

### [191] [Safety Targeted Embedding Exploit via Refinement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01859)
*Joshua Adrian Cahyono*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了大型语言模型（LLMs）安全训练主要基于英语，导致在低资源语言和混合语言代码切换场景下安全机制泛化能力不足。为此，作者提出STEER方法，通过梯度引导攻击识别并翻译关键词汇以规避拒绝行为，实现高达93.0%的攻击成功率，且结果可迁移至GPT-4o-mini。研究证明当前安全对齐策略在多语言环境下存在显著缺陷，呼吁加强多语言覆盖与分布外检测机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型的安全训练主要集中于英语，缺乏对低资源语言和混合语言输入的有效覆盖，导致模型在非英语语境下可能错误地生成有害内容而无法有效拒绝，形成认知差距。

Method: 提出STEER（Safety Targeted Embedding Exploit via Refinement），一种基于梯度引导的攻击方法，通过识别影响模型拒绝行为的关键词，并将其迭代翻译为低资源语言，以削弱拒绝响应但保持有害意图。

Result: 在六个8B参数开源模型上，STEER在JailbreakBench上达到最高93.0%的攻击成功率，在AdvBench上达96.7%，优于随机代码切换和GCG方法；攻击样本可成功迁移至GPT-4o-mini，实现35.5%的成功率，表明该漏洞具有普遍性。

Conclusion: 当前以英语为主的安全对齐机制无法有效泛化到多语言环境，提升多语言安全性需在对齐阶段扩大语言覆盖范围，并引入对分布外输入的检测与拒答机制。

Abstract: Safety training for large language models (LLMs) is conducted predominantly in English, leaving uncertain how well safety mechanisms generalize to low-resource languages and mixed-language code-switching. We show that this creates an epistemic gap in which models confidently generate harmful responses for inputs that fall outside the distribution of their safety training. To study this phenomenon, we introduce STEER (Safety Targeted Embedding Exploit via Refinement), a gradient-guided attack that identifies words contributing most strongly to the model's refusal behavior and iteratively translates them into low-resource languages to suppress refusal while preserving harmful intent. Across six open-source 8B-parameter models, STEER achieves attack success rates of up to 93.0% on JailbreakBench and 96.7% on AdvBench, outperforming random code-switching and Greedy Coordinate Gradient (GCG). The resulting prompts also transfer to GPT-4o-mini, achieving a 35.5% attack success rate without requiring access to the target model, suggesting that the underlying weakness is not specific to a single architecture. These findings demonstrate that safety mechanisms aligned primarily on English cannot be assumed to generalize across multilingual inputs. We argue that improving multilingual safety requires broader coverage during alignment and mechanisms that explicitly detect and abstain on out-of-distribution inputs.

Traditional COD models rely on hand-designed architectures and multi-scale feature fusion, which are often guided by intuition rather than systematic search. This paper introduces CamoNAS, a frequency-aware multi-resolution Neural Architecture Search (NAS) framework for COD. CamoNAS automatically searches both cell-level operations and network-level downsampling paths, forming a hierarchical search space tailored to detect camouflaged objects. Additionally, it adopts an RGB frequency dual-stream architecture, where a learnable wavelet transform complements the RGB spatial stream. CamoNAS achieves state-of-the-art performance on four COD benchmarks (CAMO, COD10K, NC4K, CHAMELEON), highlighting the effectiveness of NAS for COD. Our code is available at https://github.com/rendaweiSIMIT/CamoNAS.

### [193] [SkillCoach: Self-Evolving Rubrics for Evaluating and Enhancing Agentic Skill-Use](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01874)

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SkillCoach 是一种自演化评分框架，用于评估和提升 LLM 代理在使用技能时的性能。它从实际运行中提取基于技能的过程评分标准，从四个维度（技能选择、遵循、组合和反思）评估轨迹，并将外部验证器作为独立的结果信号，以区分过程质量与偶然成功。演化后的评分标准还可用于筛选高质量训练轨迹，显著提升评估精度，揭示最终准确率无法发现的失败，并提供比仅依赖结果的过滤更强的监督信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 实验表明，演化后的评分标准显著提升了评估质量，揭示了最终准确率无法发现的失败，并提供了比仅依赖结果的过滤更强的监督信号，从而有效增强代理技能使用能力。

Conclusion: SkillCoach 通过自演化评分框架，实现了对代理技能使用的精细化评估与强化，克服了传统方法因依赖最终结果而导致的评估偏差，为构建更鲁棒的智能代理系统提供了有效支持。

Abstract: Skills are becoming a reusable operational layer for LLM agents, encoding SOPs, domain rules, tool workflows, scripts, and validation routines. In realistic skill repositories, overlapping skills make reliable skill-use difficult. Final verifier success is too coarse for both evaluation and training, since an agent may pass through trial and error while selecting distractor skills, skipping required steps, composing workflows incorrectly or omitting final checks. We introduce SkillCoach, a self-evolving rubric framework for evaluating and enhancing agentic skill-use. SkillCoach derives skill-grounded process rubrics from real rollouts and evaluates trajectories along four dimensions: skill selection, skill following, skill composition, and skill-grounded reflection. It keeps the external verifier as a separate outcome signal, allowing process quality to be distinguished from accidental task success. The evolved rubrics further serve as process supervision for selecting high-quality training trajectories. Experiments show that evolved rubrics substantially improve evaluation quality, expose failures hidden by final accuracy, and provide stronger supervision signals than outcome-only filtering for enhancing agentic skill-use.

### [194] [Spec-AUF: Accept-Until-Fail Training under Train-Inference Misalignment for Masked Block Drafters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01893)
*Tianjian Yang,Meng Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: AUF通过仅在草案生成器首次预测失败处保留交叉熵支持，实现对接受前缀的敏感监督，无需修改推理流程或引入辅助目标，在Qwen3-8B上将DFlash草案生成器的平均输出长度从2.40提升至2.61，且在所有基准上均有提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统全块交叉熵损失对每个位置进行监督，但推理中仅使用首个接受前缀，导致训练与推理不匹配；现有方法虽尝试重加权，但AUF提出基于教师强制学习的思路，使监督集中在实际被采纳的前缀部分。

Method: 提出AUF（Acceptance-aware Unfolding），仅在草案生成器首次预测失败的位置保留交叉熵支持，从而模拟前缀敏感的监督信号，无需额外目标或改变验证机制。

Result: 在六项基准测试中，AUF使DFlash草案生成器的平均输出长度τ从2.40提升至2.61，且每项任务均获增益；在Domino两分支头结构中，τ从2.56升至2.68。实验显示，仅衰减权重的基线虽提升块级准确率，但解码性能更差，且一旦采用AUF截断，标准指数位置衰减权重不再起效。

Conclusion: AUF是一种轻量、高效且可迁移的训练改进策略，通过聚焦于实际接受的前缀来优化草案生成器，显著提升自回归生成效率，同时保持原有推理架构不变。

Abstract: Speculative decoding accelerates autoregressive generation by drafting a block of tokens that the target model verifies left-to-right, committing only the longest accepted prefix. Block (DLM-style) drafters predict the whole block in parallel, which is fast but trained with a full-block cross-entropy that supervises every position against the gold continuation -- even though inference discards every token after the first rejection. Recent acceptance-aware objectives patch this by reweighting the full-block loss; we instead use teacher-forced learning as a motivation for how supervision should concentrate on the accepted prefix. A mask-only block drafter has no input-side channel for gold-prefix conditioning, so AUF approximates that prefix-sensitive supervision on the loss side by keeping the cross-entropy support only through the drafter's first predicted failure. AUF is a single, detached change to the CE support -- no auxiliary objective, no verifier rollouts, and no change to the inference pipeline or the exactness contract. Within fixed drafter backbones and serving settings on Qwen3-8B, AUF raises the DFlash drafter's average emitted length $τ$, averaged over six benchmarks, from 2.40 to 2.61, with a gain on every benchmark, and transfers to Domino's two-branch head (2.56 to 2.68). Two findings sharpen the picture: the decay-only baseline reaches higher token accuracy on the shared block mask yet decodes worse, and on DFlash, once AUF truncates the support, the standard exponential position-decay weighting becomes empirically inert.

### [195] [Rethinking Complexity Metrics for LLM-Integrated Applications: Beyond Source Code](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01903)
*Zihao Xu,Yuekang Li,Gelei Deng,Yi Liu,Zhenchang Xing*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: HECATE is the first tool to assess complexity in both prompt and code layers of LLM-integrated applications. It introduces Prompt-as-Specification, a formalism treating prompts as behavioral specifications, and derives 52 metrics from 25 complexity dimensions. After empirical validation using maintenance activity from 18 repositories, only 10 metrics remain significant, with 7 emphasizing structural breadth (e.g., distinct LLM call sites, memory attributes, templates). These prompt-layer metrics outperform traditional code-level metrics like Halstead and RFC, and remain predictive even when code complexity is controlled for, proving prompt complexity is an independent dimension. Validation on 6 additional repositories confirms their generalizability.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing complexity metrics focus only on code, ignoring the significant behavioral logic embedded in prompts of LLM-integrated applications. This gap limits accurate assessment of system maintainability and complexity.

Method: HECATE uses Prompt-as-Specification—a Hoare-logic-inspired formalism—to model prompts as behavioral specifications. It generates 52 candidate metrics across 25 complexity dimensions. Metrics are evaluated against maintenance activity from version history in 18 open-source repos, with statistical control for code size. Only metrics retaining significance after controlling for code size are retained.

Result: Ten metrics survive rigorous testing; seven are new and measure structural breadth rather than volume. These prompt-layer metrics significantly predict maintenance effort independently of code complexity. The top two metrics generalize well, validated on 20 components from six held-out repositories.

Conclusion: Prompt complexity is a distinct and critical dimension in LLM-integrated applications. HECATE’s structural breadth metrics offer superior predictive power over traditional code-centric measures and should be integrated into software complexity assessment practices.

Abstract: LLM-integrated applications blend natural language prompts with program code, and much of their runtime behavior originates in the prompt layer rather than in the code itself. Existing complexity metrics, however, operate solely at the code level and therefore overlook this behavioral logic entirely. We present HECATE, the first tool designed to assess complexity in both the prompt and code layers of such applications. Central to HECATE is Prompt-as-Specification, a Hoare-logic-inspired formalism that interprets every prompt as a specification of intended behavior. Grounded in 25 complexity dimensions identified across published taxonomies, the tool generates 52 candidate metrics. We assess each metric against 118 components collected from 18 open-source repositories, relying on maintenance activity derived from version history as an empirical proxy for complexity, and discard any metric that loses significance once code size is accounted for. Only ten metrics withstand this test. Seven belong to our newly introduced set; rather than measuring sheer volume, each tallies structurally distinct elements, such as LLM call sites, memory attributes, and prompt templates, an attribute we call structural breadth. Of the three surviving conventional metrics, RFC exhibits a similar breadth-oriented character, while Halstead N and V survive only as a residual effect of size; our top-performing metrics exceed all three. Crucially, the prompt-layer metrics retain significance even when the strongest code-level metric is added as a covariate, establishing prompt complexity as a dimension in its own right. A final validation on 20 components spanning six held-out repositories shows that the two best-performing metrics continue to predict maintenance effort, supporting their generalizability beyond the training set.

</details>


### [196] [ContextSniper: AntTrail's Token-Efficient Code Memory for Repository-Level Program Repair](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01916)
*Chiwang Luk,Matin Mohammad Najafi,Zhifeng Jia,Wei Yang,Xiuchang Li,Jinwei Zhu,Yang Ren,Lei Chen,Gao Cong*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ContextSniper 是一种针对代码修复任务的高效上下文管理机制，通过精确选择证据、混合检索信号排序、意图感知的上下文门过滤等技术，显著减少大语言模型在修复仓库级问题时的上下文开销。在 SWE-bench Lite 上的实验表明，它能降低 36.4% 到 51.5% 的总令牌消耗和成本，同时仅轻微影响提交成功率。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型代理在修复真实仓库问题时，因频繁读取整文件、广泛搜索及输出冗长日志，导致上下文预算浪费严重，有效信息被大量无关代码和日志淹没。因此需要一种更高效的上下文管理机制来提升资源利用效率。

Method: ContextSniper 作为 AntTrail 的代码记忆层，采用狙击式精准证据选取策略：通过候选代码与运行时证据的混合检索，结合多信号排序；利用意图感知的上下文门过滤冗长输出，并生成紧凑的证据包，同时保留提示外可恢复的源码上下文。

Result: 在 SWE-bench Lite 测试中，ContextSniper 对 OpenClaw 和 Claude Code 均显著降低令牌使用量（分别减少 51.5% 和 38.9%）与成本（分别减少 36.4% 和 27.3%），提交成功率略有下降（OpenClaw 从 26.0% 降至 24.0%，Claude Code 从 32.0% 降至 30.0%）。

Conclusion: ContextSniper 有效提升了大语言模型在仓库级程序修复中的上下文效率，实现了在极小性能损失下大幅降低计算成本的目标，其原型脚本已开源。

Abstract: Large language model agents can repair real repository issues, but they often spend large context budgets on whole-file reads, broad searches, and long terminal outputs where useful evidence is mixed with irrelevant code and logs. This paper presents ContextSniper, AntTrail's token-efficient code memory layer for repository-level program repair. As the coding specialization of AntTrail's broader agent memory engine, ContextSniper implements the Sniper feature for precision evidence selection: it retrieves candidate code and runtime evidence, ranks it with hybrid retrieval signals, filters long outputs through an intention-aware context gate, and returns compact evidence packets while preserving recoverable source context outside the prompt. We evaluate ContextSniper on SWE-bench Lite with OpenClaw and Claude Code, using 50 task runs per host-agent condition. ContextSniper reduces total token use by 51.5% and logged cost by 36.4% for OpenClaw, and reduces total token use by 38.9% and estimated cost by 27.3% for Claude Code. Submitted-resolution rates decrease slightly, from 26.0% to 24.0% for OpenClaw and from 32.0% to 30.0% for Claude Code. ContextSniper's pilot testing scripts are open-sourced at https://github.com/Calluking/ContextSniper

### [197] [ElephantAgent: Contextual State Continuity in Agentic Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01919)
*Jiankai Jin,Xiangzheng Zhang,Zhao Liu,Wenzhuo Xu,Dongdong Yang,Deyue Zhang,Quanchen Zou*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ElephantAgent 是一种保护智能体上下文状态连续性的协议，通过重新计算并验证上下文状态摘要来防御工具和记忆投毒攻击，利用可信硬件维护可线性化的授权状态转移日志，并提供历史可追溯性以实现事后审计与恢复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体系统依赖外部工具和持久记忆，但这些依赖引入了新的攻击面，如工具描述符和记忆被恶意篡改，导致代理行为被隐蔽偏移。当前缺乏对代理上下文状态的可验证连续性保障，因此需要一种机制来确保上下文状态的安全性和完整性。

Method: ElephantAgent 定义了安全关键的上下文状态范围（如工具状态和记忆），在每次处理查询前重新计算本地上下文状态的摘要，并与最新的授权摘要进行比对；利用复制的可信硬件维护一个线性化的授权状态转换日志，检测带外状态篡改；并通过历史可追溯性机制，支持条件性的事后审计和回滚至已知良好状态。

Result: 该方法有效抵御了上下文状态投毒攻击，增强了智能体在复杂环境下的安全性与可靠性，同时支持事后审计与恢复，提升了系统的可信赖程度。

Conclusion: ElephantAgent 为智能体系统提供了可验证的上下文状态连续性保障，解决了因外部依赖带来的安全漏洞问题，是构建可信智能体的重要一步。

Abstract: Agentic systems enhance their capabilities by invoking external tools and maintaining persistent memory. However, these external dependencies introduce novel attack surfaces. Recent tool and memory poisoning attacks show that maliciously crafted tool descriptors and poisoned memory can covertly bias agent behavior. These threats reflect a deeper issue: the lack of verifiable continuity in the agent's contextual state for planning and execution. We present ElephantAgent, a protocol that enforces Contextual State Continuity to defend against contextual state poisoning. Inspired by prior state-continuity mechanisms (e.g., Nimble), ElephantAgent extends this protection to the evolving contextual state of agentic systems. We define the contextual state as the bounded, security-critical subset of the agent's entire context (e.g., tool state and memory). Before processing each query, ElephantAgent recomputes the digest of the local contextual state and verifies it against the latest authorized digest. Using replicated trusted hardware, ElephantAgent maintains a linearizable ledger of authorized contextual state transitions and detects out-of-band state tampering. To handle in-band semantic abuse, ElephantAgent additionally provides Historical Traceability, enabling conditional post-hoc audit and recovery to a known-good prior state.

### [198] [A-TMA: Decoupling State-Aware Memory Failures in Long-Term Agent Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01935)
*Zitong Shi,Yixuan Tang,Anthony Kum Hoe Tung*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文研究了大语言模型代理中因状态协调失败导致的'幽灵记忆'问题，即旧事实、当前事实和过渡事实共存并混淆，误导回答模型。提出ATMA（状态感知叠加层）来解决此问题，通过保留过时与过渡记录、构建查询所需状态视图的证据包，并在问答中暴露当前、历史和过渡标签。同时提出LTP基准测试以测量幽灵记忆，并验证了Graphiti+ATMA在冲突准确率和时间F1上的显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有记忆系统无法有效区分当前、过去和过渡事实，导致幽灵记忆现象，影响问答准确性。需要从记忆维护、检索和答案解析三个层面优化记忆系统。

Method: 提出ATMA，一种对现有记忆系统的状态感知叠加层；保留过时与过渡记录；构建针对查询状态视图的证据包；在答案生成阶段显式暴露状态标签；设计LTP基准测试以评估幽灵记忆问题。

Result: 在LTP基准上，Graphiti+ATMA相比Graphiti提升冲突准确率0.240；在LoCoMo上，时间F1从0.0295提升至0.1705，表明显式状态管理可有效缓解隐藏于最终答案准确率中的记忆错误。

Conclusion: 记忆系统应从银行维护、检索和答案解析三个层次进行设计与评估；引入状态感知机制（如ATMA）能显著减少幽灵记忆带来的错误，提升长期记忆的可靠性。

Abstract: Long term memory lets LLM agents act as persistent assistants, but user facts change. A useful memory system must know what is true now, what used to be true, and what changed. We study \emph{ghost memory}, a state coordination failure in which old, current, and transition facts coexist in the memory bank, remain mixed during retrieval, and mislead the answer model. We argue that memory systems should be understood and optimized from three levels: bank maintenance, retrieval, and answer time resolution. We propose ATMA, a state aware overlay for existing memory systems. ATMA keeps superseded and transition records in the bank, builds evidence packets for the query's requested state view, and exposes current, historical, and transition labels to QA. We further call for decoupled evaluation of bank, retrieval, and answer level failures, since final QA accuracy can hide where ghost memory occurs. To make this failure measurable, we build LTP (LoCoMo Temporal Plus), a conflict heavy benchmark for ghost memory, and evaluate on LoCoMo for long conversation generalization. On LTP, Graphiti+ATMA improves conflict accuracy by 0.240 absolute over Graphiti. On LoCoMo, Graphiti+ATMA raises temporal F1 from 0.0295 to 0.1705. The gains are host dependent, but they indicate that explicit state roles can reduce memory failures hidden by final QA accuracy.

### [199] [Atomic Task Graph: A Unified Framework for Agentic Planning and Execution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01942)
*Yue Zhang,Sihan Chen,Ziwen Huang,Hanyun Cui,Kangye Ji,Zhi Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ATG是一种统一的控制框架，通过显式图结构暴露子任务间的依赖关系，支持中间结果复用。它在规划阶段递归分解任务生成可追溯的有向无环图（DAG），在执行阶段实现并行化以提升效率，并在失败时基于图演化历史定位错误并修复局部区域，从而保持已验证部分不变。实验表明，仅使用7B-8B规模的模型，在三个交互式基准上均显著优于强基线，在成功率和执行效率上表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于大模型的智能体在解决复杂多步任务时，性能提升主要依赖于扩大模型规模或特定任务微调，前者成本高，后者泛化性差；而现有的提示控制方法仍隐式处理输入输出依赖，难以有效复用中间结果。因此亟需一种无需训练、高效且可复用的控制机制。

Method: 提出原子任务图（ATG）框架，通过构建显式图结构表示任务依赖关系，在规划阶段递归分解任务形成可追踪的有向无环图（DAG），在执行阶段利用依赖关系实现并行执行，并在失败时基于图演化历史进行错误定位与局部修复。

Result: 在三个交互式基准测试中，使用7B-8B规模模型的ATG在成功率和执行效率上均显著优于现有强基线，证明其在不依赖大规模模型或微调的情况下具备卓越的通用性和鲁棒性。

Conclusion: ATG通过显式建模任务依赖与可追溯的图演化，实现了高效、可复用、可修复的多步任务求解，为轻量级大模型智能体提供了一种通用且高效的控制范式。

Abstract: LLM-based agents have shown strong potential for solving complex multi-step tasks, yet existing performance improvements often rely on either scaling to larger backbone models or task-specific fine-tuning. The former incurs substantial computational costs, while the latter typically generalizes poorly across different tasks. Although prompt-based control is training-free and broadly applicable, existing methods still leave input-output dependencies between subtasks implicit in textual trajectories, making verified intermediate results difficult to reuse. To address these limitations, we propose Atomic Task Graph (ATG), a unified control framework for planning and execution. Specifically, ATG maintains an explicit graph to expose dependencies and support reuse. During planning, it recursively decomposes a high-level task into subtasks, forming a sequence of directed acyclic graphs (DAGs) whose evolution can be traced. During execution, the dependencies exposed by ATG allow independent branches to be executed in parallel, thereby improving execution efficiency. When failures are detected, ATG leverages the graph evolution history to localize the error source and repair only the affected region, preserving validated regions unchanged. Experiments show that ATG consistently outperforms strong baselines in success rate and execution efficiency across three interactive benchmarks using only 7B-8B backbones.

### [200] [OntoLearner: A Modular Python Library for Ontology Learning with Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01977)
*Hamed Babaei Giglou,Jennifer D'Souza,Andrei Aioanei,Nandana Mihindukulasooriya,Sören Auer*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前本体学习（OL）研究分散，缺乏统一的评估基础设施和本体访问机制，导致进展缓慢且关键问题未被解决。

Method: 提出 OntoLearner 框架，集成本体访问、LLM 驱动的学习管道和标准化基准；构建跨领域、多任务的数据集与评估体系；开展大规模实证研究，对比多种模型在不同任务和领域中的表现。

Result: 发现本体学习失败模式随本体复杂性增加而加剧，核心瓶颈是模型知识表示与本体组织结构之间的结构性不匹配，而非模型能力本身。

Conclusion: 通过 OntoLearner 提供的跨领域、多任务基准评测，有效本体学习已成为可能，其成功依赖于对结构适配性的重视。

Abstract: Ontology learning (OL) aims to automatically construct structured knowledge models from text, yet progress remains fragmented across methods, domains, and evaluation practices. Despite decades of research, OL lacks a shared infrastructure for systematic evaluation and ontology access. This absence has hindered progress and fragmented research, leaving the central challenges of OL largely unaddressed. We introduce OntoLearner, a modular, cross-domain, and first-of-its-kind framework that unifies ontology access, large language model (LLM)-driven learning pipelines, and standardized benchmarking. OntoLearner releases 180 machine-readable ontologies spanning 22 domains and provides pipeline-ready datasets with train/dev/test splits for three core OL tasks: term typing, taxonomy discovery, and non-taxonomic relation extraction. Using this infrastructure, we conduct a large-scale empirical study of OL, evaluating 22 retrieval models and 12 LLMs across domains and tasks. The results converge on a finding that reframes the central challenge of OL: failure modes scale with ontological complexity rather than model size or architectural sophistication. The primary bottleneck is not model capability, but a structural mismatch between how models encode knowledge and how ontologies organize it. These findings establish that effective OL is reachable through the cross-domain, multi-task benchmarking enabled by OntoLearner. OntoLearner is open-source (MIT license) at https://github.com/sciknoworg/OntoLearner/.

### [201] [Multimodal Knowledge Edit-Scoped Generalization for Online Recursive MLLM Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01978)
*Siyuan Li,Youyuan Zhang,Ruitong Liu,Junxi Wang,Jing Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ScopeEdit提出了一种范围感知的在线多模态知识编辑方法，通过分解更新为模态局部吸收分支和证据门控共享泛化分支，实现对每次编辑传播边界的精确控制。该方法在保持低计算开销的同时，显著提升了跨模态迁移与非相关输入隔离之间的平衡，且在多种模型架构和真实场景下均表现出优异的可靠性、稳定性和效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有在线多模态知识编辑方法虽注重编辑可靠性和长期稳定性，但缺乏对每次编辑语义边界的控制。研究发现，仅在实例层面成功并不保证跨模态泛化，也难以避免对无关输入的干扰，且编辑相关响应集中在深层语义层，因此需要重新定义编辑目标为控制编辑的传播范围。

Method: ScopeEdit将每次更新分解为两个分支：模态局部吸收分支用于稳定吸收编辑内容，证据门控共享泛化分支仅在视觉与文本证据充分对齐时才允许跨模态传播。两个分支在正交低秩空间中执行分离写入，并通过Sherman-Morrison递推维护分支级预条件器，从而实现恒定的每编辑开销。

Result: 在多个基准测试、长时序编辑流、不同MLLM骨干网络、真实世界VLKEB场景及复杂视觉-语言架构上，ScopeEdit均显著提升了在范围内跨模态传递与范围外局部性之间的权衡，同时保持了编辑的可靠性、稳定性和在线效率。

Conclusion: ScopeEdit通过引入编辑作用范围的显式控制，实现了更精准、高效、稳定的在线多模态知识编辑，为构建可信赖的持续学习多模态系统提供了新范式。

Abstract: Online multimodal knowledge editing requires injecting a continual stream of visual-textual corrections into multimodal large language models (MLLMs) with bounded overhead and minimal disruption to unrelated behaviors. Existing editors mainly emphasize edit reliability and long-horizon stability, but rarely control the semantic boundary of each edit. Our pilot analyses of post-edit behaviors and internal neuronal activities reveal a scope gap behind reliable edits: instance-level success neither guarantees transfer to valid cross-modal variants nor prevents leakage to unrelated inputs, while edit-related cross-modal responses concentrate in deeper semantic layers. Therefore, we formulate Edit-Scoped Generalization, reframing online MLLM editing from merely correcting an instance to controlling the propagation boundary of each edit. To this end, we propose ScopeEdit, a scope-aware online editor that decomposes each update into a modality-local absorption branch and an evidence-gated shared generalization branch. The local branch supports stable edit absorption, whereas the shared branch enables cross-modal propagation only when visual and textual evidence are sufficiently aligned. Both branches perform scope-separated write geometries in orthogonal low-rank spaces and maintain branch-wise preconditioners via Sherman--Morrison recursions, yielding constant per-edit overhead. Extensive experiments across diverse benchmarks, long-horizon edit streams, MLLM backbones, real-world VLKEB scenarios, and complex vision-language architectures show that ScopeEdit consistently improves the trade-off between in-scope cross-modal transfer and out-of-scope locality, while preserving edit reliability, stability and online efficiency. Our code is available at https://github.com/lab-klc/ScopeEdit.

### [202] [Episodic-to-Semantic Consolidation Without Identity Drift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01988)
*Xue Qin,Simin Luan,Cong Yang,Zhijun Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种新型知识巩固机制，将记忆巩固视为从情景记忆到语义知识层的确定性函数变换，而非对智能体身份的修改。该方法通过保持代理身份哈希不变，实现知识更新而不改变其可认证身份，支持审计追踪与可信更新。实验验证了其在减少无效规划尝试方面的显著效果（平均降低79.82%），且身份在多次巩固后仍保持字节级一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长期运行的自适应智能体面临知识固化与信息完整性之间的结构性矛盾；传统方法通过微调模型或修改提示来实现巩固，但在受监管的自主部署中会破坏其已认证的身份绑定，导致合规风险。

Method: 将记忆巩固建模为一个确定性函数 f: M^ep → M^sem，将情景记忆映射至独立可寻址的语义知识层；身份哈希不读取语义层，从而保证身份不变；设计可审计的聚合算法，输出带有置信度和事件溯源的数据库记录。

Result: 合成实验表明，该方法在10次种子测试中平均减少79.82%的无效规划尝试（95% BCa CI [78.02%, 81.49%]），且身份在所有巩固过程中保持字节相等；成功实现知识累积与身份不变性的统一。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了一种适用于受控环境中自主智能体的知识更新范式，使智能体能够持续学习并积累可查询的事实知识，同时维持其在整个生命周期内的可认证身份一致性，以服务型智能体为实证案例。

Abstract: Long-running adaptive intelligent agents face a structural tension between knowledge consolidation and information integrity. Memory consolidation is conventionally treated as an agent-changing operation: a model is fine-tuned, a prompt rewritten, a policy distilled, or a reflection appended to the context that governs future behaviour. In regulated autonomic deployment this is a liability because the agent operates under commitments and audit contracts that bind to a specific, cryptographically certified identity. We propose to treat consolidation not as a mutation of the planner or the identity manifest, but as a deterministic function f: M^ep -> M^sem over episodic memory whose output is a separately addressable semantic knowledge layer; the identity hash does not read M^sem, so consolidation updates knowledge without changing the agent's certified identity. We give a formal account of the agent representation, prove identity invariance through a structural lemma on the manifest's hash-input set, specify a deterministic aggregation algorithm whose outputs are auditable database rows with explicit confidence and supporting-event provenance, and validate the construction with synthetic experiments demonstrating per-field correctness, byte-equal identity across consolidation passes, and a mean 79.82% reduction in unproductive planner attempts (95% BCa CI [78.02%, 81.49%] across 10 seeds) against a calibrated Bayesian-shrunk baseline. The construction is a knowledge-update discipline for autonomic agents in which lessons accumulate as queryable facts while the agent's certified identity remains byte-equal across its operational lifetime, with an embodied service agent as the running case study.

</details>

This digest presents a traceable BESS fault-diagnosis assistant that uses retrieval-augmented multi-agent reasoning to connect operational data, domain knowledge, visual evidence, and report generation. Reliability is improved through BESS-specific task routing, schema-constrained natural-language database access, hybrid text-image retrieval, and evidence-based answer synthesis. ### [204] [InduceKV: Fixed-Footprint Continual Adaptation of Multimodal LLMs via Inducing KV Memories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02010)
*Qianyu Chen,Ziteng Feng,Canran Xiao,Runxuan Tang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出InduceKV，一种基于检索的固定内存预算持续适应方法，通过存储训练前缀为可直接使用的记忆条目（包含冻结检索键和紧凑的层间键值对），在不更新主干模型的前提下实现任务特定更新的外部化。该方法通过双层选择构建紧凑诱导集，在保持当前任务似然、锚点保留和冻结检索空间覆盖性之间取得平衡，显著优于PEFT、MoE、重放和提示检索基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在有限部署资源下，多模态大模型持续学习面临参数重复更新或回放缓存增长导致的适应状态累积问题，需要在不改变主干模型且内存预算固定的条件下实现高效持续适应。

Method: InduceKV采用检索机制，将每个选定的训练前缀作为注意力就绪的记忆条目存储，包括冻结的检索键和紧凑的层间键值（KV）数据；通过轻量级校准进行检索，并利用双层选择策略优化记忆条目的选取，以平衡任务似然、锚点保留与检索空间覆盖性。

Result: 在任务增量指令微调、持续视觉问答、领域增量适应及终身多模态指令微调等场景中，InduceKV在相同内存预算下均显著优于PEFT、MoE、重放和提示检索基线；并通过匹配主干模型、阶段1 CoIN、计算量匹配和可扩展性分析验证了性能提升并非由更强主干模型、单纯重放或无限候选池引起。

Conclusion: InduceKV实现了固定内存预算下的高效持续适应，无需修改主干模型，通过外部化任务特定更新和智能记忆选择，有效缓解了适应状态累积问题，具备良好的泛化性和可扩展性。

Abstract: Multimodal large language models must adapt to evolving tasks and domains, yet continual improvement under bounded deployment footprint remains difficult because repeated parameter updates or growing replay stores can accumulate adaptation state over time. We study fixed-footprint continual adaptation: the deployed adaptation state is kept under a fixed memory budget, while the backbone model is left unchanged and task-specific updates are externalized. We propose InduceKV, a retrieval-based method that stores each selected training prefix as an attention-ready memory entry, consisting of a frozen retrieval key and compact layerwise key--value (KV) payloads that can be appended to the model's self-attention cache. Under a strict memory budget, InduceKV constructs a compact inducing set through bilevel selection: a lightweight calibration is fit for retrieval, while the selected memory balances current-task likelihood, anchor-based retention, and coverage in the frozen retrieval space. Across task-incremental instruction tuning, continual VQA, domain-incremental adaptation, and lifelong multimodal instruction tuning, InduceKV consistently improves over PEFT, MoE, replay, and prompt-retrieval baselines under matched memory budgets. We further report backbone-matched, stage-1 CoIN, compute-matched, and scalability diagnostics, showing that the gains are not due to a stronger backbone, replay alone, or an unbounded candidate pool.

### [205] [Hidden Forgetting in Continual Multimodal Learning: When Accuracy Survives but Grounding Fails](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02020)
*Qianyu Chen,Canran Xiao,Runxuan Tang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了多模态大语言模型在持续学习过程中忽视的“隐性证据使用遗忘”问题，即模型虽保持答案准确率，却悄然改变依赖的视觉、文本、OCR、图表等证据来源。为此提出无需重放的依赖约束持续学习框架RCL，通过对比反事实通道干预估计师生模型的证据依赖分布，并联合优化任务学习、预测保留与依赖保留，无额外推理开销。在CoIN、COAST、MCITlib及多模态流数据上，RCL显著优于现有方法，减少模态依赖漂移、主导证据突变和隐性遗忘率，表明鲁棒的持续多模态学习需保留正确答案背后的证据路径，而不仅是答案本身。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准持续学习评估仅关注旧任务答案是否正确，忽略了多模态模型在回答过程中对视觉、文本、OCR、图表等证据的依赖关系是否稳定。然而，即使答案正确，若模型悄悄转向不相关或低质量的证据源，其可解释性和可靠性将受损。因此需要更深入地考察多模态模型在持续学习中的证据使用稳定性。

Method: 提出RCL框架：冻结前一检查点作为行为参考；通过反事实通道干预估计教师与学生模型的证据依赖分布；联合优化任务学习、预测一致性与证据依赖一致性，实现无需重放且无推理开销的持续学习。

Result: 在CoIN、COAST、MCITlib及一个敏感证据的多模态流数据集上，RCL在最终性能和遗忘控制方面均优于回放式、PEFT、路由和记忆辅助基线方法，显著降低模态依赖漂移、主导证据切换频率和隐性遗忘率。

Conclusion: 真正的鲁棒持续多模态学习不仅要求答案正确，还需保持其背后证据路径的稳定性。RCL通过约束证据依赖关系，有效缓解了隐性证据使用遗忘问题，为未来多模态系统提供了更可靠的学习范式。

Abstract: Multimodal large language models must continually adapt to evolving tasks and domains, yet standard continual learning metrics mainly measure whether old answers remain correct, leaving the stability of multimodal grounding largely unexamined. We study this overlooked failure mode and ask whether a continually adapted MLLM can preserve not only what it answers, but also how it uses visual, textual, OCR, chart, and document evidence. We identify \emph{hidden evidence-use forgetting}, where answer accuracy is retained while the model silently shifts toward different or less grounded evidence channels, and propose \textsc{RCL}, a replay-free reliance-constrained continual learning framework. \textsc{RCL} freezes the previous checkpoint as a behavioral reference, estimates teacher and student evidence-reliance profiles through counterfactual channel interventions, and jointly optimizes task learning, prediction preservation, and reliance preservation without adding inference-time cost. Across CoIN, COAST, MCITlib, and an evidence-sensitive multimodal stream, \textsc{RCL} consistently improves final performance and reduces forgetting over replay-free, PEFT, routing, and memory-assisted baselines, while substantially lowering modality reliance drift, dominant evidence flips, and hidden forgetting rates. These results suggest that robust continual multimodal learning requires preserving the evidence path behind correct answers, not merely the answers themselves.

### [206] [PACE: A Proxy for Agentic Capability Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02032)
*Yueqi Song,Lintang Sutawika,Jiarui Liu,Lindia Tjuatja,Jiayi Geng,Yunze Xiao,Daniel Lee,Aditya Bharat Soni,Vincent Lo,Xiang Yue,Graham Neubig*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文提出PACE框架，通过从非代理型基准中选择一组原子实例构建代理基准，以低成本、高效率地预测大型代理型基准（如SWE-Bench和GAIA）上的模型表现。实验表明，PACE-Bench在14个模型、4个代理基准上实现低于4%的平均绝对误差、超过0.80的斯皮尔曼相关系数和约85%的模型排名准确率，成本仅为原评估的1%以下。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代理型大模型评估成本高昂、耗时长，而单个能力评估（如推理、代码生成）快速且廉价。因此需要一种方法，通过少量高效评估来准确预测模型在复杂代理任务中的表现，从而支持模型开发与选型过程中的快速迭代。

Method: 提出PACE框架，结合目标相关局部选择与全局信息性全局选择策略，从多个非代理型基准中筛选最具预测力的原子实例，利用回归模型将这些实例得分映射到代理型基准得分，形成紧凑的代理基准（PACE-Bench）。

Result: PACE-Bench在跨14个模型、4个代理型基准、19个非代理型基准的实验中表现出优异性能：LOOCV下平均绝对误差低于4%，斯皮尔曼相关系数高于0.80，模型排名准确率达约85%，同时评估成本不足原评估的1%。进一步分析揭示了各代理型基准所独有的关键技能需求。

Conclusion: PACE框架能够以极低的成本可靠预测大模型在复杂代理任务中的表现，显著降低评估开销，适用于模型开发、选择与路由等实际场景，为高效评估提供有效解决方案。

Abstract: Evaluating LLM agents on benchmarks like SWE-Bench and GAIA can be expensive, time-consuming, and requires complex infrastructure. A single evaluation can cost thousands of dollars and take days to complete. In contrast, non-agentic LLM benchmarks that test individual capabilities (e.g., reasoning, code generation) are fast and cheap to run. In this paper, we investigate whether performance on expensive agentic benchmarks can be accurately predicted by the performance on a small, carefully selected subset of atomic evaluation instances. We introduce PACE, a framework that constructs proxy benchmarks by selecting instances from existing non-agentic evaluations whose aggregate scores most reliably predict model performances on agentic benchmarks. Given a pool of candidate instances spanning atomic capabilities, PACE fits a regression that maps a model's scores on a compact subset of source instances to its score on the target agentic benchmark. The subset itself is curated by combining two complementary instance-selection strategies, target-relevance local selection and globally informative global selection. We apply PACE to the 4 target agentic benchmarks in this paper, which yields PACE-Bench, the concrete proxy benchmark that we evaluate in the paper. Experiments across 14 models, 4 agentic benchmarks, and 19 non-agentic benchmarks show that PACE-Bench predicts agentic scores with leave-one-out cross-validation (LOOCV) mean absolute error (MAE) under 4%, Spearman correlation above 0.80, and pairwise model-ranking accuracy around 85%, all at much less than 1% of the full agentic evaluation cost. We further analyze the selected proxy instances, revealing which skills each agentic benchmark uniquely demands. PACE enables practitioners to obtain reliable estimates of agentic performance during model development, selection, and routing, without the overhead of full agent evaluation.

### [207] [Algebraic Model Counting for Global Analysis of Optimal Decision Trees](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02069)
*Hiroki Arimura*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为代数决策树计数（ADTC）的框架，用于对最优和近似最优决策树进行全局分析。该方法将优化、计数和采样等任务统一为在半环上的求和-乘积计算，并通过动态规划实现时间复杂度为 $O^*(n^{O(Δ)})$，其中 $n$ 为特征数，$Δ$ 为最大深度。引入模型行为张量以高效处理多指标约束，支持准确率、大小、公平性等多目标权衡分析。软件工具 emtrees 在真实数据集上验证了其在敏感领域中基于证据的模型选择能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在可解释人工智能中，确保模型可靠性需要对假设空间进行全局评估，但传统方法难以高效处理决策树的复杂结构与多目标权衡问题。

Method: 基于代数模型计数（AMC）思想，将决策树分析任务形式化为半环上的求和-乘积计算；采用动态规划算法降低时间复杂度；引入模型行为张量与张量半环卷积，以高效聚合多指标信息。

Result: ADTC实现了对决策树假设空间的全面分析，能够高效生成包含准确性、规模、公平性等多维度权衡的模型轮廓；emtrees工具在真实数据集上验证了其在敏感场景下的实用性，支持证据驱动的模型选择。

Conclusion: ADTC提供了一个形式化且高效的框架，用于全局评估决策树模型，显著提升了可解释人工智能中模型选择的科学性与可靠性。

Abstract: Ensuring model reliability in Explainable AI requires a global assessment of the hypothesis space. We propose a formal framework for the exhaustive analysis of optimal and near-optimal decision trees, called Algebraic Decision Tree Counting (ADTC). Inspired by Algebraic Model Counting (AMC) in knowledge representation, ADTC reformulates diverse analytical tasks, such as optimization, counting, and sampling, into a unified sum-of-products computation over a semiring $R$. While the hypothesis space of decision trees is doubly exponential with respect to the maximum depth $Δ$, our dynamic programming algorithm achieves $O^*(n^{O(Δ)})$ time complexity in the number of features $n$, where $O^*$ suppresses polynomial factors. To handle complex constraints consisting of multiple tree metrics, we introduce model behavior tensors that aggregate semiring values via convolution products over a tensor semiring. This algebraic approach efficiently constructs a model profile that captures the global landscape and trade-offs between criteria such as accuracy, size, and fairness. We demonstrate the utility of our software, emtrees, on real-world datasets, illustrating how ADTC facilitates evidence-based model selection in sensitive domains.

### [208] [Evidence-State Rewards for Long-Context Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02073)

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Maven 是一种基于强化学习的长上下文推理框架，通过可编辑的证据记忆机制，对中间动作的状态转移进行奖励，包括添加、链接和删除证据的动作。该方法在 Llama 和 Qwen 模型上优于传统仅奖励最终答案或静态证据提取的方法，在 LongBench v2、LongReason 和 RULER 基准测试中表现出更充分的证据集和更低的干扰项保留率，证明了状态感知的证据导航优于一次性证据提取。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: Maven 引入可编辑的证据记忆，定义基于答案的证据状态价值函数，并为不同类型的动作（添加、链接、删除）设计特定奖励：添加动作依据边际收益和事后贡献，链接动作依据证据协同效应，删除动作依据移除误导性证据后答案支持度的提升。这些奖励被分配给对应的动作片段，并用于 GRPO 训练。

Result: 在 LongBench v2、LongReason 和 RULER 数据集上，Maven 在多个模型（Llama、Qwen）上均超越了基于结果奖励和证据识别的基线方法，生成了更完整且更少干扰项的证据集，显著提升了推理性能。

Conclusion: 长上下文推理的强化学习应聚焦于状态感知的证据导航，而非一次性的证据提取，这能有效提升模型对长文本中分散信息的利用能力。

Abstract: Long-context reasoning requires models to locate, revise, and synthesize evidence distributed across lengthy inputs. Existing long-context RL methods usually reward final answers or static evidence extraction, offering little feedback on how intermediate actions change the model's evidence state. We propose Maven, a reinforcement learning framework with an editable evidence memory. Maven defines an answer-conditioned evidence-state value and rewards action-level state transitions: add actions are credited by marginal gain and hindsight contribution, link actions by evidence synergy, and drop actions by improved answer support after removing misleading evidence. These rewards are assigned to the corresponding action spans in GRPO. Across Llama and Qwen models on LongBench v2, LongReason, and RULER, Maven outperforms outcome-only RL and evidence-identification baselines, producing more sufficient evidence sets and lower distractor retention. Our results show that long-context RL benefits from optimizing stateful evidence navigation rather than one-shot evidence extraction.

### [209] [SUNTA: Hierarchical Video Prediction with Surprise-based Chunking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02087)
*Tomoshi Iiyama,Masahiro Suzuki,Yutaka Matsuo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SUNTA提出了一种基于预测误差（惊喜度）的分层时间抽象方法，通过解耦训练和利用内部不一致性作为顶层惊喜度指标，解决了传统分层状态空间模型在长时序预测中的边界对齐问题。实验表明，SUNTA在2D和3D视频预测任务中显著优于基线方法，可在250个时间步内保持准确预测，而基线方法在前10步内即出现性能下降。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有分层状态空间模型依赖固定长度或基于相似性的分块方式，难以对齐数据内在的时间结构；而基于预测误差的分块虽更合理，但面临训练过程中层次坍塌及开环预测时缺乏惊喜信号的问题。

Method: 提出SUNTA方法，采用解耦训练策略以保留惊喜信号，并引入内部不一致性作为顶层惊喜度指标，在想象的滚动预测中动态确定分块边界。
