Conclusion: 基于预测误差驱动的分块机制能更有效地捕捉长期依赖关系，SUNTA通过创新的训练策略与惊喜度度量设计，实现了对长时序序列的稳健建模，为复杂动态系统的长期预测提供了新范式。

Abstract: Hierarchical state-space models (HSSMs) offer a promising approach to long-horizon prediction by segmenting sequences into temporal chunks. However, their performance hinges on how chunk boundaries are determined. While prior HSSMs typically rely on fixed-length chunking or similarity-based boundary detection, these methods often misalign with the intrinsic temporal structure of the data. We argue that chunking should instead be driven by prediction errors, which more directly indicate when longer-range context becomes necessary. Nevertheless, integrating surprise-based chunking into HSSMs introduces critical challenges, including hierarchical collapse during end-to-end training and the absence of surprise signals during open-loop prediction. To address these issues, we propose Surprise-based Nested Temporal Abstraction (SUNTA), a method that employs a decoupled training strategy to preserve surprise signals and uses internal inconsistency as a top-down surprise metric to determine chunk boundaries within imagined rollouts. Experiments on video prediction tasks in 2D and 3D environments demonstrate that SUNTA outperforms baselines, uniquely maintaining accurate predictions over 250 timesteps, whereas all baselines degrade within the first 10 timesteps.

### [210] [ContextNest: Verifiable Context Governance for Autonomous AI Agent](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02116)
*Misha Sulpovar,Benn R. Konsynski,Qaish Kanchwala,Gabe Goodhart*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ContextNext 是一个开放规范和参考实现，旨在为人工智能可消费的知识库提供上下文治理，解决传统检索管道在出处、版本身份、完整性、可追溯性及时间点重建方面的不足。它不替代 RAG，而是作为其底层治理层，确保检索前的知识项经过审批、验证且可追溯。通过结合带元数据的 Markdown 文档、确定性选择器、SHA-256 哈希链版本历史、图级检查点、MCP 数据源支持和审计追踪，实现对知识使用过程的完全可复现与可审计。实验表明，在过时版本攻击场景中，该方法在答案质量与输入令牌成本上均优于 BM25；在检索确定性测试中，其确定性选择器表现稳定（Jaccard=1.0），远超密集向量+HNSW 的非确定性表现（平均 Jaccard 0.611）。项目已开源核心引擎、CLI 和 MCP 服务器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前自主 AI 代理依赖外部知识库，但现有检索系统缺乏对知识来源的可信保障，如出处、版本、完整性与可追溯性，导致潜在风险。需引入一种机制来确保知识在被使用前具备可验证的治理属性。

Method: 提出 ContextNext 规范，融合类型化 Markdown 文档、元数据、确定性集合选择器、contextnest:// URI 引用、SHA-256 哈希链版本历史、图级检查点、Model Context Protocol (MCP) 支持的实时数据源以及审计日志，构建可治理、可追溯、可重建的知识存储体系。

Result: 在两个控制实验中，ContextNext 在应对过时版本攻击时，以约三分之一的输入令牌成本实现更高答案质量（97% 对比 90–93%）；在 1,060 篇文档的检索确定性测试中，其确定性选择器保持 1.0 的 Jaccard 相似度，而 dense+HNSW 方法在 80% 查询中出现非确定性，最差仅 0.210。结果表明上下文治理能有效解决仅靠检索质量无法覆盖的系统性失败模式。

Conclusion: ContextNext 提供了面向 AI 知识使用的上下文治理框架，填补了传统 RAG 中缺失的可信性保障环节，实现了知识使用的可验证、可审计与可复现，是迈向安全可控 AI 代理的关键一步。

Abstract: Autonomous AI agents increasingly depend on external knowledge stores, yet most retrieval pipelines provide relevance without durable guarantees of provenance, version identity, integrity, traceability, or point-in-time reconstruction. We formalize this as context governance and present ContextNext, an open specification and reference implementation for governed AI-consumable knowledge vaults. ContextNext does not replace Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG); it supplies the governance layer beneath retrieval, determining which artifacts are approved, current, attributable, and integrity-verified before retrieval systems operate over them.
  The specification combines typed Markdown documents with metadata, deterministic set-algebraic selectors, contextnest:// URI references, SHA-256 hash-chained version histories, graph-level checkpoints, source nodes for live data through the Model Context Protocol (MCP), and audit traces of agent context consumption. These mechanisms let organizations reconstruct which knowledge versions informed an agent output and whether those versions were AI-eligible when consumed.
  We report first empirical results from two controlled experiments. In a stale-version attack isolating the governance-versus-retrieval failure mode, governed selection strictly Pareto-dominates BM25 sparse retrieval, with higher answer-quality pass rate (97% versus 93-90%) at about one-third the input-token cost. In a retrieval-determinism experiment over a 1,060-document corpus, deterministic selectors and BM25 return stable document sets across repeated identical queries (Jaccard 1.0), while a dense+HNSW baseline is non-deterministic on 80% of queries (mean Jaccard 0.611, worst case 0.210). These results suggest that context governance addresses failure modes retrieval quality alone is not designed to resolve. We release a core engine, CLI, and MCP server under open licenses.

</details>


### [211] [Enhancing Fitness Intelligence through Domain-Specific LLM Post-Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02118)
*Xingtao Zhao,Tian Yang,Han Jiang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出FitOne，一种基于Qwen3基础模型的8B和32B参数规模的健身领域专用大语言模型，通过持续预训练、监督微调和强化学习三阶段后训练流程，结合高质量知识工程数据集，显著提升健身教练任务中的专业性与可靠性。在ACSM-EP和NSCA-CSCS等专业健身认证考试中，FitOne-8B/32B相比基线模型分别提升最高达10.09%/9.29%和12.73%/7.01%，同时保持强通用能力。消融实验证明各训练阶段均必要，验证了该方法在增强领域专长与保留通用能力之间的平衡效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有通用大语言模型在科学健身教练（SFC）应用中因缺乏领域知识而表现不佳，难以满足复杂场景需求；同时，人工健身教练成本高、可及性差，亟需低成本、高可靠的智能化解决方案。因此，需要构建具备强领域专业知识的大语言模型以推动普惠化健身服务。

Method: 基于Qwen3基础模型，设计三阶段后训练流程：持续预训练（利用大规模健身领域语料）、监督微调（基于高质量标注数据）、强化学习（优化指令遵循与推理能力），并结合严格知识工程构建高质量数据集。

Result: FitOne-8B/32B在ACSM-EP和NSCA-CSCS认证考试中分别实现最高10.09%/9.29%和12.73%/7.01%的性能提升，优于Qwen3基线模型；同时在知识推理与指令遵循等通用能力上保持竞争力；消融实验表明三阶段训练流程缺一不可，有效平衡了领域专长与通用能力。

Conclusion: FitOne成功实现了大语言模型在科学健身领域的专业化与可靠性提升，为构建可信赖的领域专用LLM提供了有效范式，推动智能健身服务向更广泛人群普及，并为未来垂直领域大模型研发提供重要参考。

Abstract: Scientific Fitness Coaching (SFC) is typically delivered by human professionals, making it costly and inaccessible to many. While recent advances in Large Language Models (LLMs) show considerable promise for more inclusive fitness coaching, directly deploying prevailing general-purpose LLMs in SFC reveals critical limitations. These models often lack sufficient domain-specific knowledge integration, leading to weak performance on complex SFC scenarios. In this paper, we introduce FitOne, a series of fitness LLMs (with 8B and 32B parameters) designed to improve reliability and domain specialization for SFC applications. Built upon the Qwen3 foundation models, FitOne is developed through a three-stage post-training pipeline consisting of continual pre-training, supervised fine-tuning, and reinforcement learning, using large-scale, high-quality datasets derived from rigorous knowledge engineering. We conduct comprehensive evaluations of FitOne on professional fitness certification exams, including ACSM-EP and NSCA-CSCS, as well as general capabilities such as knowledge reasoning and instruction following. Experimental results show that, while retaining strong general capabilities, FitOne-8B/32B achieves average improvements of up to 10.09%/9.29% and 12.73%/7.01% on the ACSM-EP and NSCA-CSCS exams, respectively, compared with the Qwen3 base models. Furthermore, in-depth ablation studies confirm the necessity of each training stage, highlighting the pipeline's effectiveness in balancing domain expertise enhancement with general ability retention. We believe this research advances LLM systems toward more reliable fitness intelligence and will inspire future research on developing domain-specific LLMs.

### [212] [Coding-agents can replicate scientific machine learning papers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02134)
*Atharva Hans,Ilias Bilionis*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Paper-replication is a workflow that turns scientific machine learning claims into verifiable targets with recorded evidence, implemented as a coding-agent skill. It ensures replication by reconstructing methods, running experiments, linking outputs to provenance, and validating results against paper claims. Evaluated across 12 runs on 4 papers, all workspaces passed completion with full target coverage, though variations in execution details (e.g., target division, fidelity, time, intermediate steps) were observed. Completion depends on evidence and validation, not agent output.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing coding agents struggle to reliably replicate scientific ML claims from paper materials alone, as prompts do not ensure progress tracking or evidence validation. There is a need for a systematic, auditable replication process that ensures claims are verified through reproducible computational experiments.

Method: Introduce Paper-replication: a structured workflow where each paper claim becomes a target. The coding agent records targets, reconstructs the paper's method, executes experiments, links outputs to provenance and comparisons, documents evidence in a replication report, and passes validation checks before completion.

Result: All 12 runs across 4 papers successfully completed, with 158 targets fully matched to report coverage. Variability was observed in target decomposition, numerical fidelity, replication time, number of intermediate executions replaced, and evidence acceptance rules. Completion is now dependent on validated evidence rather than final agent message.

Conclusion: Paper-replication establishes a robust, traceable framework for replicating scientific ML claims. It shifts validation from subjective agent output to objective, evidence-based completion, improving reliability and transparency in computational reproducibility.

Abstract: Scientific machine learning papers typically make computational claims, e.g., that the relative mean square error is less than 5% or that the 95% predictive credible interval covers the test data. A coding agent can be prompted to replicate those claims from paper materials alone, but the prompt does not by itself reliably preserve progress or check whether generated evidence supports the paper's claims. We introduce Paper-replication, a workflow that makes each selected paper claim a target with recorded evidence, and implement it as a coding-agent skill. The workflow makes the agent record those targets, reconstruct the paper's method, run computational experiments, link generated outputs to provenance and comparisons with the paper's claims, record where matched evidence appears in the replication report, and pass validation checks before completion. We evaluate Paper-replication on twelve independent runs across four scientific machine learning papers. All twelve workspaces pass the completion gate, and all 158 recorded targets are matched with report coverage. Even in this completed workspace state, repeated runs differ in how papers are divided into targets, in numerical fidelity to the source papers, in elapsed replication time, in the number of intermediate executions replaced before final evidence is accepted, and in the rules used to accept evidence. Paper-replication makes completion depend on workspace evidence and validation checks rather than on the agent's final message.

Result: 在SRDD基准上，UA-ChatDev在完整性、可执行性、一致性及整体质量方面均优于现有框架；消融实验与通信分析验证了不确定性感知交互对代码执行可靠性的提升作用。

Abstract: Software development is a complex task that demands cooperation among agents with diverse roles. Large language models (LLMs) have enabled autonomous multi-agent software development frameworks that leverage role-based collaboration to automate requirements analysis, coding, testing, and refinement. However, existing approaches typically assume that intermediate agent outputs are equally reliable, leaving them vulnerable to hallucination propagation, where incorrect decisions generated in early development phases are transferred to downstream agents and negatively impact final software quality. To address this challenge, we propose UA-ChatDev, an uncertainty-aware multi-agent software development framework that integrates uncertainty quantification into agent interactions. It introduces a lightweight uncertainty estimation mechanism based on token-level log probabilities to assess the confidence of agent responses and employs phase-aware threshold calibration to selectively trigger retrieval-based verification when uncertainty exceeds acceptable levels. Extensive experiments on the SRDD benchmark demonstrate that UA-ChatDev consistently outperforms existing single-agent and multi-agent software development frameworks across completeness, executability, consistency, and overall quality metrics. Further ablation studies and communication analyses verify that uncertainty-aware interactions enhance code execution reliability.

### [214] [Criticality-Based Guard Rail Validation for AI Agent Decisions in Autonomous Telecom Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02210)
*Ravi Kant Sharma*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出Guard Rail Validation (GRV)框架，旨在为电信网络中自主决策的AI/ML代理提供标准化的运行时验证机制，以防止错误决策导致网络故障。该框架通过多维度评估（如动作范围、服务关键性、可逆性等）确定决策的严重性等级，并据此应用不同级别的验证策略（如日志记录、边界检查、独立代理验证或多方共识）。同时支持跨代理冲突检测与优先级解决，并提供符合监管要求的运行时合规日志。在O-RAN架构下进行了部署与威胁覆盖评估，验证了其对已知AI/ML攻击的有效防御能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前电信网络向完全自治（级别4-5）演进，但缺乏标准化的运行时机制来拦截和验证AI/ML代理的推理输出，存在因错误决策引发网络异常的风险。亟需一种可标准化、可扩展的验证框架保障自主决策的安全性与合规性。

Result: GRV框架能有效拦截高风险决策，显著降低误操作风险；在模拟攻击场景下展现出对多种已知AI/ML攻击的良好威胁覆盖能力；支持EU AI Act等法规的合规要求，具备良好的可扩展性和部署可行性。

Conclusion: GRV框架为电信网络中的高级别自主决策提供了可靠、可标准化的运行时安全屏障，是实现安全可信自主网络的关键技术支撑。

Abstract: The evolution toward fully autonomous telecommunications networks (Autonomous Network Levels 4-5) requires AI/ML agents to make real-time network decisions without human intervention. However, no standardized runtime mechanism exists to intercept and validate individual inference outputs before they trigger live network state changes, creating risks of erroneous autonomous decisions. This paper proposes the Guard Rail Validation (GRV) framework, a standardizable runtime architecture for intercepting and validating AI-driven decisions before execution. The framework evaluates decisions across multiple weighted dimensions -- including action scope, action type, service criticality, agent autonomy level, reversibility, and temporal behavioural patterns -- to determine a criticality level. Based on this level, graduated validation mechanisms are applied: execute-with-logging, bounds checking, independent agent validation, or multi-agent consensus. The framework additionally provides cross-agent conflict detection with criticality-weighted priority resolution and runtime conformance logging for regulatory compliance (e.g., EU AI Act Article 14). We present the architecture, algorithmic procedures, O-RAN deployment model, and evaluate threat coverage against known AI/ML attacks in telecommunications.

Abstract: Mental health disorders affect nearly one billion people globally, yet 75% of individuals in low- and middle-income countries receive no treatment due to workforce shortages, cost barriers, and stigma. Current AI-powered wellness solutions predominantly rely on single-mode conversational interfaces that suffer high abandonment rates and fail to provide measurable, immediate relief calibrated to users' dynamic emotional states. This paper presents Copewell, a novel multi-agent swarm system designed to expand access to mental wellness support through human-centered AI principles. ### [216] [DRIFTLENS: Measuring Memory-Induced Reasoning Drift in Personalized Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02374)
*Xi Fang,Weijie Xu,Yingqiang Ge,Yuhui Xu,Stephanie Eckman,Chandan K. Reddy*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了个性化记忆对大型语言模型推理轨迹的影响，提出无需真实答案的DRIFTLENS框架来量化推理变化。结果显示，用户属性记忆会导致显著的推理漂移，即使最终回答仍流畅且合理。尽管基于GRPO和DPO的后训练方法能减少漂移，但效果因模型和奖励机制而异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究个性化记忆是否改变语言模型在开放性问题上的推理过程，尤其是当没有唯一正确答案时，以理解个性化带来的潜在影响。

Method: 引入DRIFTLENS框架，将每个推理步骤映射到价值类别，并比较无记忆与注入用户属性记忆下的推理轨迹差异；使用四种大模型和十类用户属性进行实验验证。

Result: 用户属性记忆引发中等至较大的推理漂移，高于模型自身的语用噪声基线；基于GRPO和DPO的后训练方法可减轻漂移，但效果不一致，且对下游能力、帮助性和指令遵循有模型依赖影响。

Conclusion: 记忆引起的推理漂移是可测量的，且仅部分可缓解，表明这是个性化语言模型的一个重要缺陷。

Abstract: Personalization changes what a model says to a user; we show that it can also change the reasoning trajectory used to justify the response. Modern LLMs personalize interactions by storing user attributes, preferences, and prior context, then injecting this information into future prompts. We study whether such memory reshapes reasoning on open-ended questions where no single ground-truth answer exists. To quantify this effect, we introduce DRIFTLENS, a ground-truth-free framework that maps each expressed reasoning step to a value category and measures divergence between a question's no-memory trajectory and its trajectory under injected user-attribute memory. We first validate that DRIFTLENS distinguishes content-free pragmatic noise from substantive reasoning changes. Across four LLMs and 10 user-attribute categories, including age, occupation, and disability, user-attribute memory induces medium-to-large reasoning drift above each model's pragmatic-noise floor, even when final answers remain fluent, on-topic, and plausible. We then evaluate GRPO- and DPO-based post-training methods for reducing drift. Both reduce drift, but neither uniformly dominates; effects on downstream capability, helpfulness, and instruction following are model-and reward-dependent. These results suggest that memory-induced reasoning drift is a measurable and only partly mitigated failure mode of personalized language models.

### [217] [Steerability via constraints: a substrate for scalable oversight of coding agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02389)
*Thomas Winninger*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出通过借鉴管理大型人类工程团队的方法（如访问控制、网络策略、严格的编码规范）来实现对代码生成代理的有效监管，相比近期复杂的代理架构，该方法在成本（token消耗）上更优。实验表明，在约束性基础设施与轻量级工具（约200行的CLI文档工具）共同作用下，检测后门的召回率从54.5%提升至90.9%，且两者贡献独立。研究以Python为例，因其默认保障最少，效果最显著，但原则可推广至Rust等语言。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前代码生成代理虽能力强，但缺乏约束会带来安全风险、降低代码库可扩展性，并使人工审查成本急剧上升。现有方法中，依赖复杂代理框架的方案代价高昂，亟需更高效、低成本的监督机制。

Method: 采用与管理人类团队相同的工程实践：实施访问控制、网络策略和由工具强制执行的严格编码规范，构建一个从头到尾的受控系统；引入轻量级工具（如~200-LoC的`docs` CLI）辅助审查，实现可扩展的人工监督。

Result: 在控制实验中，使用约束性底层环境与轻量工具后，检测11个植入后门的Python代码库的召回率从54.5%提升至90.9%，且底层约束与工具支持分别贡献独立提升效果。

Conclusion: 将传统工程管理方法迁移至代码生成代理是可行且高效的策略，能显著提升安全性与可维护性，同时降低监督成本，适用于多种编程语言，尤其在弱保障语言中效果更佳。

Abstract: Coding agents are capable; human oversight is the bottleneck. Unconstrained agents introduce security risks, erode codebase scalability, and make human review increasingly costly. We argue that the same methods used for decades to manage large human engineering teams: access control, network policies, strict coding conventions enforced by tooling; transfer directly to coding agents, and are cheaper (in token) than recent agentic scaffolding. We sketch a start-to-end system on this principle, and report a controlled experiment in scalable oversight: a small reviewer (Gemma 4 e4b) inspects a Python codebase containing 11 inserted backdoors. Recall rises from 54.5% (unconstrained, no tools) to 90.9% (constrained substrate plus a ~200-LoC `docs` CLI), with substrate and tools contributing independently. We choose Python deliberately: substrate-level oversight gains are largest where the language gives the fewest guarantees by default; the principles extend to languages like Rust.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法提取多维行为子空间计算成本高，难以应用于生成长推理轨迹的模型，亟需更高效、可扩展的替代方案以支持安全与可解释性需求。

Method: 采用探测引导的递归特征机器（RFM）算法，通过高效计算实现对多维拒绝子空间的快速定位，并结合探针初始化提升准确性。

Result: 在Qwen 3（推理模型）和Qwen 2.5（非推理模型）上均实现了秒级子空间识别，且在消融任务中表现优于其他方法，验证了其高效性与有效性。

Conclusion: RFM为大规模语言模型中的子空间提取提供了一种低成本、可扩展的替代方案，具有广泛应用前景，未来需进一步探索不同方法发现的子空间间关系。

Abstract: Steering and monitoring activations in Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly used for both safety and interpretability. Early work assumed behaviours are encoded along single linear directions, but recent findings suggest complex behaviours, such as the refusal to answer harmful queries, live in multi-dimensional subspaces. However, existing methods for extracting these subspaces are computationally expensive, which becomes prohibitive on reasoning models who produce long reasoning traces. By adapting the Recursive Feature Machine (RFM) algorithm -- which can be computed efficiently -- with a probe-informed initialization, we are able to identify the multi-dimensional refusal subspace in seconds, on reasoning (Qwen 3) and non-reasoning (Qwen 2.5) models. While RFM allows for faster subspace identification, it also showed better performances on the ablation task than its alternatives. More work is planned to better understand the relations between subspaces found by different methods. If confirmed, RFM could be a cheap and scalable complement to existing subspace-extraction methods in LLMs.

</details>


### [219] [G-RRM: Guiding Symbolic Solvers with Recurrent Reasoning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02491)
*Timo Bertram,Sidhant Bhavnani,Richard Freinschlag,Erich Kobler,Andreas Mayr,Günter Klambauer*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为G-RRM的神经符号方法，将符号等变的递归推理模型（SE-RRM）与符号约束求解器结合，以提升大规模问题的外推能力。实验表明，当问题具有庞大的组合搜索空间且求解器能动态修正分支选择时，神经引导可显著提高搜索效率，实现冲突次数归零和显著的运行时间加速；而若求解器无法重写分支提示，则无法获得明显收益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有神经方法在处理大规模约束满足问题时外推性差，而传统符号求解器虽准确但效率受限。为结合两者优势，需设计一种能有效引导符号求解器、并适应不完美提示的神经符号框架。

Method: 提出G-RRM方法，利用SE-RRM生成解提议作为神经引导信号，输入至背向追踪或基于SAT的求解器（如Glucose 4.1、CaDiCaL 3.0.0），通过动态调整分支策略来增强搜索效率。

Result: 在9×9数独上，回溯法加速33.3倍，Glucose 4.1加速1.70倍（中位数，p<0.001）；在25×25完美提示网格上仍保持1.17倍加速；而CaDiCaL因无法重写提示，仅得1.02倍加速（非显著），甚至平均出现0.90倍减速。

Conclusion: 神经引导能否带来实际加速取决于两个条件：问题必须具有大组合搜索空间，且求解器必须具备动态覆盖分支决策的能力。该研究明确了神经符号引导在实践中有效的边界条件。

Abstract: In this work, we focus on SE-RRMs, a symbol-equivariant instantiation of RRMs that exhibits improved extrapolation to larger problem sizes. We propose a neuro-symbolic approach, ``Guiding with Recurrent Reasoning Models'' (G-RRM), which integrates SE-RRMs with symbolic solvers for constraint satisfaction problems. SE-RRMs act as neural solvers that generate full solution proposals and guide classical symbolic solvers, such as backtracking or SAT-based methods like Glucose 4.1 and CaDiCaL 3.0.0, that produce globally correct solutions. Centrally, we investigate when neural guidance with G-RRM improves the search efficiency of symbolic solvers. %
Our experiments show that the efficacy of G-RRM depends on two conditions: first, the problem instances must have an expansive combinatorial search space to expose potential gains, and second, the solver architecture must be capable of dynamically overwriting its branching choices to recover when neural hints are imperfect. When these conditions hold, guidance drives median conflict counts to zero and yields significant wall-clock speedups: on $9\times9$ Sudoku, where the SE-RRM correctly solves $91.1\%$ of instances, backtracking accelerates by $33.3\times$ and Glucose 4.1 by $1.70\times$ (median, $p<0.001$), with Glucose 4.1 retaining a $1.17\times$ speedup on perfect-hint $25\times25$ grids. In contrast, CaDiCaL 3.0.0, whose runtime is overhead-dominated and which always respects the injected branching hints rather than overwriting them, shows no significant speedup (median $1.02\times$, n.s.) and even a small significant mean slowdown ($0.90\times$) on $9\times9$. These results delineate the regimes in which neural guidance translates into practical speedups.

</details>


### [220] [ReContext: Recursive Evidence Replay as LLM Harness for Long-Context Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02509)
*Yanjun Zhao,Ruizhong Qiu,Tianxin Wei,Yuanchen Bei,Zhining Liu,Lingjie Chen,Ismini Lourentzou,Hanghang Tong,Jingrui He*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: RECONTEXT是一种无需训练的推理方法，通过利用模型内部的相关性信号构建查询相关的证据池，并在生成最终答案前进行递归重放，从而提升长上下文推理中对相关信息的利用效率。该方法不依赖外部记忆或上下文修剪，基于关联记忆理论，将上下文视为记忆存储，问题作为检索线索，注意力机制视为线索-痕迹关联，而重放则对应痕迹重新激活。实验表明，在8个长上下文数据集上，该方法显著提升了Qwen3-4B、Qwen3-8B和Llama3-8B等模型的证据利用率，平均排名表现最佳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型虽具备较长的上下文窗口，但在处理长文本时仍难以有效利用已有信息，存在上下文访问与实际使用之间的差距。如何在不改变模型结构或训练的前提下提升长文本中的证据利用能力，成为关键挑战。

Method: 提出Recursive Evidence Replay（RECONTEXT）方法：利用模型内部相关性信号动态构建与查询相关的证据池；通过递归选择和重放这些证据，在保留原始完整上下文的基础上增强关键信息的可及性；整个过程无需训练、外部记忆或上下文剪枝。

Result: 在8个长上下文数据集（最大128K上下文长度）上，RECONTEXT显著提升多个主流模型（Qwen3-4B、Qwen3-8B、Llama3-8B）的证据利用效果，所有模型在各项指标上均达到最优平均排名。

Conclusion: RECONTEXT为长上下文推理提供了一种高效、通用且无需训练的解决方案，其核心思想是通过内部信号驱动的证据重放机制，增强模型对冗长上下文中关键信息的提取与利用能力，具有良好的泛化性和理论基础。

Abstract: Understanding and reasoning over long contexts has become a key requirement for deploying large language models (LLMs) in realistic applications. Although recent LLMs support increasingly long context windows, they often fail to use relevant evidence that is already present in the input, revealing a gap between context access and effective context utilization. In this work, we propose Recursive Evidence Replay as LLM Harness for Long-Context Reasoning (RECONTEXT), a training-free inference method for improving long-context reasoning. RECONTEXT uses model-internal relevance signals to construct a query-conditioned evidence pool and replays it before final generation while preserving the full original context. This recursive selection process separates evidence organization from answer generation without training, external memory, or context pruning. We also provide a theoretical analysis based on associative memory, which characterizes the context as a memory store, the question as a retrieval cue, attention as cue-trace association, and replay as trace reactivation. Experiments on eight long-context datasets with 128K context length show that RECONTEXT consistently improves evidence utilization across Qwen3-4B, Qwen3-8B, and Llama3-8B, achieving the best average rank on all three backbones. Code is available at https://github.com/Yanjun-Zhao/ReContext.

</details>

### [221] [Multilayer Q-Matrix-Embedded Neural Network for Cognitive Diagnosis (M-QCDNet): Structure-Aware Deep Learning Architecture for Psychometric Interpretability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01278)
*Yiyao Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: M-QCDNet 是一种多层嵌入 Q 矩阵的神经网络，用于认知诊断，结合了认知诊断模型（CDMs）的结构可解释性与深度学习神经网络的灵活性。该模型利用 Q 矩阵作为结构先验，确保潜在掌握状态与认知理论一致，并通过带有 L2 惩罚的损失函数，使未对齐技能受到惩罚，从而平衡预测性能与结构一致性。研究还提出了基于可解释性的评估指标，量化预测技能激活与题目层面技能的一致性。该方法有助于早期发现学习困难并支持基于掌握情况的干预，推动心理测量透明性与神经网络灵活性的融合，实现可解释、公平且可操作的认知诊断 AI。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有认知诊断模型在处理复杂数据时缺乏灵活性，而纯神经网络模型又缺乏可解释性。因此需要一种既能保持认知理论一致性，又能具备深度学习优势的模型，以提升诊断的准确性与实用性。

Method: 提出 M-QCDNet 模型，将 Q 矩阵作为结构先验嵌入神经网络，设计包含 L2 惩罚的损失函数以约束非预期技能激活，并构建基于对齐的可解释性评估指标。

Result: M-QCDNet 在保持高预测性能的同时显著提升了模型的可解释性，其预测的技能激活与实际题目技能高度对齐，能有效识别学生知识掌握情况，支持精准教学干预。

Conclusion: M-QCDNet 成功融合了认知诊断模型的理论可解释性与神经网络的建模灵活性，为可解释、公平且实用的认知诊断 AI 提供了新范式。

Abstract: The research proposes a multilayer Q-matrix-embedded neural network for cognitive diagnosis (M-QCDNet), which integrates the structural interpretability of cognitive diagnostic models (CDMs) with the deep learning neural network (NN). M-QCDNet structures the item-skill relationship using the Q-matrix as a structural prior, ensuring latent mastery profiles remain interpretable and consistent with cognitive theory, followed by the proposed loss function with an L2 penalty to penalize skills not aligned with the Q-matrix and to balance predictive performance and structural alignment. Corresponding evaluation matrices, the interpretable alignment-based metrics that quantify the degree to which predicted skill activations correspond to item-level skills, were further developed. M-QCDNet offers practical benefits for classroom practice, enabling early detection of learning difficulties and supporting mastery-based interventions. By embedding diagnostic validity into model design, M-QCDNet bridges psychometric transparency and neural flexibility, advancing interpretable, fair, and actionable AI for cognitive diagnostics.

### [222] [I\textsuperscript{2}RiMA: Spectral Riemannian Representation with Temporal Attention for Mental Stress Detection based on EEG Signals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01279)
*Cheng He,Kunyu Peng,Shangen Han,Jinming Ma,Jinhong Ding,Likun Xia*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出一种新型的Intra-Inter Riemannian Manifold Attention Network（\method{}）用于跨被试脑电（EEG）压力检测，通过在频域构建空间协方差矩阵并映射到对称正定（SPD）切空间，保留通道几何与频率特异性特征；引入频率聚类聚合以提取关键频段、减少冗余；结合局部时序动态与全局时间上下文的注意力机制，显著提升跨被试压力识别性能。在三个数据集上优于5个先进基线方法，最高达82.78%平衡准确率，参数量仅1.60M，计算开销31.95M FLOPs。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在跨被试EEG压力检测中面临两大挑战：一是传统Riemannian方法多在时域建模空间协方差，忽略对高级认知状态判别至关重要的神经振荡特性；二是标准时间分块方式破坏了片段间的时序连贯性。因此亟需一种能同时捕捉频率特异性和时序结构的高效模型。

Method: \\method{}通过在每个频率点独立构建空间协方差矩阵，并将其映射至对称正定（SPD）切空间，保留通道间几何关系及频率敏感特征；采用数据驱动的频率聚类聚合策略，筛选出与脑电节律一致的信息频段，降低冗余；设计内-间片段注意力模块，自适应融合局部频谱动态与全局时间上下文，实现对跨被试EEG信号的精准建模。

Result: 在三个公开数据集上的实验表明，\\method{}在跨被试压力检测任务中持续优于五种主流基线方法，最高达到82.78%的平衡准确率，同时保持极低的模型复杂度（仅1.60M参数，31.95M FLOPs），验证了其有效性与高效性。

Conclusion: \\method{}成功解决了跨被试EEG压力检测中的频率特异性与时序连贯性难题，通过融合频域协方差建模、频率聚类与注意力机制，在保证高精度的同时具备良好的泛化能力与计算效率，为未来脑电信号解码提供了新范式。

Abstract: Cross-subject EEG stress detection remains challenging because discriminative stress-related patterns are both subject-dependent and frequency-specific. Conventional Riemannian methods model spatial covariance mainly in the time domain, overlooking neural oscillations that are critical for high-level cognitive state decoding, while standard temporal tokenization often fragments inter-slice temporal coherence. To address these limitations, we propose \method{}, an Intra-Inter Riemannian Manifold Attention Network for EEG-based stress detection. \method{} constructs spatial covariance matrices independently at each frequency point and maps them to the SPD tangent space, preserving channel-wise geometry together with frequency-specific discriminative cues. It further introduces frequency cluster aggregation to select informative spectral components and reduce redundancy by forming compact, data-driven frequency clusters aligned with EEG rhythms. Finally, an intra-inter slice attention module adaptively integrates local slice-level spectral dynamics and global temporal context across EEG sequences. Experiments on three datasets show that \method{} consistently outperforms five state-of-the-art baselines, achieving up to 82.78\% balanced accuracy while remaining efficient with only 1.60M parameters and 31.95M FLOPs.

</details>


### [223] [Fixed-Set Robustness in Programming by Example: Example Corruption and Semantic Partition Recovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01280)
*Yuan Si,Jialu Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文研究编程范例（PBE）系统在面对有目的性错误示例时的鲁棒性问题，提出一种对抗性污染模型，即对手选择最能破坏合成程序的示例。通过引入版本空间划分聚合（VPA）作为防御机制，并在多个任务和基准上验证其有效性。结果显示，在低边界任务中，传统随机错误评估无法捕捉对抗鲁棒性维度，而VPA仅在清洁语义保持足够投票边界时有效，但这一条件在真实任务中常不满足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有PBE系统多假设错误示例为随机噪声，但忽视了潜在的对抗性污染——即对手可精心设计示例以最大化破坏合成结果。本文旨在揭示这种对抗性威胁的存在及其对系统鲁棒性的关键影响，尤其在低边际任务中被传统评估忽略。

Method: 提出固定集最坏情况污染模型；实现精确与启发式污染搜索算法；设计版本空间划分聚合（VPA）防御策略，通过对不相交示例组进行合成并基于语义签名投票来提升鲁棒性。

Result: 实验表明，对抗性污染可使8个编辑任务全部失效，而随机打字错误等控制组仅在极少数情况下失败（10.3%-16.7%）。生成的低边距示例虽可在预算内被污染，但VPA能恢复部分；然而在公开SyGuS数据集上，由于投票边界接近1，自适应攻击使VPA准确率降至零。此外，实际任务跨越了精确解池边界，且Playgol实验显示配对自举法在对抗性控制下仍具优势。

Conclusion: 低边际PBE任务存在被传统方法忽略的对抗鲁棒性维度；尽管VPA是一种有潜力的防御手段，但其有效性高度依赖于语义投票边界，而该边界在现实任务中往往难以维持，因此其应用具有局限性。

Abstract: Programming-by-example systems infer programs from a small set of input-output examples. Robust PBE work usually models wrong examples as samples from a stochastic noise process and then minimizes an expected or empirical loss. This paper studies a different failure mode: an adversary who sees the synthesizer and chooses the examples whose corruption most damages the returned program. We formalize fixed-set worst-case corruption for finite PBE version spaces, implement exact-within-bounded-pool and heuristic corruption searches for a string-transformation DSL, and introduce version-space partition aggregation (VPA), a defense that synthesizes on disjoint example groups and votes by semantic signatures. The central claim is deliberately bounded and partly negative: low-margin PBE tasks have an adversarial robustness dimension that random-typo and noisy-PBE evaluations miss, while semantic partition aggregation helps only when the clean semantics keep a partition vote margin, which often fails on realistic tasks. Evidence from curated/generated DSL tasks, accepted public SyGuS PBE_SLIA slices, SYNTRA Playgol v2, and noisy-PBE objective baselines supports that boundary. One curated edit flips all 8 spike tasks while 200-trial typo, DSL-pool, and distance-matched random controls succeed on 10.3%, 11.0%, and 16.7%; generated margin-1 rows flip under budget 1 yet VPA recovers them; on public SyGuS the vote margin is near one, so an adaptive attacker drives VPA accuracy to zero; accepted public SyGuS slices move across exact-within-pool budget boundaries; and Playgol shows positive paired-bootstrap gaps against typo and same-pool random controls on the 141 accepted rows. A small exact-output prompt harness over 20 controlled margin-1 tasks shows the same qualitative clean-to-attacked pattern across local and API models, while it is treated as a scope check, not a broad LLM benchmark.

</details>


### [224] [Domain Knowledge Based Temporal-Spatial Graph Convolution Network for ECG Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01282)
*Wenting Ma,Zhipeng Zhang,Xiaohang Yuan,Ningwei Xie,Yuxin Xie,Xiaolin Wang,Meng Guo,Xingang Chai,Zhenjie Yao*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前人工智能在医疗领域广泛应用，但其模型可解释性仍面临挑战，尤其是在心电图识别等专业领域。传统端到端卷积神经网络缺乏对医学先验知识的利用，导致对罕见类别识别效果不佳。因此需要结合领域知识以提升模型性能与可解释性。

Method: 提出一种基于领域知识的图卷积网络模型，构建双流有向图：空间有向图用于捕捉关键点之间的位置关系，时间有向图用于刻画相邻心电周期间的时序依赖；关键解剖学特征点（如PRQST）被作为先验知识嵌入模型中，增强模型对生理结构的理解能力。

Result: 在首个中文心电图智能竞赛数据集上，所提模型整体平均F1得分为88.1%，罕见类别平均F1得分为76.3%，均优于当前最先进的模型，表明引入领域知识显著提升了模型在复杂和稀有类别上的识别能力。

Conclusion: 结合领域知识的图卷积网络有效提升了心电图识别的准确率与可解释性，尤其在处理罕见类别时表现突出，为医疗AI模型的设计提供了新思路。

Abstract: In light of strides in Arti cial Intelligence (AI) and its wide spread application, challenges persist in the interpretability of AI models, particularly within specialized domains like healthcare, such as electro cardiograph (ECG) recognition. Rather than relying solely on end-to-end convolutional neural networks, this paper introduces a novel approach using a domain knowledge-based graph convolution network for ECG recognition. Key landmarks points of PRQST, vital to ECG interpreta tion, are incorporated as domain knowledge. The double-stream directed graph is employed to model both intra and inter ECG cycles. Speci cally, spatial directed graphs capture the positional relationships among key points, while temporal directed graphs delineate temporal dependencies between adjacent cycles in extended ECG sequences. Experimental re sults on the First Chinese ECG Intelligent Competition dataset, which speci cally classify ECG into nine categories, prove the e cacy of the proposed model. The overall average F1 score is 88.1%, the average F1 score of rare categories is 76.3%, both outperform the state-of-the-art models. The introduction of domain knowledge did enhance the detec tion performance, especially for rare categories.

### [225] [Scaling Laws for Grid-Based Approximate Nearest Neighbor Search in High Dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01283)
*Matthew J Liu,Wei Hang Zheng,Vidhan Purohit,Siqi Xie,Chieh-En Li,Jerry Li,Noah Flynn*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文系统地分析了多探针网格算法在数据集大小N和维度d方面的表现，发现其在GloVe嵌入族中存在未被报道的d-缩放交叉现象，即多探针网格搜索在高维下保持近似恒定的维度缩放指数，而其他基于图、树和划分的方法则表现出吞吐量下降。该方法具有接近线性的查询缩放性（N），且索引成本低于其他ANN方法，因此在重建频繁或高维场景中具有竞争力。此外，由于自注意力可形式化为ANN操作，该研究结果对高效Transformer架构的成本分析具有指导意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有网格基近似最近邻（ANN）搜索方法在现代扩展性分析中被忽视，亟需系统评估其在大规模、高维数据下的性能表现；同时，自注意力机制与ANN的关联使得对ANN算法的缩放特性研究具有更广泛的应用价值。

Method: 采用多探针网格算法进行系统性实验，考察其在不同数据集规模N和维度d下的性能表现，对比多种主流方法（图、树、分区等）的缩放行为，并分析索引开销与查询效率之间的权衡。

Result: 在GloVe嵌入族上观察到显著的维度缩放交叉现象：多探针网格法在高维下保持稳定性能，而其他方法性能显著下降；同时，其查询时间近似线性于数据规模N，且索引成本更低。

Conclusion: 网格基方法如多探针网格在重建频繁或高维场景中具备竞争力，尤其在索引成本和维度鲁棒性关键时更具优势；此外，其缩放特性可为高效Transformer架构的设计提供成本分析依据。

Abstract: Grid-based approaches to approximate nearest neighbor (ANN) search have been absent from modern scaling analyses. We present a systematic characterization of a multiprobe grid algorithm with respect to dataset size $N$ and dimensionality $d$. Our experiments reveal a previously unreported $d$-scaling crossover on the GloVe embedding family, in which multiprobe grid search maintains an approximately constant dimensional scaling exponent while other graph-, tree-, and partitioning-based methods exhibit degrading throughput. The advantage comes with near-linear query scaling in $N$, but also with lower indexing cost than competing ANN methods. Our results suggest that grid-based methods such as multiprobe grid may be competitive in rebuild-heavy or high-dimensional settings where indexing cost and dimensional robustness dictate performance. More broadly, recent work has formalized self-attention as an ANN operation. Thus, the $N$- and $d$-scaling properties of ANN algorithms may guide cost analysis of efficient transformer architectures. Code is available at: https://github.com/weiz345/MultiProbeANN.

Abstract: Public lithium-ion battery datasets are increasingly used for state-of-health estimation, remaining-useful-life prediction, anomaly detection, electrochemical diagnostics, second-life analytics, and battery safety research. The released artifact includes metadata tables, scoring scripts, robustness checks, link-checking utilities, and SQL-style query examples. IonSense-QKG positions dataset selection as a data-management problem and provides a reproducible foundation for data-centric quantum battery analytics.

Abstract: Deep learning has outgrown any single mathematical explanation. Rather than presenting isolated results, the book organizes a broad literature into a coherent research narrative: each theory is examined through the object it controls, the assumptions that make it valid, and the phenomena it leaves unexplained. Written for researchers, graduate students, and mathematically trained practitioners, this monograph offers a rigorous map of deep learning theory as it stands today: powerful, incomplete, and increasingly centered on the question of how learned mechanisms arise from scale, data, architecture, and training.

### [229] [Black-Box Inference of LLM Architectural Properties with Restrictive API Access](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01313)
*Christopher Ellis,Shreyas Chaudhari,Mei-Yu Wang,Leighton Barnes,Giulia Fanti,José M. F. Moura*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: NightVision 是一种针对当前受限黑盒 API 的攻击方法，能够通过有限的 API 访问（仅输出单个词元的 logit）推断大型语言模型（LLM）的关键架构参数，包括隐藏维度、深度和参数量。该方法利用新颖的公共集合提示技术结合谱分析来估计隐藏维度，并结合首次生成时间（TTFT）与估计的隐藏维度来推断深度和参数量。在 32 个开源 LLM 上的实验表明，隐藏维度估计平均相对误差为 23%（MoE 模型为 9%），深度和参数量估计误差在超过 30 亿参数的模型上不超过 53%。结果表明，现有 LLM API 仍不足以完全隐藏模型架构细节。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管多数商业 LLM 提供商限制了 API 接口以防止泄露模型架构，但已有研究表明即使在有限接口下仍可恢复部分架构信息。为应对这一威胁，许多厂商已进一步收紧接口，仅提供单个词元的 logit，且禁用 logit 偏置功能。本文旨在验证：即便在这些更严格的限制下，是否仍有架构信息可被推断。

Method: 提出 NightVision 攻击框架，核心包括：1）公共集合提示技术，通过多个提示生成相同输出词元集的对数概率；2）基于这些概率的谱分析以估计隐藏维度；3）结合端到端的首次生成时间（TTFT）测量与估计的隐藏维度，推断模型深度与参数总量。

Result: 在 32 个开源模型上的评估显示，隐藏维度估计平均相对误差为 23%（MoE 模型为 9%），深度和参数量估计误差在参数量大于 30 亿的模型中不超过 53%。消融实验表明精度随提示预算和模型特性变化。

Conclusion: 即使在当前最严格的商用 LLM API 限制下，仍存在可被利用的隐蔽信号，使得关键架构参数得以推断。这表明现有 API 限制不足以完全保护模型架构隐私，需更严格的设计与防护机制。

Abstract: In practice, most commercial LLM providers do not publicly release details of underlying LLM architectures. However, prior work has shown that given limited API access to an LLM (namely, top-$k$ logits and/or a logit bias function), one can recover certain architectural details of an LLM, such as the hidden dimension of the feed-forward network. Perhaps in response to these results, most commercial LLM providers have restricted their APIs to expose only the single logit for each decoded token, and they no longer give users the ability to bias logits. We show that even under current restrictive APIs, several architectural parameters are still recoverable. We present NightVision, an attack that uses restrictive black-box API access to estimate the hidden dimension, depth, and parameter count of an LLM. Algorithmically, NightVision relies on a novel common set prompting technique in which multiple prompts expose log probabilities for the same set of output tokens; a spectral analysis of these results is used to infer hidden dimension. NightVision additionally uses end-to-end time to first token (TTFT) measurements and the estimated hidden dimension to estimate depth and parameter count. We empirically evaluate NightVision on 32 open-source LLMs, recovering hidden dimension to within 23% average relative error across all models (9% on MoE models), and depth and parameter count to within 53% for models exceeding three billion parameters. We run extensive ablations to demonstrate how these accuracies scale with token budget and model properties. Overall, our results suggest that current LLM APIs are not sufficiently restricted to fully obfuscate the architectural details of their underlying models.

</details>

### [231] [How Should Transformers Encode Numeric Values in Electronic Health Records?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01391)
*Maria Elkjær Montgomery,Christian Igel,Mikkel Odgaard,Martin Sillesen,Mads Nielsen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文系统比较了在电子健康记录（EHR）数据中使用离散、连续和混合编码策略对数值进行编码的方法，发现显式建模值-概念交互的策略在精度敏感的算术任务中表现最佳，而保留数值并采用分箱后投影的混合标记方法更具鲁棒性和普适性，最优分箱数遵循与数据集大小相关的幂律关系。模型在各类任务中表现出可靠的“足够好”的数值计算能力，而非精确算术；临床预测中的实验室值增益取决于具体任务。因此，在实际应用中，稳健性和可部署性常优于最大数值精度，建议以混合标记方法作为默认实践。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 显式建模值-概念交互的方法在精度敏感任务中表现最优；混合标记方法（保留数值并分箱后投影）具有更强的鲁棒性和广泛适用性，最优分箱数遵循数据集大小的幂律规律；模型普遍表现出‘足够好’的数值计算能力，而非精确算术；实验室值带来的临床收益因任务而异。

Conclusion: 在实际应用中，稳健性和可部署性往往比极致的数值精度更重要，因此推荐采用混合标记方法作为默认的数值编码策略。

Abstract: How do we encode numeric values in transformer-based sequence processing, particularly in electronic health record (EHR) data? We systematically compare discrete, continuous, and hybrid value encoding strategies using synthetic arithmetic tasks embedded within real-world EHR data, as well as real-world clinical prediction tasks. Our study reveals trade-offs between numeric precision, optimisation stability, and architectural flexibility. We find that approaches that explicitly model value-concept interactions perform best on precision-sensitive arithmetic tasks when architectural constraints permit. Hybrid token-based approaches that retain numeric values but apply binning prior to projection provide a more robust and broadly applicable alternative, with the optimal number of bins following a simple empirically derived power-law in dataset size. Across tasks, models consistently exhibit reliable "good enough" numeric computation rather than exact arithmetic, while clinical gains from incorporating laboratory values are task-dependent. This suggests that robustness and deployability often outweigh maximal numeric precision in practice, motivating hybrid token-based approaches as a practical default.

*Chenxing Liang,Yuchao Lin,Andrii Kryvenko,Wendi Yu,Chuan Li,Jianwen Xie,Xiaofeng Qian,Shuiwang Ji*

TL;DR: 本文提出SpinGTP，一种基于自旋加权球谐函数（SWSH）的新型张量积方法，用于解决现有$\mathrm{E}(3)$-等变网络在3D原子系统建模中因Clebsch-Gordan张量积（CGTP）复杂度高（$O(L^6)$）而导致的可扩展性问题。通过引入SWSH，SpinGTP不仅恢复了被传统GTP遗漏的反对称路径，保持了与GTP相当的渐近效率，还增强了对张量积中奇偶性成分的表达能力。在Tetris、3BPA、SPICE-MACE-OFF和OC20等多个基准测试中，SpinGTP表现接近完整CGTP，尤其在手性材料和非中心对称几何任务中优势显著，为大规模3D原子系统模拟中的高阶等变性提供了完整、高效且数学严谨的解决方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有$\mathrm{E}(3)$-等变网络在3D原子系统建模中受限于CGTP的$O(L^6)$高复杂度，虽有GTP降低复杂度但牺牲了反对称路径的表达能力，导致模型表达不完整。因此亟需一种既能保持计算效率又能完整捕捉物理对称性的新方法。

Method: 提出SpinGTP，将传统标量函数推广至自旋加权球谐函数（SWSH），利用SWSH的代数性质重构张量积，从而恢复缺失的反对称交互路径，并实现对奇偶性成分的自然建模，同时维持GTP的渐近计算效率。

Result: SpinGTP在多个基准数据集上达到与全CGTP相当的精度；在涉及手性材料和非中心对称结构的任务中表现更优，验证了其对反对称路径的有效捕获能力。

Conclusion: SpinGTP提供了一条完整、可扩展且数学严谨的路径，实现高阶等变性，适用于大规模3D原子系统模拟，兼具高效性与强表达力。

Abstract: $\mathrm{E}(3)$-equivariant networks are promising for 3D atomistic system modeling, yet their scalability is limited by the $O(L^6)$ complexity of the Clebsch-Gordan Tensor Product (CGTP). The recently proposed Gaunt Tensor Product (GTP) reduces the complexity but is unable to capture the antisymmetric paths, resulting in incomplete expressivity. In this work, we present SpinGTP, an approach to overcome the GTP incompleteness by generalizing from scalar functions to Spin-Weighted Spherical Harmonics (SWSH). By relying on the algebraic properties of SWSH, SpinGTP recovers the missing antisymmetric interactions while maintaining the asymptotic efficiency of GTP. It also allows for a more expressive equivariant basis that naturally accounts for the parity-odd components of tensor products. We evaluate SpinGTP across diverse benchmarks, including Tetris, 3BPA, SPICE-MACE-OFF, and OC20. Our results show that SpinGTP achieves accuracies comparable to full CGTP. Notably, by explicitly capturing antisymmetric paths, SpinGTP exhibits superior performance in tasks involving chiral materials and non-centrosymmetric geometries. This work provides a complete, scalable, and mathematically rigorous path toward high-order equivariance in large-scale 3D atomistic system simulations.

</details>


### [234] [The Rollout Infrastructure Tax in Coding-Agent Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01415)
*Daniel Thi Graviet,Lovre Pesut,Ivan Dagelic,Vedran Jukic,Ivan Burazin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究比较了四种执行底座（单容器、托管沙箱、Kubernetes编排容器、云虚拟机），发现冷启动延迟差异高达110倍，百万次150步轨迹的预估工时相差1.8倍。表明在训练阶段优化执行底座可显著提升效率，不应仅视为部署基础设施。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前编码代理强化学习将执行基础设施视为背景实现细节，尽管其依赖大量交互式软件回放。忽略基础设施开销导致错失实际效率提升机会，尤其是在训练后阶段，微小的每次回放节省可在大规模下累积成显著收益。

Method: 对四种不同的执行底座进行对比实验：单容器、托管沙箱、Kubernetes-orchestrated容器、云虚拟机，评估其在冷启动延迟和资源消耗方面的表现，并基于此计算大规模训练场景下的工时差异。

Result: 冷启动延迟最高相差110倍，百万次150步轨迹的预估工作量相差1.8倍，表明执行底座选择对整体效率有决定性影响。

Conclusion: 未来的编码代理强化学习系统应将执行底座作为训练系统的一部分进行优化，而不仅将其视为部署的附属组件。

Abstract: Coding-agent reinforcement learning treats execution infrastructure as a background implementation detail, despite relying on large numbers of interactive software rollouts. This is a missed opportunity: measuring infrastructure overhead can reveal practical efficiency gains for RL post-training, where small per-rollout savings compound at scale. We present a comparative study of four execution substrates: single containers, hosted sandboxes, Kubernetes-orchestrated containers, and cloud virtual machines. We find up to $110\times$ variation in cold-start latency and a $1.8\times$ spread in projected worker-hours for one million 150-step trajectories. Our results suggest that future coding-agent RL systems should optimize execution substrates as part of the training system itself, not merely as deployment plumbing.

### [235] [Conditional Inference Trees and Forests for Feature Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01417)
*Robert Milletich,Justin Downes,Steve Goley,Newel Hirst*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Conditional inference forests (CIF) are effective top-$k$ feature-ranking methods, performing competitively in downstream prediction tasks despite computational costs. Bonferroni-corrected Monte Carlo permutation tests control nodewise error under the null. Adaptive stopping and threshold search strategy significantly impact runtime—turning them off increases fitting time by up to 10.8×, but downstream performance is minimally affected (≤0.011 change). Sparse high-dimensional simulations show that forest feature sampling may exclude informative features from splits. Overall, CIF is a robust and reliable feature-ranking method.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To evaluate conditional inference trees (CIT) and forests (CIF) as top-$k$ feature-ranking methods for downstream prediction, especially given their computational cost due to repeated permutation tests and threshold searches. The goal is to assess their performance, scalability, and reliability in real-world and synthetic settings.

Method: The study uses real-data benchmarks across 22 classification and 8 regression datasets, runtime ablation studies to measure the impact of adaptive stopping and threshold search strategies, and synthetic feature-recovery experiments in high-dimensional sparse settings. Statistical control is achieved via Bonferroni-corrected $+1$ Monte Carlo permutation $p$-values under the complete permutation null.

Result: CIF ranks 4th among 17 classification methods and 3rd among 18 regression methods. Runtime increases by 4.0–8.4× when adaptive stopping is disabled and 1.9–10.8× with exact threshold search, yet downstream prediction scores change by at most 0.011. Simulations show that forest feature sampling can omit informative features in high-$p$ settings.

Conclusion: Conditional inference forests are strong performers as top-$k$ feature-ranking methods in the evaluated benchmarks, offering reliable feature selection with minimal impact on downstream prediction even when computational optimizations are disabled.

Abstract: Conditional inference trees (CIT) and conditional inference forests (CIF) reduce split-selection bias by testing features before choosing split thresholds, but repeated permutation tests and threshold searches can make these methods computationally expensive. We study CIT and CIF as top-$k$ feature-ranking methods for downstream prediction using real-data benchmarks, runtime ablations, and synthetic feature-recovery experiments. At a fixed node, if the features and permutation budget do not depend on the node responses, Bonferroni-corrected $+1$ Monte Carlo permutation $p$-values control nodewise rejection under the complete permutation null. CIF ranks 4th among 17 classification methods on 22 datasets and 3rd among 18 regression methods on 8 datasets. With Bonferroni correction held fixed, the CIF runtime ablations indicate that adaptive stopping and the number of thresholds searched have the largest measured effect on runtime: turning off adaptive stopping and using exact threshold search increase fitting time by 4.0--8.4$\times$ and 1.9--10.8$\times$, respectively, while downstream score changes are at most 0.011. Sparse high-$p$ simulations indicate that forest feature sampling can leave informative features out of many split decisions. Overall, the results support CIF as a top-$k$ feature-ranking method in the evaluated downstream prediction benchmarks.

### [236] [On the Utility and Factual Reliability of Pruned Mixture-of-Experts Models in the Biomedical Domain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01444)

Method: 评估四种MoE模型、六种剪枝方法及多种剪枝比例，在生物医学域内与跨域设置下的生成与分类任务表现，综合分析效用与可靠性变化。

Result: 适度剪枝可维持域内效用且短期内不显著影响可靠性，但极端剪枝导致幻觉风险上升；跨域迁移时，模型效用与可靠性均快速下降。

Conclusion: 模型压缩的安全性高度依赖于任务与领域特性；仅以效用为评价标准无法满足高风险应用需求，必须纳入可靠性评估。

Abstract: Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) models offer inference speedups via selective activation but impose substantial memory requirements because the whole network must remain loaded. Structured expert pruning is a practical approach for reducing deployment costs in resource-constrained settings. However, prior studies primarily evaluate benchmark utility, leaving the effect of pruning on factual reliability underexplored, particularly in high-stakes domains such as biomedicine. In this paper, we investigate how domain-specific expert pruning affects both utility and reliability. We assess four MoE models, six pruning methods, and multiple pruning ratios across generation and classification tasks under in-domain (biomedical) and cross-domain settings. Results reveal that moderate pruning preserves in-domain utility without immediate reliability decline, although hallucination risks increase at extreme pruning ratios. When shifting to the general domain, both utility and reliability degrade rapidly. These findings indicate that safe compression depends heavily on the task and domain. Evaluating pruned MoE models solely on utility is inadequate for high-stakes deployment without reliability assessment.

Abstract: We propose a novel hybrid neural architecture, the Geometry-aware R-Structured Kolmogorov-Arnold Network (GRS-KAN), which integrates V.L.Rvachev's R-functions into the Kolmogorov-Arnold Network (KAN) framework. The proposed approach combines two complementary modeling mechanisms: smooth nonlinear structure is learned by KAN branches, while known geometric or logical constraints are encoded analytically using differentiable R-functions. This enables explicit representation of discontinuities, feasible regions, and implicit geometric boundaries within a trainable neural architecture.
  The framework implements differentiable logical operations through R-conjunctions and R-disjunctions, allowing complex geometric supports to be represented analytically and incorporated directly into regression models. Several GRS-KAN variants are introduced, including additive, multiplicative, and agnostic branch-weighted architectures.
  The method is demonstrated on regression problems involving discontinuities with circular and rectangular supports. Numerical experiments show that explicit geometric encoding substantially improves predictive accuracy and boundary localization compared with standard KANs. In the considered benchmarks, geometry-aware GRS-KAN models reduce test RMSE by up to 67% while simultaneously improving interpretability through explicit analytical representation of the learned geometric structure. The agnostic variant further demonstrates the ability to automatically determine whether geometric priors are beneficial for a given learning task.

### [238] [Token Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01455)
*Kathan Shah*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 设计Ember优化器，利用嵌入和LM头矩阵独特的梯度结构，采用低维近似与轻量状态管理，通过分析优化轨迹的1D射线性质，构建高效、可扩展的更新机制，并实现分布式部署。

Result: Ember在多种任务（监督微调、强化学习、预训练）中均优于或相当优于Adam，显存占用减少约50%，支持更大批量和参数规模，且优化轨迹可被简单的一维射线模型良好拟合。

Abstract: Language models learn continuous programs over discrete symbols, with the embedding table and LM-head acting as the read/write interface between them. We show that this interface has gradient geometry distinct from dense hidden weights which can be exploited to improve the Pareto frontier across supervised finetuning, RL, and pretraining, while only utilizing kilobytes of optimizer state. We introduce Ember, a lightweight optimizer for embedding and LM-head matrices that utilizes O(V + D) VRAM, instead of Adam's O(2VD), and forgoes the need to shard both token table optimizer states. We provide empirical evidence that Ember scales effectively across batch size and parameter count. We show that the optimization trajectory of tokens can be well described by a simple 1D ray, counter to the popular belief that neural net parameters navigate a heavily nonconvex landscape. We provide a principled view on the surprisingly narrow space of optimizers that suffice for Transformer training. Finally, we open-source our distributed Ember implementation that merges cleanly with existing ZeRO/FSDP setups to support further research at https://github.com/katop1234/ember

### [239] [Class-Grouped Normalized Momentum and Faster Hyperparameter Exploration to Tackle Class Imbalance in Federated Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01474)
*Haemin Park,Diego Klabjan,Martin W. Braun,Xiuqi Li,Balakrishnan Ananthanarayanan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出FedCGNM，一种用于联邦学习中类别不平衡问题的客户端优化器。通过将类别按最小组内方差分组，为每组维护动量并归一化，以均衡多数类与少数类的梯度幅度，并降低稀有类别梯度中的噪声。进一步提出FedHOO算法，基于X-armed-bandit方法高效优化采样率，在小客户端场景下实现线性成本下的并行评估。实验表明，该方法在多个公开和私有数据集上均优于基线，尤其在小规模联邦设置下表现更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 联邦学习中类别不平衡导致少数类预测性能差，而传统集中式处理方法因隐私和异构性约束无法应用，亟需在客户端侧设计有效解决方案。

Method: FedCGNM将类别分组，基于最小组内方差进行聚类；每组维护独立动量，归一化后求和作为更新方向；结合理论分析考虑时变重采样率；引入FedHOO算法，利用联邦并行性以线性成本评估多组采样率组合。

Result: 在四个公开长尾基准数据集和一个专有芯片缺陷数据集上的实验显示，FedCGNM显著优于现有基线方法，且在小规模联邦场景下，结合FedHOO可进一步提升性能。

Conclusion: FedCGNM通过分组动量归一化有效缓解联邦学习中的类别不平衡问题，结合FedHOO在小客户端场景下实现高效采样率优化，整体性能领先，具备理论保障与实际应用价值。

Abstract: Class imbalance poses a critical challenge in federated learning (FL), where underrepresented classes suffer from poor predictive performance yet cannot be addressed by standard centralized techniques due to privacy and heterogeneity constraints. We propose FedCGNM (Federated Class-Grouped Normalized Momentum), a client-side optimizer in FL that partitions classes into a small number of groups based on minimum within-group variance, maintains a momentum per group, normalizes each group momentum to unit length, and uses the summation of the normalized group momentums as an update direction. This design both equalizes gradient magnitude across majority and minority groups and mitigates the noise inherent in rare-class gradients. We further provide a theoretical convergence analysis explicitly accounting for time-varying resampling-rates. Additionally, to efficiently optimize these rates in small-client regimes, we introduce FedHOO, an X-armed-bandit (XAB) based algorithm that exploits federated parallelism that evaluates many combinations of two candidate rates per client at linear cost. Empirical evaluation on four public long-tailed benchmarks and a proprietary chip-defect dataset demonstrates that FedCGNM consistently outperforms baselines, with FedHOO yielding further gains in small-scale federations.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有缩放定律未能充分分离训练步数和批量大小的影响，导致对最优批量大小的预测不够准确。为了提升模型训练效率和可扩展性，需要一种更精确且鲁棒的缩放定律。

Result: 三元定律能准确预测最优批量大小的缩放行为，且仅需较少训练运行即可实现稳健拟合；进一步推导出的次优批量缩放规律与已有实证结果高度一致。

Conclusion: 三元缩放定律在模型规模、训练步数和批量大小之间建立了更精确的关系，显著提升了缩放规律的准确性与实用性，为高效训练深度学习模型提供了理论支持。

Abstract: We propose a scaling law that takes into account model size and training data while explicitly splitting the latter into training steps and batch size (called three-term law). Fitting the proposed law on a large set of training runs, we find that it correctly recovers the scaling of the optimal batch size. Moreover, because it makes use of training runs with suboptimal batch size, our proposed law can be robustly fit with a significantly smaller amount of training runs. We further show that the three-term law can be used to derive scaling laws for suboptimal batch sizes, and that it matches previous empirical findings related to the critical batch size.

### [241] [Don't Let Gains FADE: Breaking Down Policy Gradient Weights in RL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01490)
*Juliette Decugis,Sean O'Brien,Francis Bach,Gabriel Synnaeve,Taco Cohen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出FADE（Focal Advantage with Dynamic Entropy），一种自适应优势函数，通过动态调整梯度权重来解决强化学习后训练中训练不稳定和多样性崩溃的问题。它基于一个统一框架，将优势分解为正负梯度质量在两个正交轴上的分布：符号轴上平衡更新以避免熵或权重几何的坍塌；难度轴上聚焦难题以增强信号但需权衡样本量。训练过程中探索与利用阶段的需求不同，因此FADE根据训练动态自动调节策略。实验表明，FADE在7B和32B模型规模下分别比最佳静态基线提前20k和2k步达到峰值性能，并在LiveCodeBench和AIME上实现了最优的准确率-多样性权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有强化学习后训练方法存在训练不稳定和多样性崩溃问题，尽管优势函数能有效重塑训练目标并重加权回溯路径，但方法繁多且缺乏选择依据，亟需一个统一框架指导优势函数的设计与使用。

Method: 提出一个统一框架，将任意优势函数分解为沿符号轴和难度轴的正负梯度质量分布；设计FADE模型，根据训练动态自动调度梯度权重，实现对探索与利用阶段需求的自适应响应。

Result: FADE在7B模型上比最优静态基线提前20,000步达到最高pass@1性能，在32B模型上提前2,000步；同时在LiveCodeBench和AIME数据集上实现了最佳的准确率-多样性平衡，显著优于现有方法。

Conclusion: 通过构建统一的优势函数分析框架并引入自适应机制，FADE有效解决了强化学习后训练中的稳定性与多样性矛盾，展现出更强的训练效率与综合性能，为大语言模型推理能力提升提供了新范式。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning post-training dramatically improves LLM reasoning, but suffers from training instability and diversity collapse. Advantage functions offer an appealing fix: they reshape the training objective, reweight which rollouts drive learning, and are trivial to implement. Yet a proliferation of methods makes it unclear which advantage to use and when. We cut through the confusion with a unifying framework that decomposes any advantage into its positive and negative gradient mass along two orthogonal axes. On the sign axis, imbalanced updates collapse either entropy or weight geometry. On the difficulty axis, hard-problem focus sharpens signal but costs sample size. Both trade-offs shift during training: exploration favors balance and hard focus; exploitation favors suppression and medium focus. This motivates FADE (Focal Advantage with Dynamic Entropy), a self-adapting advantage that reads training dynamics to schedule the gradient weight automatically. FADE reaches peak pass@1 20k steps earlier than the best static baseline at the 7B scale and 2k steps earlier at the 32B , while achieving the best accuracy-diversity trade-off across all pass@k on LiveCodeBench and AIME.

</details>


### [242] [Unveiling the Non-Monotonic Effect of Privacy on Generalization under Byzantine Robustness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01492)
*Thomas Boudou,Batiste Le Bars,Nirupam Gupta,Aurélien Bellet*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文研究了分布式学习中拜占庭鲁棒性、局部差分隐私（LDP）和泛化误差之间的权衡关系。研究表明，这种权衡并非普遍成立，而是依赖于隐私强度：在高噪声（强隐私）情况下，增加隐私反而降低泛化误差，无冲突；而在低噪声（弱隐私）情况下，隐私增强会恶化泛化性能，存在冲突。理论通过算法稳定性上下界解释了泛化误差的非单调现象，并通过实证验证了结论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究揭示了拜占庭鲁棒性、局部差分隐私（LDP）与优化误差之间的基本三难困境。然而，该三难是否适用于泛化误差尚不明确。本文旨在探究泛化误差与隐私、鲁棒性之间的关系，揭示其依赖于隐私强度的关键机制。

Method: 通过构建匹配的上下界分析算法稳定性，结合理论推导与实证评估，研究在不同隐私噪声水平下，拜占庭鲁棒分布式学习在LDP约束下的泛化行为。

Result: 在高噪声（强隐私）环境下，提升隐私可减少泛化误差，无冲突；在低噪声（弱隐私）环境下，隐私增强导致泛化性能下降，存在冲突。理论与实验一致支持这一非单调现象。

Conclusion: 泛化误差与隐私、鲁棒性之间的权衡并非普适，而是由隐私强度决定。该发现为设计兼顾隐私与鲁棒性的分布式学习系统提供了新的理论指导。

Abstract: Recent work has established a fundamental trilemma between Byzantine robustness, local differential privacy (LDP), and optimization error in distributed learning. We show that this trilemma does not universally extend to generalization error, but instead depends critically on the privacy regime. Specifically, in the high-noise regime (strong privacy), we prove that increasing privacy reduces the generalization error, i.e., there is no tension between robustness and privacy. In the low-noise regime (weaker privacy), however, the tension between robustness and privacy reappears and increasing privacy indeed degrades generalization. Our theory explains this surprising non-monotonic behavior of the generalization error via matching lower and upper bounds on the algorithmic stability of Byzantine-robust distributed learning under LDP constraints. We corroborate and further analyze these theoretical findings with empirical evaluations.

Result: 实验表明，即使使用基础方法，所学的策略嵌入仍能捕捉到有意义的行为特征，且不同方法在下游任务上的表现差异显著，说明嵌入具有实际效用。

Conclusion: 本工作首次系统地比较了自监督学习在博弈策略表示中的应用，证明了学习到的嵌入具备实用性，为后续研究提供了可复现的基准与工具。

Abstract: We investigate the problem of learning useful policy representations (embeddings) in two-player zero-sum imperfect-information games. We make three contributions: First, we introduce methods of creating datasets of policies for a given game. Second, we propose methods to learn policy representations. Third, we introduce downstream tasks to evaluate the effectiveness of such representations.
  We evaluate each dataset method, embedding method, and downstream task on Kuhn and Leduc Poker. Although our methods are very basic, we demonstrate that useful behavioral representations are present in the learned embeddings. To our knowledge, this work is among the first to systematically compare self-supervised learning techniques for learning policy representations in games. Our code is available at https://github.com/VitamintK/ssl-project for others to extend.

### [244] [The risk of KV cache compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01520)
*Lukas Haverbeck,Carmen Amo Alonso,Andres Felipe Posada-Moreno,Sebastian Trimpe,Marco Pavone*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了长序列下Transformer推理中因注意力机制反复读取大缓存导致的计算开销问题，提出通过压缩键值（KV）缓存来缓解瓶颈。现有方法多依赖经验设计，缺乏理论指导。本文从理论上分析了KV缓存压缩的最小最大风险，揭示了在何种条件下压缩是可能且有效的，并据此提出新的设计原则，适用于预填充和自回归解码场景，实现最优压缩性能。基于这些原则，作者开发了一种实用算法，在LongBench基准上表现出色，为具有理论保障的高效缓存压缩提供了系统性路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Transformer在处理长序列时，由于软注意力机制需要频繁访问大型键值（KV）缓存，导致推理成本高昂。虽然已有方法尝试通过压缩缓存来优化，但其设计主要依赖实验试错，缺乏理论支撑。尤其在最坏情况下，压缩可能不可行，而现有理论无法提供在可行区间内的系统性设计指导。因此亟需一个能刻画压缩可能性与效率的理论框架。

Method: 本文引入最小最大风险分析，以衡量KV缓存压缩的理论极限。通过定义缓存的内在可压缩性（intrinsic compressibility），建立压缩误差的下界，并据此推导出在因果掩码约束下的最优压缩策略。这些理论结果转化为可落地的设计原则，支持高效实现于预填充和自回归解码流程中。

Result: 理论分析揭示了在特定条件下准确压缩是可能的，并给出了最小最大风险的下界。基于此设计的算法在LongBench上的实验显示优异性能，优于现有方法，验证了理论指导的实际有效性。

Conclusion: 本文建立了KV缓存压缩的理论基础，首次将压缩可行性与缓存内在特性关联，提出了可实现最小最大风险的压缩设计原则。所提出的算法在实际任务中表现良好，为高效、可靠、有理论保障的缓存压缩提供了新范式。

Abstract: Transformer inference on long sequences is expensive because softmax attention repeatedly reads from a large KV cache. The prevalent approach to this bottleneck is KV cache compression, which replaces the full cache with a compact summary. Despite its practical importance, the design of such summaries is largely driven by empirical experimentation. On the theoretical side, existing results show that KV cache compression can be impossible in the worst case, but offer little systematic guidance for designing algorithms in regimes where accurate compression is possible. We bridge this gap by characterizing the minimax risk of KV cache compression in terms of the intrinsic compressibility of a cache, revealing when and how accurate compression is possible. These results yield novel design principles for KV cache compression under causal masking that map efficiently to prefill and autoregressive decoding while achieving minimax-optimal risk. We instantiate these principles in a practical algorithm and report promising performance on LongBench in targeted experiments. Overall, our results provide a principled avenue for practical KV cache compression with theoretical guarantees.

### [245] [Multi-Head Recurrent Memory Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01523)
*Jiatong Li,Samuel Yeh,Sharon Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出Multi-Head Recurrent Memory (MHM)框架，通过将记忆分区为独立头并采用阶段式选择-更新策略，解决长上下文下记忆保留能力下降的问题。其中轻量级实例MHM-LRU在10万至100万token范围内显著提升记忆保留率与端到端准确率，在896K token的RULER-HQA任务中，记忆保留率从不足30%提升至73.96%。该方法无需训练、无额外词元开销，且适用于不同模型规模和任务类型，证明了架构优化在实现可靠长上下文记忆中的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有循环记忆代理在长上下文场景下性能随上下文长度增长而系统性下降，主要瓶颈在于记忆保留能力不足，因传统设计将记忆视为单一文本块，每次更新都可能覆盖已有内容。

Method: 提出多头循环记忆（MHM）框架，将记忆划分为多个独立头，采用阶段式‘选择-更新’策略：每一步仅选择一个头进行更新，其余头被结构化保护，避免被覆盖；引入轻量级实例MHM-LRU，通过最近最少更新策略实现均匀头利用，零额外词元开销。

Result: 在10万至100万词元范围内的长上下文基准测试中，MHM-LRU显著提升记忆保留率与端到端准确率；在RULER-HQA任务中，896K词元时记忆保留率从<30%提升至73.96%，且性能提升在不同模型家族、规模和任务类型间具有泛化性。

Conclusion: 通过将记忆保留的负担从模型行为转移到架构设计，MHM框架，特别是其轻量级实现MHM-LRU，为构建可靠、可扩展的长上下文循环记忆提供了高效且低成本的解决方案，验证了架构优化在长序列处理中的关键作用。

Abstract: Recurrent memory agents extend LLMs to arbitrarily long contexts by iteratively consolidating input into a fixed-size memory window. Despite their scalability, these agents exhibit a well-documented reliability problem: end-to-end performance degrades systematically as context length grows. We diagnose this failure by decomposing performance into two factors--memory capture and memory retention--and quantitatively confirm that retention is the dominant bottleneck. Retention collapses because existing designs maintain memory as a monolithic text block, forcing every update to risk overwriting previously retained content. Motivated by this diagnosis, we propose Multi-Head Recurrent Memory (MHM), a general, training-free framework that partitions memory into independent heads governed by a stage-wise select-then-update strategy. At each step, exactly one head is selected for update while the remaining heads are structurally shielded from overwriting, shifting the burden of retention from model behavior to architectural design. As a lightweight instantiation, we introduce Least-Recently-Updated MHM (MHM-LRU), which guarantees uniform head utilization with zero additional token overhead. Extensive experiments on long-context benchmarks show that MHM-LRU substantially improves both retention and end-to-end accuracy across the 100K--1M token range, where baselines degrade sharply. On RULER-HQA at 896K tokens, MHM-LRU improves the memory retention rate from less than 30% to 73.96%. These gains generalize across model families, scales, and task types, positioning architectural optimization as a practical and cost-efficient path toward reliable long-context recurrent memory.

</details>


### [246] [Wind-Aware Reinforcement Learning Control of a Small Quadrotor Using Learned Onboard Wind Estimation in Simulated Atmospheric Turbulence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01528)
*Abdullah Al Tasim,Wei Sun*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种两阶段学习框架，先通过注意力增强的门控循环网络估计飞行器周围的局部风速，再将估计结果用于强化学习飞行控制器。风速估计器在未见过的风场中表现出色，水平风速误差为0.40 m/s，方向误差为3.2度，且对垂直爬升有良好泛化能力（技能得分0.861）。基于此估计的强化学习控制器相比无风感知的PID基准，在4-12 m/s平均风速下将轨迹跟踪误差降低48%，并在所有测试场景中胜出。消融实验表明，性能提升由运动学和风感知两部分贡献，其中风感知部分随风速增加而占比上升，符合气动阻力的二次方关系。控制器在超出分布的强风（13-15 m/s）下仍能稳健运行，而基准控制器则完全失效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 小型多旋翼飞行器在大气边界层执行任务时，常遭遇与自身空速相当的湍流风，导致轨迹跟踪性能下降，传统反馈控制难以应对。因此需要更智能的风感知与自适应控制方法以提升飞行稳定性与精度。

Method: 采用两阶段学习架构：第一阶段使用注意力增强的门控循环网络（GRU），基于数千次模拟飞行数据（包含von Karman湍流、幂律剪切和偏转）训练风速估计模型；第二阶段使用近端策略优化（PPO）强化学习算法，接收冻结的风速估计输入，实现鲁棒飞行控制。

Result: 风速估计器在未见风场中达到0.40 m/s的均方根误差和3.2度的方向误差，接近不可分辨湍流的物理极限；强化学习控制器相比风盲型PID控制器在4-12 m/s风速下减少48%的轨迹跟踪误差，100%胜出；在13-15 m/s强风下仍保持稳定，而基准控制器崩溃。

Conclusion: 结合风速估计与强化学习的两阶段控制框架显著提升了小型多旋翼在复杂风场中的飞行性能与鲁棒性，尤其在强风条件下展现出优异的泛化能力和容错性，为未来自主飞行系统设计提供了有效范式。

Abstract: Small multirotor aircraft are increasingly tasked with operations in the atmospheric boundary layer, where turbulent winds comparable to the vehicle's airspeed degrade trajectory tracking and can defeat conventional feedback control. This work illustrates a two-stage learning pipeline that first estimates the local wind from onboard kinematics and dynamics and then exploits that estimate inside a reinforcement learning (RL) flight controller. The wind estimator, an attention-augmented gated recurrent network trained on thousands of simulated flights through von Karman turbulence with power-law shear and veer, recovers the horizontal wind vector with a per-flight root-mean-square error of 0.40 m/s and a direction error of 3.2 degrees on unseen wind regimes, an accuracy near the floor imposed by unresolved turbulence, and generalizes to vertical ascent profiles with a skill score of 0.861 over a constant-wind reference. A proximal policy optimization controller receiving the frozen estimator's output reduces horizontal trajectory tracking error by 48% relative to a wind-blind proportional-derivative baseline across mean winds of 4 m/s to 12 m/s, winning on 100% of evaluation episodes. A three-way ablation decomposes this improvement into a kinematic component, available without wind information, and a wind-perception component; the perception share rises with wind speed, from small in light winds toward roughly half the total benefit in strong winds, consistent with the quadratic scaling of aerodynamic drag. The controller degrades gracefully on out-of-distribution winds of 13 m/s to 15 m/s, where the baseline fails catastrophically.

### [247] [Certified World Models as Sensing Clocks: Drift-Aware Deadlines for Active Perception](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01537)
*Hongbo Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于认证世界模型的感知时钟机制，通过量化预测有效性时长来决定何时需要重新感知。该方法从经过验证的等变世界模型出发，推导出无感知间隔的截止时间，并强调部署时必须考虑漂移：仅依赖流形上的李雅普诺夫率会高估有效续航时间，而校准后的原生滚动漂移包络才能提供实际部署保障。在冻结的3D VN-JEPA模型上，该时钟有效控制了不同种子和数据分片下的证书违规情况；在合成基准测试中，其在相同感知预算下显著减少事件尾部违规，优于传统期望信念调度。但研究也发现，在短时程冻结模型下，经验性符合时长与部署时钟一致，且部分重置探索未显示谱项在预算匹配下有明显优势。因此，贡献在于提供一种可认证的感知时钟原语和漂移感知的部署方法，而非宣称谱时钟在所有非谱调度中占优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有世界模型虽能估计预测有效性，但缺乏将此有效性转化为可操作的感知决策机制。尤其在实际部署中，忽略动态漂移会导致过度自信的无感知行为，引发安全风险。因此需要一种能结合模型漂移特性的、可认证的感知调度机制。

Method: 基于审计过的等变世界模型，构建一个以漂移感知为核心的感知时钟。通过分析原生滚动过程中的漂移包络，设计校准后的部署截止时间。利用冻结的3D VN-JEPA模型进行验证，并在合成基准中对比不同调度策略的表现。

Result: 在多个实验设置中，所提出的感知时钟能够有效控制证书违规，尤其在保持感知预算不变的前提下，显著降低事件尾部违规率。在短时程冻结模型中，经验性符合时长与部署时钟表现一致，谱项未显示出显著优势。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一个可认证的感知时钟原语和漂移感知的部署方法，为自主系统提供了可靠的无感知区间管理机制。但该方法并非在所有场景下都优于非谱调度器，其优势体现在对漂移敏感的部署环境中。

Abstract: Certified world models estimate how long their predictions remain valid. We turn this validity horizon into an operational sensing clock: a rule for when an agent should stop coasting and re-sense. Starting from an audited equivariant world model, we derive a deadline for no-sensing intervals and show that deployable deadlines in learned world models must be drift-aware: on-manifold Lyapunov rates alone overestimate coasting validity, while calibrated native rollout-drift envelopes carry the deployed guarantee. On a frozen 3D VN-JEPA model, the resulting clock controls held-out interval-simultaneous certificate violation across seeds and data shards. In a cue-conditioned theorem-bed (a synthetic bench where all schedulers share the exact model, isolating the scheduling rule), the clock remains valid on the deployment distribution and substantially reduces eventful-tail violations relative to exact-mixture expected-belief scheduling at matched sensing budget. We also report limits: in the short-horizon frozen VN-JEPA regime, empirical conformal horizons match the deployed clock on validity and budget, and a partial-reset exploration finds no clean budget-matched advantage for the spectral term. Thus the contribution is a certified sensing-clock primitive and drift-aware deployment method, not a claim that spectral clocks empirically dominate all non-spectral schedulers.

### [248] [Evolutionary Feature Engineering for Structured Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01548)
*Ege Onur Taga,Yilin Zhuang,M. Emrullah Ildiz,Petros Mol,Abhimanyu Das,Karthik Duraisamy,Samet Oymak*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: EFE 是一种利用大语言模型进行演化的特征工程框架，通过生成可插入现有机器学习管道的 Python 程序化转换，提升结构化数据的预处理效果。在时间序列预测中，EFE-Time 通过学习可逆、数据特定的归一化方法，显著降低预测误差（如 MASE、WQL、MAE），最大提升达 19%；在表格预测中，EFE-Tab 能演化出简洁且可解释的特征程序，提升或媲美现有 LLM 方法，在决策树等模型上保持高准确率与可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统特征工程依赖人工经验，效率低且难以适应复杂数据。大语言模型虽具备生成能力，但缺乏对数据上下文和下游性能的反馈机制。因此需要一种能结合数据上下文与模型表现反馈的自动化演化框架，以提升特征工程的准确性与可解释性。

Method: EFE 将预处理变换表示为具有标准化 fit/transform 接口的 Python 程序，通过演化算法优化候选程序。进化过程中结合数据上下文、统计摘要及验证集上的下游性能反馈进行迭代优化。分别在时间序列和表格数据场景下构建 EFE-Time 与 EFE-Tab 实例。

Result: EFE-Time 在多个时间序列数据集上平均降低预测误差 3% 以上，最高达 19%（如 COVID-Deaths）；EFE-Tab 在表格数据上提升或匹配现有 LLM 方法性能，尤其在决策树上实现高准确率与强可解释性。整体表明 LLM 演化可有效提升结构化数据处理的准确性与可解释性。

Conclusion: LLM-based 演化能够高效自动发现高质量、可解释的特征工程策略，显著提升结构化数据建模效果，同时兼顾模型可解释性，为自动化机器学习提供了新范式。

Abstract: Large language models are increasingly used as open-ended search operators in evolutionary optimization. We introduce Evolutionary Feature Engineering (EFE), a framework for using LLM-based evolution to discover preprocessing transformations for structured data. EFE represents transformations as Python programs with a standardized fit/transform interface, allowing them to be inserted directly into existing machine learning pipelines. During evolution, candidate programs are refined using dataset context, summary statistics, and downstream performance feedback on validation set. We instantiate EFE in two settings. For time-series forecasting, EFE-Time learns invertible, dataset-specific normalizations that improve off-the-shelf time-series foundation models. It reduces forecasting errors (MASE, WQL, MAE) 3% or more when averaged across datasets and improvements are as much as 19% on the COVID-Deaths dataset. Notably, these improvements occur with recent TSFMs such as Chronos-2. For tabular prediction, EFE-Tab evolves compact feature programs that add useful interpretable features and remove redundant ones, improving or matching existing LLM-based feature-engineering methods. We found EFE-Tab to be particularly effective on classical decision trees, where small sets of evolved features yield competitive accuracy while preserving interpretability. Overall, EFE demonstrates that LLM-based evolution can improve both accuracy and interpretability when automatically tackling structured data.

</details>


### [249] [X-LogSMask: Expand Transformer for Graph-Structured Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01553)
*Leyan Li,Rennong Yang,Zhenxing Zhang,Liping Hu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: X-LogSMask是一种可解释的多头对数结构掩码，通过将对称归一化的图拓扑直接注入注意力logits，使自注意力机制更适应稀疏、有结构且多尺度的图数据。它利用对数变换将连接性转化为拓扑感知的门控信号，抑制不支持的节点交互，同时保留特征依赖的注意力。通过为不同注意力头分配归一化邻接矩阵的不同幂次，实现不同结构半径和单层内的多跳信息传播。实验表明，该方法在20个节点、边和图级基准上表现优异，在13个数据集上达到当前最优性能，并在轻量级单层配置中仍具竞争力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图变换器因自注意力机制与图数据的稀疏、结构化和多尺度特性不匹配而存在局限，尽管已有方法引入结构编码或注意力约束，但往往增加复杂度且缺乏可解释性。因此需要一种简单、可解释的结构掩码来提升自注意力在图学习中的有效性。

Method: 提出X-LogSMask，通过将对称归一化的邻接矩阵进行对数变换生成结构掩码，将其注入注意力logits；不同注意力头使用归一化邻接矩阵的不同幂次，赋予各自不同的结构半径，实现多跳传播；保持原始Transformer架构不变，仅修改注意力机制。

Result: 在20个图学习任务中，配备X-LogSMask的Transformer在13个数据集上达到最优性能，且在轻量级单层设置下依然表现良好，验证了其高效性和可解释性。

Conclusion: 简单的、可解释的结构掩码能够有效提升自注意力在图学习中的表现，无需修改Transformer架构即可使其成为强大的图学习算子。

Abstract: Transformers have become general-purpose architectures, but their all-to-all self-attention is poorly matched to graph data, whose interactions are sparse, structured and multi-scale. Existing Graph Transformers address this mismatch through structural encodings, hybrid message-passing modules or learned attention constraints, often introducing additional complexity and limited interpretability. Here we introduce X-LogSMask, an explainable multi-head logarithmic structural mask that injects symmetrically normalized graph topology directly into attention logits. The logarithmic transform converts structural connectivity into a topology-aware gating signal, suppressing unsupported node interactions while preserving feature-dependent attention. By assigning different powers of the normalized adjacency matrix to different attention heads, X-LogSMask gives each head a defined structural radius and supports multi-hop information propagation within a single layer. We further show that a standard Transformer encoder can be interpreted as one-step message passing on a complete graph, motivating X-LogSMask as a topology-constrained alternative to unrestricted self-attention. Across 20 node-, edge- and graph-level benchmarks, Transformers equipped with X-LogSMask achieve state-of-the-art performance on 13 datasets and remain competitive in a lightweight one-layer configuration. These results show that simple, interpretable structural masks can make self-attention an effective graph-learning operator without changing the Transformer architecture. The code is available at https://github.com/LiLeyan-0120/X-LogSMask.
