### [250] [Geometric Signatures of Reasoning: A Spectral Perspective on Task Hardness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01571)
*Aria Masoomi,Mahsa Bazzaz,Adel Javanmard,Vahab Mirrokni*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大语言模型在链式思维（CoT）推理过程中隐藏状态空间中的轨迹几何特性，将每个推理过程形式化为$\mathbb{R}^d$中的离散曲线，并通过谱、位置和运动学几何函数进行表征。提出有效维度$d_ρ$作为轨迹复杂性的度量，理论表明更平坦的特征值谱对应更难任务，因探索更多隐藏维度。实验显示，在MATH500数据集上，$d_ρ$在区分难易问题上达到0.93 AUC；运动学特征可仅基于前20%生成标记预测正确性，且跨难度问题具有泛化能力，表明模型内部推理轨迹的形状是任务难度与解质量的可靠指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究关注链式思维（CoT）推理链的长度和内容，但对其内部几何结构了解有限。本文旨在揭示推理轨迹在隐藏状态空间中的几何特性，以理解任务难度与解质量之间的内在关联。

Method: 将推理链视为$\mathbb{R}^d$中的离散轨迹，使用谱分析（如特征值分布）、位置统计（均值、分散度）、运动学特征（速度、加速度、初始/当前状态）等几何函数对其进行建模。引入有效维度$d_ρ$量化轨迹复杂性，并构建预测模型评估其对任务难度与解正确性的判别能力。

Result: 实验表明，$d_ρ$在区分数学推理问题的难易程度时达到0.93 AUC；运动学特征可在仅生成前20%标记时预测解的正确性，且具备跨难度泛化能力。轨迹几何特征能有效反映任务难度与解质量。

Conclusion: 模型内部推理轨迹的几何形状是理解任务难度和解质量的有力工具，其几何特征不仅可用于早期预测解的正确性，还可为未来早停策略提供依据。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning enables large language models (LLMs) to solve complex problems by generating intermediate reasoning steps. While much attention has been paid to the length and content of these reasoning chains, far less is known about their internal geometry. We study the \emph{geometry} of CoT trajectories in the hidden state space of transformer models, formalizing each reasoning chain as a discrete curve in $\mathbb{R}^d$ and characterizing it through spectral, positional, and kinematic geometric functionals. We introduce the effective dimension $d_ρ$ as a measure of trajectory complexity and show theoretically that trajectories with flatter eigenvalue spectra correspond to harder tasks, as they explore more of the hidden dimensions. Lastly, we explore how kinematic features of the trajectory, mean position, positional dispersion, initial and current hidden states, mean velocity, mean speed, and speed dispersion, can be used to predict solution correctness before generation is complete, and may inform future early-stopping strategies. Experimentally, on mathematical reasoning problems from the MATH500 dataset, $d_ρ$ achieves $0.93$ AUC in distinguishing easy from hard problems, while kinematic features potentially can predict correctness from only the first $20\%$ of generated tokens. These correctness signatures transfer across questions of varying difficulty, establishing that the shape of a model's internal reasoning trajectory is a principled window into both task hardness and solution quality.

### [251] [BOUNDARY_SYNC: Measuring Communication-Induced Representational Coupling in Multi-Agent LLM Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01600)
*Zewen Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大型语言模型（LLMs）作为通信代理时，代理间通信是否导致输出趋同。提出 BOUNDARY_SYNC 协议，通过耦合放大因子（CAF）衡量表征耦合，CAF < 1 表示同质化，CAF > 1 表示多样化。在控制的 GPT-4o 实验中（N=30，约 9,900 次 API 调用），测量文本和图像通信中的耦合效应。主要发现：(1) 文本通信导致显著同质化（CAF=0.803 [0.740, 0.873]，d=1.30，p<0.001），经无通信对照和提示扰动验证；(2) 图像通信在同模态基线中也表现出同质化（CAF=0.834 [0.811, 0.858]），效果相当；(3) 群体规模调节耦合方向——K=5 时同质化，而 K=3 时 CAF > 1.0（点估计值分别为 1.14 和 1.06，置信区间待定），表明向多样化转变；(4) 跨模型复制显示极端变异（CAF 0.034–0.803），DeepSeek 受格式伪影主导；(5) 耦合为无状态，由提示上下文驱动而非累积更新，持续共识导致单调收敛。结果表明 LLM 代理耦合是真实、可测量且可在提示层面控制的，对多代理系统设计具有直接意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在揭示大型语言模型作为通信代理时，其交互是否会导致输出趋于一致（同质化），并探索影响这一过程的关键因素，如通信模态、群体规模及模型差异，以提升多智能体系统的可控性与多样性。

Method: 提出 BOUNDARY_SYNC 协议，利用耦合放大因子（CAF）量化代理间的表征耦合程度；在受控条件下使用 GPT-4o 进行实验，评估文本与图像通信下的耦合效应；采用无通信对照组、提示扰动控制、不同群组规模（K=3 vs K=5）以及跨模型复制（包括 DeepSeek）等方法进行验证；分析结果基于统计检验（如 t 检验、效应量 d）和置信区间。

Result: (1) 文本通信显著导致同质化（CAF=0.803，p<0.001）；(2) 图像通信同样引发同质化（CAF=0.834）；(3) 群体规模影响耦合方向：K=5 时同质化，K=3 时出现多样化趋势（CAF>1.0）；(4) 跨模型实验显示高变异性（CAF 0.034–0.803），DeepSeek 受格式问题干扰严重；(5) 耦合行为无状态，仅依赖提示上下文，持续共识导致输出单调收敛。

Conclusion: LLM 代理之间的耦合是真实存在的，可通过提示工程进行测量与调控。通信模式、群体规模等因素显著影响耦合方向，这对设计稳定、可控且具备多样性的多智能体系统具有重要指导意义。

Abstract: As large language models (LLMs) are deployed as communicating agents, does inter-agent communication cause outputs to converge? We introduce BOUNDARY_SYNC, a protocol measuring representational coupling via the Coupling Amplification Factor (CAF = JSD_cond / JSD_baseline), where CAF < 1 indicates homogenization and CAF > 1 indicates diversification. In controlled GPT-4o experiments (N=30, ~9,900 API calls), we measure coupling in text and image communication. Key findings: (1) text communication causes significant homogenization (CAF=0.803 [0.740, 0.873], d=1.30, p<0.001), confirmed by no-communication ablation and prompt-perturbation controls; (2) image communication also homogenizes under within-modality baselines (CAF=0.834 [0.811, 0.858]), with comparable proportional effect; (3) group size moderates coupling direction -- K=5 produces homogenization while K=3 yields CAF > 1.0 (point estimates 1.14 and 1.06, CI pending), suggesting a directional shift toward diversification; (4) cross-model replication shows extreme variation (CAF 0.034-0.803), with DeepSeek dominated by format artifacts; (5) coupling is stateless -- driven by prompt context rather than cumulative updating, with continuous consensus producing monotonic convergence. These results establish LLM agent coupling as real, measurable, and controllable at the prompt level, with direct implications for multi-agent system design.

</details>

*Saoud Aldowaish,Yashwanth Karumanchi,Kai-Chen Chiang,Mohammed Ayman Habib,Finn Murphy,Rishen Cao,Morteza Fayazi*

Abstract: Recent advances in Artificial Intelligence (AI) have revolutionized Electronic Design Automation (EDA), particularly through Large Language Models (LLMs) for circuit design tasks. However, their application to analog and mixed-signal domains remains limited by the lack of machine-readable representations of existing circuit design knowledge. Circuit schematic images found in research manuscripts, textbooks, and websites constitute a vast repository of validated designs; however, these visual representations cannot be directly processed by EDA tools. Converting them into machine-readable netlists is essential for enabling simulation, verification, and building comprehensive databases for AI-based models. Current conversion methods lack generalization across both Integrated Circuit (IC) and Printed Circuit Board (PCB) level schematics. Moreover, they struggle with component recognition and connectivity inference, and fail to distinguish between connected junctions and crossing wires. In this paper, we propose SINA, an open-source circuit schematic image-to-netlist generator. SINA is a fully automated pipeline that integrates deep learning for robust component detection, connected-component labeling for accurate connectivity inference, Optical Character Recognition (OCR) for component reference designator extraction, and a Vision-Language Model (VLM) for reliable reference designator assignment. SINA handles both IC- and PCB-level schematics and incorporates dedicated crossing-wires detection to differentiate wire intersections from connections. We validate the correctness of the generated netlists using graph isomorphism techniques. Our experiments demonstrate an overall netlist generation accuracy of 96.67%, which is 2.72x higher compared to state-of-the-art approaches.

### [254] [DeadPool: Resilient LLM Training with Hot-Swapping via Zero-Overhead Checkpoint](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01646)
*Haotian Xie,Junlin Chen,Mingkai Zheng,Lishan Yang,Zhao Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DeadPool提出一种用于大规模语言模型训练的容错机制，通过热插拔方式在不中断任务的情况下替换故障节点。该机制利用内存中的非关键路径检查点实现空间冗余，并引入通信器重构协议实现实时替换。在无故障运行时，检查点与计算重叠，实现零开销；发生永久性节点故障时，可基于内存检查点快速恢复，仅需少量重新计算。在最多512个NVIDIA A100 GPU和650亿参数模型上评估，验证了其零开销运行与40秒内完成恢复的能力，同时满足低延迟与低开销的优化目标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大模型训练依赖数万GPU运行数月，面临软硬件栈中频繁故障问题。现有容错机制要么在无故障时引入显著开销，要么在出现永久性故障时恢复延迟高，难以兼顾高效执行与快速恢复。因此需要一种既能零开销运行又能快速恢复的容错方案。

Method: DeadPool采用两种核心设计：一是基于非关键路径的内存检查点机制，实现空间冗余并避免对主计算路径的影响；二是动态通信器重构协议，支持运行时将故障节点替换为备用节点。检查点与计算并行执行，确保正常运行无额外开销；故障后利用内存检查点快速重建状态，最小化重算成本。

Result: 在512个A100 GPU规模和650亿参数模型上测试，DeadPool实现了无检查点开销的稳定运行，且在节点永久故障后可在40秒内完成热插拔恢复，显著优于传统方法。

Conclusion: DeadPool成功实现了大模型训练中零开销的故障容忍与极低恢复延迟，突破了现有容错机制在性能与可靠性之间的权衡瓶颈，为大规模分布式训练提供了高效可靠的解决方案。

Abstract: State-of-the-art large language model (LLM) training takes tens of thousands of graphics processing units (GPUs) for months and encounters failures across the software and hardware stack. Existing fault-tolerance mechanisms either impose non-trivial overhead during failure-free execution or suffer from prolonged recovery latency, particularly under scenarios where a small subset of compute nodes experience permanent failures. %The tradeoff between failure-free overhead and recovery latency forms a space forms a Pareto frontier We present DeadPool to simultaneously address both optimization objectives. DeadPool incorporates a fault-tolerance mechanism that restores LLM training via hot-swapping, namely by replacing failed nodes with spare nodes without terminating the complete job. The hot-swapping of DeadPool is enabled by two ideas: First, it exploits an off-critical-path in-memory checkpointing mechanism for spatial redundancy. Second, it introduces a communicator reconstruction protocol that replaces failed nodes with spare nodes at runtime. DeadPool efficiently overlaps the in-memory checkpointing with computation, thus introducing zero overhead during error-free execution. Upon permanent node failures, DeadPool can rebuild memory states with minimal recomputation by leveraging in-memory checkpoints. We evaluate DeadPool across scales (up to 512 NVIDIA A100 GPUs) and LLMs (up to 65B parameters), and observe zero checkpoint overhead with hot-swapping recovery completing in under 40 seconds. These results show that DeadPool simultaneously achieves both zero-overhead error-free execution and extremely low recovery cost.

</details>


### [255] [CALM: Interpretable Cross-Modal Alignment for Biomarker Discovery from Unpaired Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01656)
*Jueqi Wang,Zachary Jacokes,John Darrell Van Horn,Kevin A. Pelphrey,Michael C. Schatz,Archana Venkataraman*

Main category: cs.LG

Motivation: 大多数大规模脑科学研究数据为单模态（仅神经影像或遗传数据），缺乏跨模态整合能力，限制了对脑结构与遗传因素交互作用的理解。因此需要一种方法能够在不依赖配对数据的情况下，从独立人群中挖掘脑区与遗传通路之间的可解释关系。

Method: CALM通过线性投影将影像和遗传数据映射到共享潜在空间，优化目标包括匹配类条件潜在分布和保证群体可分离性，从而实现跨模态对齐，并提取可解释的通路-脑区关联。

Conclusion: CALM成功实现了在无配对样本条件下，利用大规模单模态数据挖掘脑结构与遗传通路间的可解释关联，为跨模态脑疾病研究提供了新范式，具备良好的泛化与稳定性。

Abstract: The interaction between brain structure and genetic influences is key to understanding neuropsychiatric disorders. However, most large-scale datasets are unimodal, providing either neuroimaging or genetics data. We propose CALM, a framework that learns interpretable associations between brain ROIs and genetic pathways from completely disjoint populations. CALM aligns the two modalities in a shared latent space via linear projections that simultaneously match the class-conditional latent distributions and ensure group separability. These projections provide interpretable pathway--ROI associations. When trained on unimodal imaging and genetics datasets, CALM generalizes to an unseen paired dataset, outperforming several state-of-the-art methods and ablation baselines. We also demonstrate stability of the learned associations against a paired baseline. Our experiments on autism spectrum disorder reveal immune and metabolic pathways linked to specific cortical regions and are consistent with established literature. Thus, CALM opens the door to leveraging large unimodal repositories for studying cross-modal interactions in brain disorders across disparate datasets.

### [256] [Message Passing Based Two-Timescale Bayesian Learning for Joint Channel and Memory Hardware Impairments Tracking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01660)
*Wei Xu,An Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于消息传递的双时尺度贝叶斯深度学习框架（MP-TTBDL），结合残差循环门控单元（RGRU）建模硬件失真在符号内的时间记忆特性，实现信道与硬件失真的联合跟踪。针对信道快速变化与硬件失真缓慢漂移的物理时尺度差异，分别采用马尔可夫先验和高斯马尔可夫先验建模，并通过多时隙因子图构建消息传递算法。其中，跨时隙消息采用闭式更新，而因递归结构复杂的时隙内因子图被分解为信道跟踪模块（使用Turbo-OAMP）与失真校准模块（使用深度近似消息传递DAMP），两者通过期望传播（EP）迭代交换外信息直至收敛。仿真表明，该方法在不同在线失真场景与信噪比条件下均显著优于传统补偿+估计方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 硬件失真导致大规模MIMO接收机中符号间记忆和元素间耦合，严重损害信道估计性能；传统方法难以有效分离快速变化的信道与缓慢漂移的硬件失真，亟需兼顾时域动态特性的联合建模与跟踪机制。

Method: 提出MP-TTBDL框架，利用RGRU建模硬件失真内在时序依赖；设计双时尺度先验（快变马尔可夫先验用于稀疏信道，慢变高斯马尔可夫先验用于网络参数）；基于多时隙因子图构建消息传递算法，将时隙内结构分解为信道跟踪（Turbo-OAMP）与失真校准（DAMP）模块，通过期望传播迭代更新。

Result: 所提框架在多种在线失真场景和不同信噪比下均表现出更低的信道估计误差，显著优于传统补偿-估计流程，在复杂动态环境中具备更强鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 该研究成功实现了对高速时变信道与慢速漂移硬件失真的高效联合追踪，验证了双时尺度贝叶斯深度学习与消息传递机制在实际系统中的有效性，为未来智能无线接收机的设计提供了新思路。

Abstract: Hardware impairments in massive multiple-input multiple-output (MIMO) receivers introduce inter-symbol memory and inter-element coupling, severely degrading channel estimation. This paper employs a residual recurrent gated unit (RGRU) to model the intra-slot memory of the hardware impairments and proposes a message-passing-based two-timescale Bayesian deep learning (MP-TTBDL) framework for joint channel and impairment tracking. Owing to small-scale fading, the wireless channel varies rapidly across slots, whereas hardware impairments drift slowly due to hardware aging and environmental variations. To capture these distinct physical timescales, a fastvarying Markov prior and a slow-varying Gaussian Markov prior are assigned to the sparse channel and the network parameters, respectively. Based on a multi-slot factor graph formulation, a message-passing algorithm is developed. Specifically, the inter-slot messages admit closed-form updates, while the intra-slot factor graph, due to its complex recurrent structure, is partitioned into a channel tracking module and an impairments calibration module. The channel tracking module performs sparse channel estimation via turbo orthogonal approximate message passing (Turbo-OAMP), and the impairments calibration module updates the impairment parameters via a specially designed deep approximate message passing (DAMP) procedure, with the two modules iteratively exchanging extrinsic information through expectation propagation (EP) until convergence. Simulation results show that the proposed framework robustly achieves lower channel estimation error than conventional compensators followed by channel estimation across different online impairment scenarios and signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) conditions.

Method: 提出两种FTRL型算法：一种用于全信息设置，另一种用于带货设置。通过利用FTRL的对偶更新机制，结合压缩通信下的平均一致性技术，实现高效且低通信开销的分布式优化。

Abstract: Decentralized online convex optimization (D-OCO) is a popular framework for distributed applications with streaming data. To tackle the communication bottleneck, previous studies have investigated D-OCO with compressed communication and proposed several algorithms that are variants of online gradient descent (OGD). However, for D-OCO with exact communication, the best existing algorithms are variants of follow-the-regularized-leader (FTRL). In this paper, for the first time, we propose two FTRL-type algorithms for D-OCO with compressed communication. Compared with OGD-type algorithms, our algorithms are more elegant in both algorithmic design and theoretical analysis. The key insight is that the dual update mechanism of FTRL allows us to make a simple application of the technique for average consensus with communication compression. More specifically, our first algorithm considers the full-information setting, and can match the existing regret bounds. Our second algorithm is designed for the bandit setting, and can significantly improve both the regret bounds and communication costs of existing algorithms.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出物理先验估计器构建站点校准的物理先验，结合站点条件单调扭曲与共享物理功率曲线；引入物理上界约束形成软包络；设计隐状态编码器建模运行状态嵌入，并通过状态感知功率修正器实现知识引导的监督状态路由与分状态专家修正。

Abstract: Day-ahead wind power forecasting is essential for cost-effective power-system operation. It is primarily driven by future meteorological conditions while retaining temporal dependencies in power generation. In practice, observed wind-farm power often entangles physically available power with local environmental effects and latent operational states, such as shutdowns and curtailment. Existing physical models provide useful constraints but adapt poorly across wind farms, whereas data-driven models can capture rich correlations but often conflate meteorological effects with state-induced deviations. In this study, we propose UniWind, a wind power forecasting model based on physics-informed state routing. UniWind first employs a Physical Prior Estimator to construct a site-calibrated physical prior by combining site-conditioned monotonic warping with a shared physical power curve. It further applies a physical upper-bound constraint to shape this prior as a soft envelope of available wind power generation. UniWind then proposes a Latent State Encoder to model operating-state embeddings and transforms the physical prior into final power forecasts through a State-aware Power Corrector, which uses knowledge-guided supervised state routing and bounded, state-specific expert correction. Full-shot and cross-farm zero-shot experiments on more than 20 real-world datasets demonstrate the accuracy and robustness of UniWind.

### [259] [SCAPE: Accurate and Efficient LLM Training with Extreme Sparse Communication](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01678)
*Mingkai Zheng,Junlin Chen,Haotian Xie,Zhao Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SCAPE是一种针对大语言模型训练的通信高效分布式优化器，通过利用AdamS的一阶矩稳定性，实现高稀疏度下的稳定通信压缩。它基于一阶矩统计生成稀疏掩码，跨工作节点分区掩码生成，并延迟掩码使用以实现通信与计算重叠。同时，仅需一个同步的稀疏缓冲区即可重构二阶矩更新所需数据，避免额外集合操作。在Megatron-LM中实现并测试，SCAPE在GPT-345M和Llama-500M上保持90%和99%稀疏度下的训练稳定性与模型质量；在Llama-500M上将预训练时间减少43.3%，在Llama-1.8B上每步加速达3.26倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有通信压缩方法如梯度稀疏化在高稀疏度下对Adam-style优化器不稳定，而量化通信受限于位宽且常引入额外开销。为解决大规模语言模型训练中通信成本过高的问题，需要一种既能大幅减少通信量又不影响模型质量的高效优化策略。

Method: SCAPE基于一阶矩统计生成稀疏掩码，而非原始梯度；掩码生成在工作节点间分片以匹配优化器分片；延迟掩码使用一步以实现通信与计算重叠；通过单一同步稀疏缓冲区重构二阶矩更新所需信息，避免额外集体通信操作。

Result: 在GPT-345M和Llama-500M上，SCAPE在90%和99%稀疏度下仍保持训练稳定性、验证损失和下游任务准确率；在Llama-500M上端到端预训练时间减少43.3%；在Llama-1.8B上每步速度提升达3.26倍，且模型质量与密集AdamW和AdamS相当。

Conclusion: SCAPE通过创新的稀疏掩码生成机制与通信重叠设计，在不牺牲模型质量的前提下显著降低大规模语言模型预训练中的通信开销，实现了高效的分布式训练，具有实际部署价值。

Abstract: Communication increasingly dominates the cost of Large Language Model (LLM) pre-training, especially under data-parallel and sharded training schemes, where gradient synchronization and parameter reconstruction overhead increase with model size and system scale. Existing communication-reduction methods either sparsify raw gradients, which can be unstable for modern Adam-style optimizers at high sparsity, or quantize communication, whose savings are fundamentally bounded by bit width and often incur additional runtime overhead. We present SCAPE, a communication-efficient distributed optimizer for LLM training that exploits the stability of AdamS's first-moment to enable aggressive sparsification without loss of LLM quality. Instead of constructing masks from raw gradients, SCAPE derives them from first-moment-based statistics, partitions mask generation across workers to align with optimizer sharding, and delays mask usage by one step so that mask synchronization can overlap with computation. SCAPE also reconstructs the quantities required for second-moment updates from a single synchronized sparse buffer, avoiding an additional collective. We implement SCAPE in Megatron-LM and evaluate its convergence by pre-training GPT-345M on OpenWebText and Llama-500M on SlimPajama-6B using 32 NVIDIA GH200 GPUs on TACC Vista. In both models, SCAPE preserves training stability, validation loss, and downstream task accuracy under 90\% and 99\% sparsity. For Llama-500M, SCAPE reduces end-to-end pre-training wall-clock time by up to 43.3\% while maintaining model quality comparable to dense AdamW and AdamS. For Llama-1.8B, SCAPE achieves up to 3.26$\times$ speedup per step compared to dense AdamS.

### [260] [WARP: Weight-Space Analysis for Recovering Training Data Portfolios](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01686)
*Tzu-Heng Huang,Aditya Goyal,John Cooper,Frederic Sala*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: WARP 是一种用于推断基础模型训练数据混合比例的框架，通过模型合并生成伪检查点，利用几何特征映射到领域比例，可在 BERT 和 GPT-2 上实现低至 0.046 和 0.104 的平均绝对误差，优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基础模型训练数据配方（如领域混合权重）通常不公开，导致研究者无法了解模型训练分布，存在信息不对称问题；现有方法如成员推理仅能检测单个样本，无法刻画训练语料库的整体组成。

Method: WARP 通过模型合并在基础模型与微调模型之间生成伪检查点，模拟训练轨迹，提取权重空间中的几何特征，并使用参数无关的 softmax 或训练过的 MLP 投影器将特征映射为领域比例。

Result: 在 BERT 和 GPT-2 的受控实验中，WARP 对领域混合比例的恢复平均 MAE 分别达到 0.046 和 0.104，优于成员推理和基于真实训练轨迹的变体。

Conclusion: WARP 能有效从已发布的模型权重中推断出训练数据的混合比例，揭示了模型训练分布的几何足迹，为理解模型训练过程提供了新工具。

Abstract: Foundation models are routinely released to the public, yet the data recipes used to train them -- such as domain mixture weights that determine how different sources are sampled -- are rarely disclosed. This creates an access asymmetry: researchers study the resulting models but lack visibility into the training distribution that produces them. Prior works for inferring training data, such as membership inference, detect at the level of individual samples and thus cannot characterize the global composition of the training corpus. We introduce WARP, a framework that recovers a fine-tuned model's training mixtures directly from its released weights. WARP interpolates between the base and fine-tuned models using model merging, generating pseudo-checkpoints that approximate the missing training trajectory and expose a geometric footprint of the training data in the weight space. From these simulated footprints, WARP extracts geometric features and maps them to domain proportions using either a parameter-free softmax readout or an MLP projector trained on synthetic mixtures. In controlled experiments with BERT and GPT-2, WARP recovers domain mixtures with an average MAE as low as 0.046 and 0.104 respectively, outperforming membership inference and a variant with access to the true training trajectory.

### [261] [Model Merging as Probabilistic Inference in Fine-Tuning Parameter Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01689)
*Long Minh Bui,Tuan Anh Le Van,Tung Phi Duc,Phi Le Nguyen,Jana Doppa,Trong Nghia Hoang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有模型合并方法基于局部解空间的几何性质，但难以有效评估各任务更新方向在跨任务合并中的统计价值；同时，其隐含的高斯假设与实际残差的重尾特性不匹配，导致性能受限。

Method: 将每个单任务模型视为能量基专家模型（EBM），在产品专家（PoE）框架下进行模型合并；设计基于柯西分布的重尾专家模型以更准确建模残差分布，并提出可证明收敛的推断算法。

Result: 在多种任务和模型架构上，所提方法显著优于当前主流基线，尤其在处理非高斯、重尾残差时表现更优。

Conclusion: 通过引入重尾分布的PoE-EBM框架，本文提供了更符合实际残差分布特性的模型合并方法，提升了合并效果与理论可靠性。

Abstract: Model merging aims to combine existing single-task solutions into a multi-task solution without additional data-driven fine-tuning.~Most existing approaches achieve this using geometric properties of local solution spaces. However, such geometric views provide limited guidance for scoring how statistically useful each task-specific update direction is across tasks during merging. To address this, we formulate model merging from a new perspective of probabilistic inference under a product-of-experts (PoE) scenario where each single-task solution defines an energy-based expert model (EBM) over the merged parameters. We show that several existing model merging methods arise as special cases of our framework under energy designs that impose implicit Gaussian assumptions on directional residuals between merged and task-specific models. Empirically, we find that these residuals are often heavy-tailed which exposes a mismatch with the imposed light-tailed Gaussian structures. We address this with a heavy-tailed PoE design based on Cauchy experts, which better captures the observed residual behavior while admitting a provably convergent inference procedure. Experiments across multiple tasks and architectures show significant improvements over state-of-the-arts baselines. Our code is available at https://github.com/MinhLong210/PoE-EBM-Merging.git.

### [262] [A Mathematical Introduction to Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01693)
*Jianfeng Lu*

<details>

Method: 采用分层结构：首先建立核心概念与完整证明；其次在简化假设下展示代表性估计；最后陈述研究级定理并给出证明思路。内容基于概率论基础，逐步引入复杂概念。

Result: 成功构建了一个逻辑清晰、层次分明的扩散模型理论框架，使初学者能够循序渐进地理解该领域的关键思想与技术。

Conclusion: 本文为扩散模型提供了严谨而可读的数学导引，特别适合没有先验知识的研究生学习，有助于奠定坚实的理论基础。

Abstract: These notes give a proof-oriented introduction to diffusion models from the viewpoint of sampling, tracing a single arc from classical sampling dynamics to modern diffusion samplers, their error analysis, and inference-time control. Throughout, the material is layered into core definitions and identities proved in full, representative estimates proved under simplifying assumptions, and research-level theorems stated with a proof roadmap. The intended audience is beginning graduate students with a background in probability but no prior exposure to stochastic differential equations, stochastic numerics, or diffusion models.

### [263] [Frequency Shift Physics-Informed Extreme Learning Machine for Solving High-Frequency Partial Differential Equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01694)
*Xiong Xiong,Ruonan Zhai,Zheng Zeng,Sheng Zhou,Rongchun Hu,Zichen Deng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种新的FS-PIELM框架，通过频率偏移机制解决神经网络在求解高频偏微分方程时的谱偏差问题。该方法通过平移高斯权重分布的均值而非缩放，避免了方差放大，保持计算效率并提升对高频解的建模能力。实验表明其在七项基准测试中六次表现最佳，精度提升达1至近5个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统神经网络存在谱偏差，难以有效学习高频解，尤其是在物理信息机器学习中求解高频率偏微分方程时表现不佳。现有方法多采用缩放权重方式引入频率，但易导致方差增长失控。

Method: 提出频率偏移物理信息极端学习机（FS-PIELM），采用加性机制调整权重初始化：将高斯权重分布的均值进行平移，固定方差为1，避免缩放带来的方差放大；设计两种变体：独立频率分配（FS-PIELM-L）与分组频率共享（FS-PIELM-G），以平衡性能与鲁棒性。

Result: 理论分析表明，新方法下频率方差始终有界且趋近于1，不受目标频率影响；实验在七类方程（包括赫尔姆霍兹、波动、泊松等）和复杂几何上验证，线性版本在六项任务中精度领先，相较现有PIELM方法提升1至近5个数量级。

Conclusion: FS-PIELM通过创新的频率偏移初始化策略，有效缓解了谱偏差问题，在保持极端学习机高效性的同时显著提升了对高频偏微分方程的求解精度，具有广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: Solving partial differential equations (PDEs) with high-frequency solutions remains a central challenge in physics-informed machine learning due to spectral bias -- the tendency of neural networks to learn low-frequency components preferentially. This paper proposes a Frequency Shift Physics-Informed Extreme Learning Machine (FS-PIELM) framework that addresses this limitation through an additive mechanism for weight initialization. Rather than multiplying random weights by a scaling factor, the method translates the mean of the Gaussian weight distribution while keeping the variance fixed at unity, thereby avoiding the variance amplification inherent in scaling-based methods. Two variants are developed: FS-PIELM-L assigns independent frequency magnitudes to individual neurons, while FS-PIELM-G groups neurons for improved robustness. Theoretical analysis shows that the frequency variance under the proposed framework remains bounded and approaches unity regardless of target frequency, in contrast to the quadratic growth of conventional approaches. The method preserves the computational efficiency of extreme learning machines, requiring only a single linear solve. Experiments on seven benchmark problems spanning six equation types -- Helmholtz, wave, Poisson, Klein-Gordon, heat, and advection-diffusion -- on both regular and complex geometries show that the linear variant achieves the best accuracy in six of seven cases, with improvements of one to nearly five orders of magnitude over existing PIELM variants. The code and data accompanying this manuscript will be made publicly available at https://github.com/xgxgnpu/Physics-informed-vibe-coding/tree/main/FS-PIELM.

</details>


### [264] [Predicting Closed-Loop Performance of Latent World Models: Offline Checkpoint Selection for MPC and Model-Based RL Under Non-Markovian Rewards in LunarLander](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01736)
*Nikolai Smolyanskiy*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究如何仅通过验证阶段的诊断指标来预测学习到的潜在世界模型在下游闭环任务中的表现。针对世界模型训练中选择最佳检查点的难题，提出一套基于最优控制理论的结构化验证诊断方法，并应用于带有奖励塑形的LunarLander v3环境。通过40个指标与基于CEM-MPC回报的黄金标准对比，发现奖励可观察性分数（ROF）是最强的单一预测指标。进一步将ROF与三个结构正则化项结合，形成综合评分CROF，用于离线检查点选择。使用CROF选出的模型训练出的MB-A2C策略在返回值上比公平评估的MF-A2C基线高出约24.5分，且仅需约65倍更少的真实环境交互次数；该模型还能驱动强大的零样本CEM-MPC策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在世界模型训练过程中，验证损失和多步预测均方根误差持续下降，但闭环性能可能早已崩溃，导致无法通过传统验证指标准确选择最优检查点。因此需要一种能反映闭环性能的验证阶段诊断工具。

Method: 基于最优控制理论设计一系列结构化验证诊断指标；在LunarLander v3环境中训练RSSM世界模型；以每检查点的CEM-MPC回报作为闭环性能的黄金标准；评估40个指标与该标准的相关性；提取最强预测因子——奖励可观察性分数（ROF）；结合三个结构正则化项构建复合指标CROF，用于离线检查点选择。

Result: ROF是最佳单一预测指标；结合正则化项形成的CROF能有效筛选出高性能检查点；基于CROF选择的模型所训练的模型基A2C策略优于模型自由基线约24.5回报点，且交互次数减少约65倍；同一模型亦能成功驱动零样本CEM-MPC策略。

Conclusion: 通过引入结构化验证诊断，特别是奖励可观察性分数（ROF）及其组合形式CROF，可以有效解决世界模型训练中检查点选择的难题，显著提升模型在真实环境中的闭环性能，同时大幅降低对真实环境交互的需求。

Abstract: We study how to predict the downstream closed-loop performance of a learned latent world model from validation-time diagnostics alone. Choosing the right checkpoint from a world-model training run is difficult: validation loss and multi-step prediction RMSE keep improving long after closed-loop performance has collapsed. We present a suite of structural validation-time diagnostics drawn from optimal-control theory and apply them to Gymnasium's LunarLander v3, which features shaped rewards. We train an RSSM [5, 4] world model on it and treat per checkpoint CEM-MPC return as the oracle for closed-loop quality. By evaluating 40 metrics against this oracle, we find that the strongest single predictor is the Reward Observability Fraction (ROF), which measures the reward predictor's dependence on the observable subspace. We combine ROF with three structural regularizers into a single-number offline checkpoint selection score, the Composite Reward Observability Fraction (CROF). The CROF-selected world model trains a model-based A2C policy that beats a fairly evaluated model-free A2C baseline by ~24.5 return points while using ~65x fewer real-environment interactions, and the same world model also drives a strong zero-shot CEM-MPC policy. Code and data: https://github.com/nsmoly/LunarLander_RSSM.

### [265] [Finite-Lag Operator Geometry of Recurrent Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01746)
*Kanishka Reddy*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出有限滞后算子几何框架，用于分析递归隐藏状态的轨迹特性。通过条件传输律 $Q_Δ(dy\mid x)$ 和源中心传输张量 $G_Δ$，分解出条件扩散与相干位移，并引入反对称坐标循环 $W_Δ^ρ$ 揭示滞后的定向流动。理论证明了仿射协变性、估计器稳定性及有限滞后分离性，线性高斯模型提供了可解析校准形式。实验验证了分解、循环、协方差与稳定性预测。在重复复制网络中，揭示了架构对总传输尺度和相干位移的依赖性，而相干位移占比受度量与分辨率影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法多基于静态快照测量表示几何，难以捕捉递归系统的动态轨迹特征。本文旨在建立一种基于观测源-后继对 $(X_t,X_{t+Δ})$ 的有限滞后算子几何框架，以更准确刻画递归隐藏状态的动态演化行为。

Method: 提出基于密集高斯源平滑算子估计条件传输律 $Q_Δ(dy\mid x)$，构建源中心传输张量 $G_Δ$ 与反对称坐标循环 $W_Δ^ρ$，实现对条件扩散与相干位移的精确分解，并推导其在仿射变换下的不变性质与稳定估计条件。

Result: 理论证明了仿射协变性、估计器稳定性与有限滞后分离性；线性高斯模型提供闭式解；实验验证了分解结构、循环效应、协方差与稳定性预测；在重复复制网络中发现架构影响总传输尺度与相干位移，而相干位移占比受度量与分辨率调节。

Conclusion: 该框架有效捕捉递归系统中的确定性运动模式，超越传统无穷小柯西-查姆几何，为理解深度递归网络中的动态表示提供新工具。

Abstract: Recurrent representations are trajectories, but representation geometry is often measured from static snapshots. We develop finite-lag operator geometry for recurrent hidden states from observed source-successor pairs $(X_t,X_{t+Δ})$. The primitive is the conditional transport law $Q_Δ(dy\mid x)$, estimated by a dense Gaussian source-smoothing operator. From this directed finite-lag law we derive a source-centered transport tensor $G_Δ$, which decomposes exactly into conditional spread and coherent displacement, and an antisymmetric coordinate circulation $W_Δ^ρ$, which summarizes directed lagged flow. We prove affine covariance with explicit metric dependence of scalar summaries, dense estimator stability on bounded trajectory clouds, and a finite-lag separation result showing that source-centered transport detects deterministic recurrent motion not recorded by infinitesimal carre-du-champ geometry. A linear-Gaussian closed form calibrates the quantities in terms of the update $A_Δ$, source covariance, and innovation covariance. Controlled experiments validate the decomposition, circulation, covariance, and stability predictions. In performance matched repeat-copy networks, the framework reveals architecture dependent differences in total transport scale and coherent displacement trace, while coherent displacement fraction is metric and resolution dependent.

### [266] [Efficient Temporal Point Processes via Monotone Alternating Splines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01752)
*Cheng Wan,Quyu Kong,Feng Zhou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种名为单调交替样条（MAS）的新框架，用于改进时间点过程（TPPs）中累积条件强度函数（CCIF）的建模。现有方法依赖单调神经网络（MNNs），但存在凸性限制、饱和问题和不满足CCIF建模要求等结构性缺陷，限制了其对复杂时间动态的表达能力。MAS通过分离插值与外推组件，实现了灵活高效的CCIF建模，在理论上兼具高拟合精度与强泛化能力，显著减少了MNNs的不可约近似误差。实验表明，MAS在合成与真实数据集上均表现更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于单调神经网络（MNNs）的累积条件强度函数（CCIF）建模方法存在凸性限制、饱和问题及违反CCIF建模要求等结构性缺陷，导致其对复杂时间动态的表达能力受限，亟需新的建模范式以提升性能与灵活性。

Method: 提出单调交替样条（MAS）框架，利用分离的插值与外推组件，实现对CCIF的灵活且高效建模。插值部分保证高精度拟合，外推部分增强泛化能力，从而克服MNNs的固有局限。

Result: 在多个合成与真实世界数据集上的实验结果表明，MAS显著优于现有方法，在建模精度与泛化能力方面均取得优越表现。

Conclusion: MAS通过创新的结构设计有效解决了传统MNNs在CCIF建模中的三大结构性瓶颈，为时间点过程提供了更强大、灵活且高效的建模工具，具有广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: Temporal point processes (TPPs) have widespread applications across various domains. Compared to modeling the conditional intensity of a TPP, modeling its cumulative conditional intensity function (CCIF) improves computational efficiency and eliminates numerical approximation errors. However, current CCIF parameterizations uniformly rely on Monotone Neural Networks (MNNs), which we identify as suffering from three structural deadlocks--convexity restrictions, saturation limits, and violations of CCIF modeling requirements--that fundamentally restrict their representational capacity for complex temporal dynamics. To resolve these bottlenecks, this paper proposes a novel framework called Monotone Alternating Splines (MAS). By leveraging distinct interpolation and extrapolation components, MAS provides a flexible and efficient framework for modeling CCIFs. Theoretically, MAS's interpolation provides strong fitting accuracy, while its extrapolation supports robust generalization, reducing the irreducible approximation gaps of MNNs. Extensive experiments show that MAS achieves superior performance on both synthetic and real-world datasets.

### [267] [Role-Aware Neural Convex Divergence Heads for Asymmetric Representation Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01762)
*He Huang,Lu Shen,Yunfeng Huang,Li Qi*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准的欧几里得、余弦和马氏距离是对称的，而通用神经评分器虽能建模方向性但缺乏几何结构；因此需要一种既能捕捉方向性又具备良好几何结构的模型。

Method: 提出角色感知的神经凸散度头，先进行源角色和目标角色投影，再计算输入-凸神经Bregman散度，生成非负结构化得分，并分析其投影空间性质、源角色凸性、方向间隙分解及海森矩阵局部曲率。

Result: 在多个基准测试中（包括词汇、句子、本体和有向图），所提方法在十次随机种子实验中均优于普通ICNN-Bregman头，在方向准确性和结构可解释性上表现更佳；但在固定特征的引文预测任务中，对称或双曲基线仍更优。

Conclusion: 所提头可视为一个结构化且可解释的插件式距离模块，特别适合方向性关系建模任务。

Abstract: Many representation learning problems involve directed relations, such as lexical entailment, sentence entailment, ontology hierarchy, and citation links. Standard Euclidean, cosine, and Mahalanobis heads are symmetric, while generic neural scorers can model directionality but provide limited geometric structure. This paper proposes a role-aware neural convex divergence head for asymmetric representation learning. The head applies source- and target-role projections before evaluating an input-convex neural Bregman divergence, yielding a nonnegative structured score in the role-projected space. We characterize its projected-space identity, source-role convexity, directional-gap decomposition, and Hessian-based local curvature. Experiments on lexical, sentence, ontology, and directed graph benchmarks compare symmetric distances, unstructured asymmetric scorers, order/hyperbolic baselines, plain ICNN-Bregman heads, and the proposed role-aware variant. Across ten random seeds on the main semantic and ontology benchmarks, role-aware projections consistently improve directional accuracy over plain ICNN-Bregman heads while preserving zero observed negative divergence rate. The results also identify a boundary case: on large fixed-feature citation prediction, specialized symmetric or hyperbolic baselines remain stronger in ranking accuracy. Overall, the proposed head is best understood as a structured and interpretable plug-in distance module for tasks where directional relations matter.

### [268] [Denser $\neq$ Better: Limits of On-Policy Self-Distillation for Continual Post-Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01763)
*Meng Wang,Haohan Zhao,Wenzhuo Liu,Lu Yang,Geng Liu,Haiyang Guo,Guo-Sen Xie,Gaofeng Meng,Hongbin Liu,Fei Zhu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了持续后训练中基于自蒸馏的策略优化（SDPO）的有效性。实验表明，当教师信号稳定且对齐时，SDPO可加速领域内专业化，但在分布外场景下表现不佳，易导致遗忘甚至模型崩溃；相比之下，GRPO等基于策略梯度的强化学习方法更保守，更能保留已有能力。分析指出，密集自蒸馏会引发参数空间和响应空间的较大偏移，并通过师生循环放大高频格式错误。结论是：仅靠在线数据不足以支撑持续学习，密集自蒸馏虽在特定条件下有效，但不应作为持续后训练的默认稳定机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决基础模型在持续后训练中面临的知识遗忘问题，探索自蒸馏策略优化（SDPO）是否能有效缓解遗忘并提升持续学习性能。

Method: 提出自蒸馏策略优化（SDPO），通过在线策略学习与自蒸馏结合的方式进行持续后训练，并对比其与GRPO等强化学习方法在不同场景下的表现。

Result: SDPO在教师信号稳定、任务内场景下表现良好，能加速专业化；但在分布外场景下出现严重遗忘甚至模型崩溃；密集自蒸馏加剧参数与响应空间漂移，放大格式错误；而GRPO等方法更具鲁棒性，能更好保留旧知识。

Conclusion: 仅依赖在线数据和密集自蒸馏无法保障持续学习的稳定性；尽管在特定条件下有效，但应谨慎使用，不能视为默认的稳定策略。

Abstract: Continual post-training enables foundation models to acquire new knowledge while preserving existing capabilities. Recent work suggests that on-policy learning can mitigate forgetting, with on-policy self-distillation emerging as a particularly attractive approach. In this work, we revisit this optimistic view through self-distillation policy optimization (SDPO). Our experiments show that SDPO can accelerate in-domain specialization when teacher signals are stable and well aligned, but it struggles to generalize to out-of-distribution scenarios. In continual post-training, SDPO exhibits stronger forgetting and can even collapse, whereas on-policy reinforcement learning methods such as GRPO adapt more conservatively and better preserve prior capabilities. Further analyses reveal that denser self-distillation induces larger drift in both parameter space and response space, and can amplify high-frequency formatting artifacts through a self-reinforcing teacher--student loop. These findings suggest that on-policy data alone is insufficient for continual learning. Dense self-distillation can accelerate specialization when teacher targets are stable and token-level supervision is reliable, but it should not be treated as a default stabilizer for continual post-training. Our code is available at https://github.com/Moenupa/SDPO-CL.

### [269] [Set Diffusion: Interpolating Token Orderings Between Autoregression and Diffusion for Fast and Flexible Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01775)
*Marianne Arriola,Volodymyr Kuleshov*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Set diffusion introduces a novel language model framework that uses flexible-position, flexible-length token sets and a set-causal diffusion architecture, enabling faster inference, support for any-order decoding, and KV cache updates after each step. It outperforms prior diffusion models in speed-quality tradeoffs and excels in infilling tasks compared to block diffusion.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing discrete diffusion models are limited to fixed-length generation and lack KV caching support, while block diffusion suffers from rigid sequential blocks that hinder flexibility and parallelism. This work aims to overcome these limitations by enabling more flexible and efficient token generation.

Method: The paper proposes set diffusion, which factorizes likelihood over flexible-position, flexible-length token sets and employs a set-causal diffusion architecture allowing KV cache updates after every inference step. This enables arbitrarily-ordered token decoding, including sliding-window sets.

Result: Set diffusion achieves superior speed-quality tradeoffs on mathematical reasoning, summarization, and unconditional generation tasks compared to prior diffusion models. It also demonstrates stronger infilling performance than block diffusion.

Conclusion: Set diffusion provides a flexible, efficient, and high-performing alternative to existing diffusion-based language models, supporting advanced decoding strategies and better integration with caching mechanisms.

Abstract: Discrete diffusion models have steadily improved in quality relative to autoregressive (AR) models. However, these models are normally constrained to fixed-length generation and do not support key-value (KV) caching. Block diffusion partially bridges diffusion and AR by generating token blocks left-to-right, but its fixed-size sequential blocks limit decoding flexibility and parallelism. Here, we present a new class of language models, set diffusion, comprised of (i) a likelihood parameterization that factorizes over flexible-position, flexible-length token sets and (ii) a set-causal diffusion architecture that supports KV cache updates after every inference step. By factorizing over token sets instead of fixed-size blocks, tokens can be decoded in arbitrarily-ordered sets, including sliding-window sets, enabling faster inference and support for any-order decoding. Set diffusion achieves better speed-quality tradeoffs on mathematical reasoning, summarization, and unconditional generation compared to prior diffusion language models while offering stronger infilling performance than block diffusion. We provide the code, along with the model weights and blog post on the project page: https://m-arriola.com/setdlms/

</details>


### [270] [EHHN: An Event-driven Heterogeneous Hypergraph Network for Object-Centric Next Activity Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01785)
*Jiaxing Wang,Kaitao Chen,Zhubin Han,Chenyu Hou,Bin Cao,Jing Fan,Ji Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: EHHN 是一种用于对象中心的下一活动预测的事件驱动异构超图网络。它通过构建包含事件-对象超边和生命周期超边的异构超图来保留跨对象上下文，并采用双流架构分别建模事件驱动的对象状态演化和全局时间动态，最终融合预测下一活动。在四个公开的 OCEL 基准上优于九个基线模型，准确率和宏 F1 分数最高提升达 8.1 和 12.4 个百分点，且 GPU 内存占用降低最多达 24 倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在处理对象中心事件日志（OCEL）时，要么丢失跨对象上下文（如扁平化方法），要么仅通过成对关系表示多对象事件（如图模型），无法同时捕捉事件驱动的对象状态变化、事件间时间间隔以及全局执行模式。因此需要一种能联合建模这些复杂关系的新方法。

Method: 提出 EHHN 模型，将每个预测前缀表示为异构超图：事件-对象超边连接共同参与的多个对象，生命周期超边聚合主对象的生命周期事件。采用双流架构——微空间流建模事件驱动的对象状态演化，宏观演化流利用检索到的全局原型捕捉时间动态，最后融合两路信息进行下一活动预测。

Result: 在四个公共 OCEL 数据集上的实验表明，EHHN 在所有数据集上均达到最佳准确率和宏 F1 得分，相比最强基线提升最高达 8.1% 和 12.4%；与最强的 OCEL 原生图基线相比，峰值 GPU 内存使用减少最多 24 倍。

Conclusion: EHHN 有效解决了对象中心场景下多对象交互与复杂动态建模的挑战，显著提升了下一活动预测性能，同时大幅降低内存开销，为服务过程分析提供了高效且精准的新工具。

Abstract: Next activity prediction helps service-oriented processes anticipate upcoming steps before delays, exceptions, or service-level risks occur. Most existing methods assume classical single-case event logs, whereas real service processes often involve events shared by multiple typed business objects. Object-centric event logs (OCELs) capture such interactions, but current predictors remain limited. Flattening-based approaches lose cross-object context, and native OCEL graph-based approaches encode multi-object events through pairwise relations. Existing models also do not jointly capture event-driven object state changes, inter-event timing, and global execution patterns. We propose EHHN, an Event-driven Heterogeneous Hypergraph Network for object-centric next activity prediction. EHHN represents each prediction prefix as a heterogeneous hypergraph, where event--object hyperedges bind retained co-participating objects and a lifecycle hyperedge groups the primary object's observed lifecycle events. Based on this representation, EHHN uses a dual-stream architecture in which a micro-spatial stream models event-driven object-state evolution and a macro-evolution stream captures temporal dynamics using retrieved global prototypes. The two streams are fused to predict the next activity. Experiments on four public OCEL benchmarks against nine baselines show that EHHN achieves the best accuracy and macro F1-score on all datasets, with improvements of up to 8.1 and 12.4 percentage points over the strongest baselines. Compared with the strongest OCEL-native graph baseline, EHHN also reduces peak GPU memory by up to 24 times. Code is available at https://github.com/chenkaitao1112/EHHN.

</details>


### [271] [EPnG: Adaptive Expert Prune-and-Grow for Parameter-Efficient MoE Fine-tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01789)
*Ahin Lee,Sehyun Yun,Taesik Gong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: EPnG 是一种自适应的剪枝与增长框架，通过根据路由器门控概率推导的专家重要性重新分配 LoRA 容量，实现了对 MoE 模型的有效微调。它在保持固定参数预算的前提下，剪除低利用率专家并扩展高重要性专家，采用正交初始化进行秩增长，显著提升了资源利用效率。在 OLMoE 和 Qwen1.5-MoE 上，EPnG 在相同预算下优于 LoRA，性能接近全量微调，仅更新 0.55%-0.72% 的参数（减少 140x-180x），证明了将 PEFT 与 MoE 路由对齐可实现更高效、可扩展的微调策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有参数高效微调（PEFT）方法如 LoRA 忽略了 MoE 模型中的路由动态，导致资源利用不充分；同时，MoE 模型存在冗余专家和均匀参数分配问题，限制了其高效适应能力。因此需要一种能结合路由信息、动态调整专家权重和容量的微调方法。

Method: 提出 EPnG 框架，基于路由器门控概率评估专家重要性，动态剪裁低使用率专家，并对高重要性专家进行秩增长（rank growth）以扩展其表达能力，同时采用正交初始化保证稳定性，在固定参数预算下实现容量重分配。

Result: EPnG 在 OLMoE 与 Qwen1.5-MoE 上均优于同等参数预算下的 LoRA，性能接近全量微调，仅需更新 0.55%-0.72% 的参数，相比传统方法减少 140x-180x 的参数更新量。

Conclusion: 将参数高效微调与 MoE 路由机制对齐，能够显著提升模型微调的效率与效果，使 MoE 模型在保持低成本的同时实现更强的适应能力，是一种更具可扩展性的微调新范式。

Abstract: Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) models scale efficiently but remain costly to adapt due to redundant experts and uniform parameter allocation. Existing parameter-efficient fine-tuning (PEFT) methods such as LoRA ignore MoE routing dynamics, leading to suboptimal resource use. We propose EPnG, an adaptive prune-and-grow framework that reallocates LoRA capacity based on expert importance derived from router gate probabilities. EPnG prunes under-utilized experts and expands high-importance experts via rank growth with orthogonal initialization, while maintaining a fixed parameter budget. Across OLMoE and Qwen1.5-MoE, EPnG consistently outperforms LoRA under the same budget and achieves performance comparable to full fine-tuning while updating only 0.55%-0.72% of parameters (up to 140x-180x fewer). These results demonstrate that aligning PEFT with MoE routing yields a more effective and scalable fine-tuning strategy.

</details>


### [272] [Single-Channel EEG-Based Cognitive Load Assessment in Online Learning: A Hybrid Deep Learning Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01795)
*Rowan Hussein,Mohamed Ouf*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了使用消费级单通道EEG设备（NeuroSky MindWave Mobile 2）区分在线学习中简单与困难教育视频内容的可行性。基于公开数据集，采用CNN+LSTM+Attention混合模型结合原始波形与频带功率特征，在九名参与者中实现了最高78.5%的分类准确率，显著优于传统特征分类器（55%）。尽管正则化有效缓解了过拟合问题，但因样本量小，结果仍需谨慎解读。作者强调应以独立于被试的评估为标准，并发布可复现的评估流程。研究定位为可行性探索，配套提供开源工具，支持实时记录EEG、推理并生成认知负荷热图，辅助教师识别难点内容。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在远程学习环境中，缺乏课堂中的视觉线索使教师难以判断学生认知负荷水平。因此，亟需一种非侵入式方法自动监测学习过程中的认知负荷，以识别教学难点。

Result: 模型在被试内设置下达到最高78.5%的准确率，显著优于传统方法（55%）；正则化后验证准确率稳定在68%-73%之间；但因样本量小，主张以主体独立评估为更可靠标准。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了使用消费级EEG设备检测学习难度的可行性，但尚未达到可部署水平。建议未来工作优先采用主体独立评估，并推广开放工具以支持教育实践。

Abstract: Monitoring cognitive load during online learning could help instructors identify content that learners find difficult, but remote settings remove the visual cues that support this judgement in a classroom. We study whether a single-channel, consumer-grade EEG device (the NeuroSky MindWave Mobile 2) can distinguish easy from difficult educational-video content, using the publicly available dataset of Wang et al. [24] (ten learners, one excluded for excessive noise, leaving nine). We implement a hybrid CNN+LSTM+Attention model that combines the raw waveform with band-power features. In a within-subject setting, the model reaches up to 78.5% accuracy, compared with 55% for conventional feature-based classifiers; regularization (dropout and L2) closes the large gap between training and validation accuracy that we observe without it, keeping validation accuracy stable at roughly 68-73%. We are deliberately cautious about these numbers: with only nine subjects, within-subject evaluation is optimistic, and we argue that subject-independent evaluation -- in which no learner appears in both training and test data -- should be the standard for this task. To that end we release a reproducible evaluation pipeline. We frame the work as a feasibility study rather than a deployable system, and pair it with an open, notebook-based tool that records EEG, runs inference, and visualizes estimated cognitive load as a heatmap over the video timeline to help educators locate potentially challenging segments.

### [273] [Expander Sparse Autoencoders: Parameter-Efficient Dictionaries for Mechanistic Interpretability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01799)
*Rodrigo Mendoza-Smith*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出Expander SAEs，通过使用左-d-正则展开器掩码，将解码器和绑定编码器的支撑结构稀疏化，仅学习dn个解码器值（d≪m），显著降低存储开销。在Pythia、Qwen2.5、Llama等模型上实验表明，即使在极低参数量下（如d=7时解码器参数减少293倍），仍能保持84%的密集解码器性能。控制实验表明，性能提升主要源于稀疏且多样化的解码器结构，而非单纯参数减少；匹配参数量对比中，剩余差距部分来自编码器的摊销优势。理论分析证明，展开性与列平坦性足以保证无噪声k-稀疏码的可识别性，并推导出OMP精确恢复支持集的充分条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统稀疏自编码器（SAEs）虽能有效分解神经网络内部激活，但其全连接解码器需存储O(mn)个参数，在特征数量大时成本高昂。如何在不牺牲性能的前提下大幅降低存储开销，是当前稀疏表示研究中的关键挑战。本文旨在设计一种高效、可扩展的稀疏自编码器架构，实现存储与重建质量之间的最优权衡。

Method: 引入基于左-d-正则展开器掩码的Expander SAEs，使解码器与绑定编码器的权重仅在稀疏结构上非零，从而将参数量从O(mn)降至O(dn)，其中d≪m。利用展开器的代数性质，将原OMP算法中的矩阵-向量乘法$\mathbf{W}^\top \mathbf{r}$转化为O(dn)的gather-and-reduce操作，大幅提升计算效率。同时，结合理论分析，证明了展开性与列平坦性对稀疏码可识别性和精确恢复的保障作用。

Result: 在Pythia-70M/160M、Qwen2.5-3B、Llama-3.2-1B等主流语言模型的残差流激活上，不同d值呈现出一致的存储-保真度前沿曲线。以Qwen2.5-3B为例，当d=7时，解码器参数量仅为全连接版本的1/293，而仍能恢复84%的密集解码器交叉熵损失。控制实验验证：性能优势主要归因于稀疏且多样化的解码器结构，而非参数数量本身；在参数量匹配条件下，剩余差异部分源于编码器的优化摊销效应。

Conclusion: Expander SAEs通过引入展开器结构，在保持稀疏编码能力的同时，实现了显著的存储压缩，且在多种大型语言模型上均展现出优异的性能-存储平衡。该方法不仅具备工程实用性，也提供了坚实的理论基础，为大规模神经网络特征解析提供了新的高效范式。

Abstract: Sparse autoencoders (SAEs) decompose internal activations of neural networks into sparse linear combinations of learned features by fitting an overcomplete dictionary $\mathbf{W}\in\mathbb{R}^{m\times n}$ with $m<n$, and inferring a sparse code $\mathbf{x}\in\mathbb{R}^n$ from $\mathbf{h}\approx\mathbf{W}\mathbf{x}$. This inference problem closely resembles the canonical setup of compressed sensing, but dense decoders requires $O(mn)$ learned values, which becomes costly at large feature counts. We introduce Expander SAEs: TopK SAEs whose decoder and tied encoder are supported on a left-$d$-regular expander mask with $d\ll m$, learning only $dn$ decoder values while keeping the sparse-coding problem $(m,n,k)$ fixed. The same structure reduces storage and turns the matching-pursuit correlation step $\mathbf{W}^\top \mathbf{r}$ in OMP into an $O(dn)$ gather-and-reduce operation. Our experiments show that across Pythia-70M/160M, Qwen2.5-3B, and Llama-3.2-1B residual-stream activations, varying $d$ traces a consistent storage--fidelity frontier, and that at the most compressed modern-LM setting, Qwen2.5-3B with $d=7$ uses $293\times$ fewer learned decoder values than the full dense decoder while retaining $84$% of dense CE-loss recovered. Control experiments show that the improved storage--fidelity tradeoff is driven by sparse, diverse decoder support structure rather than by fewer learned decoder values, and that when sparse and dense decoders are compared at matched parameter count, part of the remaining gap comes from encoder amortisation. On the theoretical side, we show that expansion and column flatness are sufficient for identifiability of noiseless $k$-sparse codes, and we derive complementary sufficient conditions under which OMP recovers the support exactly.

</details>


### [274] [Do LLMs Truly Generalize in the Molecular Domain? A Perturbation-Based Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01800)
*Jiatong Li,Weida Wang,Changmeng Zheng,Shufei Zhang,Yatao Bian,Xiao-yong Wei,Qing Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了分子大语言模型（LLMs）在面对化学结构微小变化时的稳定性问题，提出通过控制图编辑距离（GED）生成语法有效的结构变体来评估其泛化能力。结果表明，即使一次微小修改也会导致性能显著下降，揭示了模型对结构变化的高度敏感性。研究进一步发现，在上下文中的调优（ICT）能部分扩展局部信任区域，提升模型鲁棒性，为稳定分子LLMs提供了新方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分子大语言模型虽在分子发现中展现潜力，但其基于序列的表示方式难以满足化学空间严格的拓扑约束，因此需要探究其是否能超越局部邻域进行泛化。

Method: 引入分子扰动框架，通过控制图编辑距离生成训练分子的语法有效结构变体，系统评估分子LLMs在结构变化下的表现。

Result: 单次结构修改即导致任务性能大幅下降，表明模型具有狭窄的局部信任区域和脆弱的敏感性；而引入在上下文中的调优（ICT）可部分缓解此问题，提升鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 分子大语言模型对结构变化极为敏感，需借助如ICT等方法增强其稳定性，以实现更可靠的分子性质预测与生成。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have recently shown promise in molecular discovery, yet a gap remains between their probabilistic nature over discrete sequential tokens and the rigid topological constraints of chemical space. This raises the question of whether molecular LLMs can generalize beyond the local neighborhoods induced by their sequence-based representations. To systematically investigate this question, we introduce a Molecular Perturbation framework that generates syntax-valid structural variants of training molecules under controlled Graph Edit Distance (GED) to probe the manifold regularity of molecular LLMs. Our analysis shows that even a single edit can cause substantial performance drops on common molecular tasks, revealing a narrow local trust region and fragile sensitivity to structural changes. Since similar molecules tend to exhibit similar properties, In-Context Tuning (ICT), which anchors predictions on structurally similar molecules, offers a natural way to mitigate such fragility. Our experiments also examine whether ICT confers robustness under controlled structural perturbations, and the results suggest that it can partially expand the local trust region and offer a promising direction for stabilizing molecular LLMs against structural variation.

### [275] [Gaming Consensus: Coordinated Manipulation in Crowdsourced Fact-Checking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01824)
*Nikil Roashan Selvam,Jay Baxter,Sophie Hilgard,Brad Miller,Keith Coleman,Ellen Vitercik,Sanmi Koyejo*

<details>

Method: 结合历史生产数据进行实证分析，并辅以理论建模，研究矩阵分解机制在面对协调攻击时的脆弱性；通过模拟攻击场景，量化操纵所需资源与成功率；设计并部署针对性防御机制以应对合成共识问题。

Conclusion: 当前主流的基于矩阵分解的事实核查系统存在被战略性操纵的风险，尤其是通过伪造跨群体支持。尽管系统已具备一定抗干扰能力，但必须引入主动防御机制。研究提出的缓解措施已在X平台成功部署，有效提升了系统的鲁棒性与可信度。

Abstract: Crowdsourced fact-checking systems have been adopted by major social media companies such as X, Meta, TikTok and Google with the aim of combating misleading information at scale without relying on centralized editorial control. These systems have been developed around a common underlying concept: a bridging mechanism that identifies notes flagging misleading information when they receive support from people with different perspectives rather than simple majority support. To our knowledge the only publicly disclosed bridging algorithms deployed for fact-checking are based on matrix factorization, as deployed by both X and Meta, augmented with additional components addressing abuse, targeted manipulation, and contributor brigades. This work examines the core matrix factorization portion of these systems, presenting theoretical and empirical evaluations of the degree to which coordinated users could vote strategically by leveraging the latent representations to fabricate the appearance of synthetic consensus within the bridging mechanism. Using historic production data, we find that up to 10.7% of lower quality notes could be manipulated above consensus thresholds using less than 10 ratings. We complement these findings with a theoretical analysis, revealing counterintuitively that rating a note as "Not Helpful" can increase its helpfulness score, as well as a cost model quantifying manipulation effort. We have developed and deployed mitigations within X's Community Notes algorithm to address synthetic consensus.

To address this limitation, we propose Multi-Role Rubric Generation (MRRG), a training-free and reference-free framework that elicits evaluation criteria from multiple complementary roles and consolidates them into an auditable rubric-based scorer. Experiments on preference validation benchmarks show that MRRG consistently outperforms single-role rubric generation baselines across multiple backbone models. ### [277] [Adaptive Group-Based Counterfactual Explanations for Time-Series Rehabilitation Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01838)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在康复运动分析中，临床医生依据肌群和关节段等语义特征组进行判断，但现有反事实方法多作用于单个通道，导致解释分散且生物力学上不连贯，亟需基于语义组的可解释性方法。

Method: 提出两阶段框架：第一阶段分析Shapley-Adaptive组排序在保持反事实有效性的同时缺乏组级稀疏性；第二阶段引入可学习门控（LG）机制，通过可训练的每组相关性门控与扰动掩码联合优化，实现组级选择与解释质量的兼顾。

Result: 在KneE-PAD数据集上的实验表明，LG方法显著提升模态组稀疏性，同时保持或优于基线在有效性、时间平滑性和生成效率方面的表现；运动特异性分析显示其生成的组结构反事实能提供简洁、符合临床逻辑的纠正建议。

Conclusion: 所提框架在不牺牲反事实质量的前提下，显著提升了康复运动分析中的可解释性，为临床提供了更可操作的解释工具。

Abstract: Counterfactual explanations (CEs) for multivariate time-series classifiers are often difficult to interpret in domains where experts reason in terms of semantic feature groups rather than individual channels. In rehabilitation movement analysis with multi-sensor inertial measurement units (IMUs), clinicians interpret motion through muscle-group and joint-segment abstractions; yet, most existing counterfactual methods operate at the channel level, producing scattered and biomechanically incoherent explanations. We propose a two-stage framework for group-based counterfactual generation in high-dimensional IMU data. We first show that Shapley-Adaptive (SA) group ranking preserves counterfactual validity but fails to enforce group-level sparsity, motivating the need for explicit group selection. We then introduce Learnable Gate (LG) methods, which incorporate trainable per-group relevance gates jointly optimized with perturbation masks. Experiments on the KneE-PAD rehabilitation dataset demonstrate that LG substantially improves modality-group sparsity compared to the channel-level M-CELS baseline while maintaining or improving validity, temporal smoothness, and generation efficiency. Exercise-specific analyses further show that group-structured counterfactuals yield concise, muscle-level corrective guidance aligned with clinical reasoning. Overall, the proposed framework enhances interpretability without sacrificing counterfactual quality, enabling more actionable explanations for rehabilitation movement analysis.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从音乐表演中恢复高阶音乐指令是一项具有挑战性的逆问题。现有的方法在处理低资源语言（如Strudel）时面临数据稀缺和代码可读性差的问题，因此需要一种能够生成高质量、可读性强且忠实还原原始MIDI的程序的方法。

Method: 提出Decomposer框架，分两阶段解决：1）构建合成数据集Strudel-Synth并用于监督微调；2）使用强化学习在无配对MIDI上优化奖励函数，兼顾MIDI重建准确性和代码可读性。

Result: 在合成与真实世界MIDI基准测试中，Decomposer在重建精度上显著优于闭源大模型，同时生成的代码更具可读性和多样性，优于启发式转换器。

Abstract: Musical performance involves executing a set of high-level musical instructions, yet recovering those instructions from the performance is a challenging inverse problem. We present Decomposer, a post-training framework for symbolic music decompilation: the task of recovering executable, editable music programs from symbolic music. We instantiate the task as MIDI-to-Strudel decompilation, where the model takes symbolic MIDI as input and produces a program in Strudel, a music programming language, that reconstructs the input when executed. The task poses two challenges: Strudel is a low-resource language with little naturally paired MIDI-code data, and optimizing faithful reconstruction of MIDI alone can collapse to unreadable note-by-note transliteration. We address these challenges in two stages. First, we construct Strudel-Synth, a synthetic corpus of paired Strudel programs and rendered MIDI, and use it for supervised fine-tuning. Second, we refine the model with reinforcement learning on unpaired MIDI, optimizing rewards for both MIDI reconstruction faithfulness and code readability. Our evaluation across synthetic and real-world MIDI benchmarks shows that Decomposer achieves substantially higher MIDI reconstruction faithfulness than closed-source LLMs while producing more readable and diverse code than the heuristic converter.

### [279] [Learning the Supports for Categorical Critic in Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01880)
*Jen-Yen Chang,Takayuki Osa,Tatsuya Harada*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种动态学习价值函数支持区间上下界的新型方法，用于改进基于直方图的损失（HL-Gauss）在强化学习中的应用。传统方法需预先设定固定支持区间，但该设定在非平稳和随机性强的强化学习任务中难以实现。本文通过联合优化支持区间的上下界与类别化值表示，提出一个新目标函数，并证明其为均方贝尔曼误差的上界，且比固定支持区间更紧。实验表明，该方法在多数连续控制任务中性能与现有方法相当，部分任务表现更优，且无需预设支持区间。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于直方图的损失方法（如HL-Gauss）需要预先设定支持区间，但在强化学习中目标值具有非平稳性和随机性，导致固定区间难以适应实际分布，影响模型性能。因此，亟需一种能动态调整支持区间的机制以提升鲁棒性与泛化能力。

Method: 提出一个联合优化支持区间上下界与类别化值表示的目标函数，通过可学习的边界参数动态适应目标值分布，同时保持对均方贝尔曼误差的上界性质。该方法结合了分布式贝尔曼更新与自适应支持结构，避免了人工设定支持范围的需求。

Result: 所提方法在多个连续控制任务中实现了与现有基于HL-Gauss的算法相当甚至更优的性能，同时具备良好的稳定性；最重要的是，无需预先指定支持区间，显著提升了方法的实用性与适应性。

Conclusion: 通过动态学习支持区间的上下界，本文提出的框架有效解决了传统直方图损失在强化学习中因固定支持区间带来的局限性，理论分析与实验证明其不仅保证了误差上界，还增强了模型的适应能力，是分布强化学习中一种高效、实用的新方法。

Abstract: Value functions are an essential component in actor-critic based deep reinforcement learning (RL). Conventionally, these functions are trained as a regression task by minimising the mean squared error (MSE) relative to bootstrapped target values. Meanwhile, in distributional RL, a distribution of returns is modelled based on the distributional Bellman operator. This work investigates the Gaussian Histogram Loss (HL-Gauss), a recent approach that reframes value estimation as classification by encoding each scalar Bellman target as a Gaussian-smoothed categorical target. Despite its potential, applying histogram-based losses to RL presents inherent challenges, most notably the requirement to pre-define a fixed support interval, which is often complicated by the non-stationary and stochastic nature of target values typically found in RL tasks. In this work, we propose an approach that dynamically learns the lower and upper bounds of the support instead of assigning them beforehand. We derive an objective that jointly learns these bounds whilst learning the categorical representation of the scalar values, and we show that this objective forms an upper bound on the mean-squared Bellman error. Our theoretical analysis further shows that this bound is tighter than that of non-learned supports of HL-Gauss. Empirically, the proposed objective enables stable adaptation of the support interval and matches HL-Gauss-based actor-critic algorithms on most continuous-control tasks whilst improving on a subset, without requiring a pre-specified support interval.

### [280] [Regularized Variational and Spectral Log-Density-Ratio Estimation in the Gaussian Location Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01895)
*Francis Bach*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究高斯位置模型中带有岭正则化的对数密度比估计，通过仿射不变性将模型简化为标准正态分布与均值向量为Δ的正态分布。提出变分估计器和最近提出的谱估计器，并在高维极限下推导出确定性渐近等价式。结果表明，在样本量较大时，变分估计器风险更小；样本量较小时，由于谱估计器基于协方差构造，方差更低，表现更优。此外，还探讨了核范数惩罚用于特征学习的可能性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究在高维设置下对数密度比估计的性能差异，尤其是在不同样本量与维度比例下的估计器选择问题。目标是理解变分与谱估计器在不同条件下的优势，并探索特征学习的新方法。

Method: 利用仿射不变性简化模型，采用变分法与谱方法分别构建估计器；结合凸高斯极小极大定理（CGMT）和加权和的随机矩阵理论推导高维确定性渐近等价式，进而比较两者在人口风险上的表现。

Result: 在大样本情况下，变分估计器具有更小的预测风险；而在小样本情况下，谱估计器因较低方差而表现更佳。核范数正则化可部分实现特征学习。

Conclusion: 根据样本数量和维度的比例，在高维渐近框架下，应根据观测数据规模选择合适的估计器：大样本时选变分估计器，小样本时选谱估计器；核范数正则化为特征学习提供了潜在路径。

Abstract: We study ridge-regularized log-density-ratio estimation in the Gaussian location model with a common covariance matrix. By affine invariance, the model is written as q $\sim$ N(0, I), p $\sim$ N($Δ$, I), with linear features, where $Δ$ is a mean vector. The variational estimator is the empirical Kullback-Leibler (KL) log-normalized fit with a squared L2-penalty on its nonconstant coefficient, and the spectral estimator recently introduced in [1] replaces a single variational problem by a continuum of ridge-regularized least-squares problems. We derive high-dimensional deterministic asymptotic equivalents when the numbers of observations and dimension tend to infinity with fixed ratios. The regularized variational limit is characterized by a scalar entropy minimization problem derived from the convex-Gaussian-min-max theorem (CGMT), while the regularized spectral limit follows from deterministic equivalents for resolvents of weighted sums of two independent Gaussian sample covariance matrices. We use these formulas to compare population risks, with experiments focused on fixed-signal aspect-ratio sweeps and optimized regularization. Our conclusion is that with many observations, under the criteria and asymptotic regimes analyzed here, the well-specified variational estimator has the smaller risk, while with fewer observations, the spectral estimator is favored because its covariance-based construction has lower variance. We also study how a nuclear penalty can be used and partially analyzed to perform feature learning.

### [281] [Rank-Then-Act: Reward-Free Control from Frame-Order Progress](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01897)
*Yuriy Maksyuta,George Bredis,Ruslan Rakhimov,Daniil Gavrilov*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: RTA是一种从专家视频演示中学习控制策略的框架，无需环境奖励。它通过在打乱的帧序列上使用组相对策略优化（GRPO）目标训练视觉-语言模型（VLM）作为基于进展的序数评分器，迫使模型从视觉语义中恢复时间顺序而非依赖时间线索。关键创新在于提出一种基于相关性的奖励函数：在每个交互窗口计算预测进展排名与真实时间索引之间的斯皮尔曼等级相关性，从而获得有界、尺度不变的学习信号。该设计解耦了奖励学习与绝对校准，实现了跨任务和环境的稳定迁移。RTA在离散控制（PyBoy: Catrap, Kirby）和连续控制（PointMaze, MetaWorld）任务中均表现优异，优于或匹配现有基于视频的奖励学习方法和基于排序的基线，并展示了单个预训练进展评分器在多任务间的强复用能力。结果表明，基于视频的序数信号的相关性结构监督足以支持策略学习，提供了一种可扩展的替代显式奖励设计的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于视频的奖励学习方法通常依赖于显式的标量奖励信号，而这些信号往往需要人工设计或难以准确建模。此外，许多方法对绝对奖励值敏感，导致跨任务迁移困难。本文旨在探索一种不依赖环境奖励、能够通过视频中的时序语义自动构建有效学习信号的方法，以实现更鲁棒、可迁移的策略学习。

Method: RTA框架包含两个核心组件：1）使用组相对策略优化（GRPO）在随机打乱的视频帧序列上训练一个视觉-语言模型（VLM），使其学会根据视觉语义判断帧的正确时间顺序；2）引入基于斯皮尔曼等级相关性的奖励函数，将模型输出的排名与真实时间索引进行相关性计算，生成稳定且尺度不变的奖励信号用于强化学习。

Result: RTA在多个离散和连续控制基准测试中表现出色，性能优于或等同于现有基于视频的奖励学习方法和基于排序的基线。更重要的是，单个预训练的进展评分器可在不同任务间有效复用，展现出良好的泛化能力。实验验证了基于相关性结构的监督机制在无奖励环境下的有效性与可扩展性。

Conclusion: 本研究证明，通过对视频中的序数信息施加相关性结构化的监督，可以有效地引导智能体学习控制策略，而无需依赖外部奖励信号。这种基于进展排名相关性的方法为减少对人工奖励设计的依赖提供了新思路，具有良好的可扩展性和跨任务迁移潜力。

Abstract: We introduce Rank-Then-Act (RTA), a framework for learning control policies from expert video demonstrations without environment rewards. RTA trains a Vision-Language Model (VLM) offline as a progress-based ordinal scorer, using a Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) objective over shuffled frame sequences, which forces the model to recover temporal ordering from visual semantics rather than trivial time cues. Importantly, instead of using the scorer directly as a scalar reward model, we propose a correlation-based reward function for reinforcement learning: at each interaction window, we compute the Spearman rank correlation between predicted progress rankings and true temporal indices, yielding a bounded, scale-invariant learning signal. This design decouples reward learning from absolute calibration and enables stable transfer across tasks and environments. We evaluate RTA on discrete control benchmarks (PyBoy: Catrap, Kirby) and continuous control tasks (PointMaze, MetaWorld). RTA consistently matches or outperforms prior video-based reward learning methods and rank-based baselines, while demonstrating strong cross-task reuse of a single pretrained progress scorer. Our results suggest that correlation-structured supervision over video-derived ordinal signals is sufficient for policy learning, offering a scalable alternative to explicit reward design.

Result: 在五个代表性任务上，Zeus 在无微调设置下均取得具有竞争力的结果，验证了其作为通用时间序列基础模型的有效性和广泛适用性。

Conclusion: Zeus 通过创新的架构设计实现了无需微调的多任务泛化能力，是迈向通用时间序列分析的重要一步。

Abstract: We present Zeus, a unified tuning-free Time Series Foundation Model (TSFM) that delivers superior performance across diverse analysis tasks without any task-specific fine-tuning. Unlike prior studies that primarily focus on zero-shot forecasting but require task-specific tuning for other tasks, Zeus bridges this gap by addressing two fundamental challenges in multi-task generalization. First, to reconcile point-level granularity with long-sequence scalability, Zeus incorporates a multi-scale Transformer featuring point-wise tokenization and a U-shaped hierarchy, effectively balancing fine-grained fidelity with computational efficiency. Second, to accommodate varying inductive biases across different tasks, Zeus introduces Multi-Objective Temporal Masking (MOTM), a unified strategy that supports heterogeneous tasks (e.g., extrapolation, interpolation, and global abstraction) within a single framework. Extensive experiments across five representative tasks demonstrate that Zeus consistently achieves competitive results in tuning-free settings, underscoring its potential as a general-purpose TSFM.

### [286] [A More Accurate Algorithm Comparison through A/B Testing using Offline Evaluation Methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01958)
*Koki Konishi,Masataka Ushiku,Yuta Saito*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了A/B测试中一个反直觉现象：其算法选择错误率可能高于离线评估。原因在于A/B测试使用的样本均值估计器不产生正相关性，而正相关性对减少关键选择错误（低估真正优算法、高估劣算法）至关重要。相比之下，离线评估通过共享数据无意中引入了这种有益的相关性。为此，作者提出一种新估计器，通过引入一个虚拟中间算法，并分步使用共享数据估计算法间的性能差异，从而在每一步中应用离线评估技术，诱导正相关性，降低关键错误。此外，文章推导出最优中间算法以最小化方差，并通过偏差-方差分析证明其优势。实验表明，该方法在仅使用一半A/B测试数据的情况下，达到与现有方法相当的选择错误率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为A/B测试是算法选择的金标准，而离线评估因精度较低通常仅作为辅助。然而，本文发现A/B测试的实际选择错误率可能高于离线评估，其根源在于缺乏正相关性，导致关键选择错误增加。因此，需要改进A/B测试中的估计方法，以提升选择准确性。

Method: 提出一种新型估计器，通过引入一个假设的中间算法，将算法性能差异的估计过程分解为多个步骤，每个步骤利用共享数据进行估计，从而在每一步中引入正相关性。该方法借鉴了离线评估的优势，使A/B测试也能受益于相关性带来的误差降低效果。进一步推导出最优中间算法，以最小化估计方差。

Result: 实验基于真实世界数据验证了所提方法的有效性。结果表明，在仅使用一半原定A/B测试数据的前提下，该方法实现了与现有方法相当甚至更低的算法选择错误率，显著提升了数据利用效率。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了A/B测试中正相关性对降低关键选择错误的重要性，并提出了一种通过引入中间算法实现正相关的新型估计器。该方法不仅理论上具有优势，且在实际应用中显著减少了所需实验数据量，为在线服务中的算法选择提供了更高效、更可靠的解决方案。

Abstract: A/B testing is the gold standard for selecting the better algorithm in online services. While offline evaluation has attracted attention as a safer alternative due to the high experimental costs and the potential risk of degrading user experience and revenue in A/B testing, it is widely recognized that the estimation accuracy of offline evaluation is substantially lower. As a result, final selection decisions are typically made through A/B testing. Contrary to this conventional view, we reveal a counterintuitive phenomenon in which A/B testing can produce a higher algorithm selection error rate than offline evaluation. This occurs because the sample mean estimator used in A/B testing does not induce positive correlation, which is crucial for reducing critical selection errors, namely underestimating the truly superior algorithm and overestimating the truly inferior one. In contrast, offline evaluation methods unintentionally generate this beneficial correlation by relying on shared offline data when estimating and comparing the performance of multiple algorithms. Building on this insight, we propose an estimator that intentionally induces positive correlation to improve algorithm selection in A/B testing. The key idea is to introduce a hypothetical middle algorithm and to estimate the performance difference between algorithms A, M, and B in a stepwise manner using shared data at each step. This approach enables the application of offline evaluation techniques in each step, thereby inducing positive correlation and reducing critical selection errors. Furthermore, we derive the optimal middle algorithm regarding the resulting variance and analyze its advantages over existing methods through bias-variance analysis. Experiments on real-world data demonstrate that our estimator achieves the same selection error rate as existing approaches while using only one half of the A/B testing data.

</details>

*Jijie Zhang,Zhe Ren,Quan Zhang,Dandan Guo*

TL;DR: 提出DALorRA，一种基于变分贝叶斯稀疏的框架，将不确定性量化从密集参数空间转移到低秩适配（LoRA）的轻量级秩层面，通过在秩维度上施加随机掩码实现训练时的贝叶斯正则化和推理时的集成式校准，显著提升大语言模型的校准性而不损失推理准确性。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) exhibit remarkable reasoning capabilities, but their task-specific fine-tuning is notoriously plagued by overconfidence, severely hindering trustworthy deployment. We propose Data-Adaptive Lower-Rank Adaptation (DALorRA), a simple and effective variational Bayesian sparse framework that shifts the paradigm of uncertainty quantification from the dense parameter space to the lightweight rank level of low-rank adaptation (LoRA). With the insight that LoRA essentially aggregates multiple rank-one components that may provide superfluous model capacity, DALorRA imposes stochastic masking on rank dimensions, enabling Bayesian regularization of model capacity during training and ensemble-like calibration during inference. Extensive experiments demonstrate DALorRA's excellent calibration of LLMs without compromising reasoning accuracy.

### [288] [Liquid Latent State Dynamics for Interpretable Turbofan Degradation Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01986)

Main category: cs.LG

Method: 采用液态神经网络构建潜空间动态模型，将历史窗口编码为潜状态，通过液态转移模型演化该状态，并解码未来传感器观测值；潜状态被分解为退化与运行条件两个分量，分别由剩余使用寿命、单调风险、潜一致性损失监督退化成分，由条件预测与去相关损失抑制运行条件信息泄露。

Conclusion: 液态潜动态模型能够有效分离退化与运行条件，构建更清晰、可解释的退化轨迹，有助于实现高精度预测与健康状态可解释性之间的平衡，为预测性维护提供可信的物理意义建模工具。

Abstract: Multivariate time-series models for prognostics are often evaluated by point prediction accuracy, yet their internal states rarely expose a coherent degradation process. We study liquid neural networks as latent dynamics models for aircraft engine health monitoring on the C-MAPSS benchmark. The proposed model encodes a history window into a latent state, evolves that state with a liquid transition model, and decodes future sensor observations. To separate health evolution from operating-condition variation, the latent state is factorized into degradation and condition components. Remaining useful life, monotonic risk, and latent-consistency losses supervise the degradation component, while condition prediction and decorrelation losses discourage operating-condition leakage. Across FD001--FD004, the full disentangled model improves overall sensor forecasting RMSE from 0.2438 for a GRU baseline to 0.2266, with the largest gains on the multi-condition subsets FD002 and FD004. The learned degradation state also forms a clearer temporal degradation axis, reaching an average state-speed Spearman correlation of 0.5960. Direct remaining-useful-life regression remains stronger for the GRU baseline, indicating that the proposed representation is currently more effective as an interpretable world model for degradation dynamics than as a calibrated lifetime regressor. These results suggest that liquid latent dynamics can bridge predictive maintenance forecasting and inspectable health-state modeling.

### [289] [A Memory Efficient Unified Algorithm for Online Learning of Linear Dynamical Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02050)
*Yuval Ran-Milo,Angelos Assos,Elad Hazan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究在观测数据下稳定未知线性动态系统（LDS）的在线预测问题，目标是实现次线性损失且内存占用适应系统内在复杂度而非全隐藏状态维度。重点关注不稳定复杂度低的系统——即非快速衰减的不稳定特征值与非可对角化模式共存的情况，记为 $k$。这类系统是稳定化的合理前提，因为高不稳定复杂度系统需指数级控制才能稳定。作者提出统一在线算法，适用于所有LDS（包括复数或爆炸性模式的非对角化系统），参数量为 $\widetilde{O}(k)$；并证明下界表明任何基于滤波器的预测器至少需要 $k$ 个滤波器。实验验证理论：在高维系统中，本方法在相同参数预算下显著优于已有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法难以在低内存开销下实现对未知线性动态系统的有效在线预测，尤其在系统具有非可对角化结构或复杂不稳定特征值时。稳定化要求系统具备低不稳定复杂度，但此前缺乏对这一复杂度的精确刻画和高效算法设计。因此，亟需一种能自适应系统内在复杂度、同时保证预测性能的在线学习框架。

Method: 提出一种统一的在线学习算法，通过引入可学习参数数量为 $\\widetilde{O}(k)$ 的滤波器结构，处理包括非对角化、复数特征值及爆炸性模式在内的各类线性动态系统。利用最小二乘估计与在线优化相结合的方式，实现子线性遗憾，并通过理论分析建立下界以证明 $k$ 作为复杂度度量的有效性。

Result: 所提算法在理论上实现了次线性后悔率，且参数规模仅依赖于不稳定复杂度 $k$，而非系统全维数；同时证明了 $k$ 是任何滤波器型预测器的必要下限。实验显示，在高维系统上该方法在相同参数量下显著优于现有基准方法。

Conclusion: 对于不稳定复杂度低的线性动态系统，可以实现高效、低内存的在线预测；$k$ 是刻画此类系统复杂性的关键指标；所提算法兼具理论严谨性与实际优越性，为系统识别与稳定化提供了新范式。

Abstract: Motivated by the challenge of stabilizing a general unknown linear dynamical system (LDS) from observations, we study the natural prerequisite of online prediction. Our goal is to achieve sublinear regret with a memory footprint that adapts to the intrinsic complexity of the dynamics rather than the full hidden -- state dimension. We focus on the practically central regime of systems with low instability complexity -- eigenvalues outside the real stable interval that do not decay rapidly, together with non-semisimple modes-potentially embedded in an otherwise stable real spectrum of much higher dimension; we write $k$ for this count. This regime is the primary setting in which stabilization is plausible: we show that many systems with high instability complexity cannot be stabilized without exponentially large controls. Thus, prediction is meaningful for stabilization precisely when the instability complexity is small. Within this regime, we introduce a unified online algorithm that handles every LDS (including non-diagonalizable systems with complex or exploding modes) with a learnable parameter count of $\widetilde{O}(k)$. Finally, we prove a lower bound showing that $k$ is a valid complexity measure: any filter-based predictor needs at least $k$ filters. Experiments corroborate our theory: on a high-dimensional system, our predictor sharply outperforms prior methods at an equal parameter budget.

### [290] [Beyond the Performance Illusion: Structure-Aware Stratified Partitioning and Curriculum Distributionally Robust Optimization for Spatially Correlated Domains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02055)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在时空相关数据中，传统的随机数据划分假设独立同分布（i.i.d.）往往不成立，导致数据泄露和隐藏分层问题，使性能评估失真，无法真实反映模型泛化能力。

Method: 提出Structure-Aware Stratified Partitioning (SASP) 用于构建减少时空泄漏的验证集，同时保持类别的合理分布；引入Curriculum Distributionally Robust Optimization (CDRO)，通过课程学习策略缓解分布鲁棒训练在严格划分下的优化不稳定性。

Abstract: Performance evaluation in AI systems commonly assumes that random dataset splits produce independent and identically distributed (i.i.d.) subsets. We show that this assumption often breaks down in spatiotemporally correlated domains such as aerial surveillance, precision agriculture, and medical imaging, leading to two systematic failures: data leakage, where correlated samples span training and validation splits and inflate performance estimates, and hidden stratification, where errors on minority subpopulations are obscured by aggregate metrics. To address these issues, we propose a unified evaluation and training framework for spatially correlated data. We introduce Structure-Aware Stratified Partitioning (SASP), which constructs validation splits that reduce spatiotemporal leakage while preserving meaningful class balance, and Curriculum Distributionally Robust Optimization (CDRO), a curriculum-based relaxation of distributionally robust training that stabilizes optimization under these stricter splits. Across multiple benchmarks, this combination yields consistently improved generalization, more reliable confidence calibration, and exposes failure modes that remain hidden under conventional random-split evaluation.

Abstract: Graph Neural Networks (GNNs) have been widely used to capture spatial functional connectivity patterns to improve electroencephalography (EEG)-based depression recognition performance. However, the functional connectivity of brain networks in patients with depression exhibits an inherent hierarchical structure, making it difficult to capture accurate connection patterns. To address these issues, this paper proposes a novel model named Sample-Adaptive Hyperbolic Graph Neural Network (SA-HGNN), which aims to accurately extract the authentic hierarchical structure of depression-affected brain networks. Specifically, the proposed model comprises three core modules. First, a Sample-Adaptive Graph Construction module dynamically constructs personalized brain network topologies to capture more complex spatial relationships within the brain network. Second, hyperbolic graph convolution is employed to overcome the representation bottlenecks of Euclidean space, leveraging hyperbolic geometry to precisely capture latent hierarchical relationships within the brain network. Finally, an Attention Pooling module adaptively filters out highly redundant noise channels in EEG signals, effectively mitigating the interference of inherent noise on the authentic hierarchical topology. Extensive experiments on public EEG datasets demonstrate the superior performance of our method across resting-state and task-related paradigms, validating its robustness to noise and efficacy in capturing abnormal functional connectivity patterns in brain networks of patients with depression.

</details>
